# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [A Non-Commutative Voronovskaya Theorem for Quantum Neural Network Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11907)
*Rômulo Damasclin Chaves dos Santos,Delvonei Alves de Andrade*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明量子神经网络算子（quantum neural network operators）在逼近任意量子信道（quantum channels）时的完整渐近展开（asymptotic expansion），即经典 Voronovskaya 定理的非交换类比。展开揭示逼近误差分为三个本质不同部分：整数幂 Fréchet 导数项、分数幂 Marchaud 分数导数项（刻画 Hölder 光滑性）、以及无经典对应的纯量子对易子项（commutator terms）。余项由显式常数给出紧界。基于该展开，本文获得三项主要进展：量子神经网络算子涨落的量子中心极限定理、通过 Kubo-Ando 均值构造量子信道间最优插值测地线的方法、以及分数光滑性如何限制量子神经网络逼近加速的系统理解。数值实验验证了理论收敛速率和对数修正的不可回避性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典 Voronovskaya 定理在逼近论中具有基础地位，但其在量子信道逼近场景下的非交换类比尚未建立，阻碍了量子神经网络（quantum neural networks）的理论理解。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立量子版本渐近展开以阐明误差结构，并由此推动量子中心极限定理、最优测地线构造及光滑性对逼近加速影响等核心问题的进展。

Method: 本文延拓了经典 Voronovskaya 定理的方法论，将其推广到非交换（non-commutative）框架下。通过解析展开量子神经网络算子的逼近误差，将误差分解为 Fréchet 导数（整数幂）、Marchaud 分数导数（分数幂）和量子对易子项三个部分，并推导出具有显式常数和 (log n)^{3m/2} 对数修正的紧余项界。数值实验采用经典类比验证理论预测。

Result: 主要结果包括：完整的量子 Voronovskaya 渐近展开公式，余项界为 ∥R_{m,n}(Φ,·)∥_⋄ ≤ C_{m,γ,d} ∥Φ∥_{C^{m,γ}} n^{-(m+γ)} (log n)^{3m/2}；由此导出量子中心极限定理、基于 Kubo-Ando 均值的最优插值测地线构造方法、以及分数光滑性对量子神经网络加速的限制机制。数值实验证实了收敛速率和对数修正是不可回避的。

Conclusion: 本文在经典逼近理论、分数阶微积分（fractional calculus）与量子机器学习（quantum machine learning）之间建立了严格桥梁，为有限维量子神经网络的设计与分析提供了理论洞见和实用工具。数值验证表明理论速率是紧的，对数修正不可消除。

Abstract: We prove a complete asymptotic expansion for quantum neural network operators when they approximate arbitrary quantum channels. This is the non-commutative analogue of the classical Voronovskaya theorem. The expansion reveals that the approximation error splits into three fundamentally different parts: integer powers of \(1/n\) involving ordinary Fréchet derivatives; fractional powers governed by Marchaud fractional derivatives, which capture the Hölder smoothness of the channel; and purely quantum commutator terms that have no classical counterpart. The remainder is bounded sharply by an explicit constant:
  \[
  \norm{R_{m,n}(Φ,\bullet)}_\diamond \le C_{m,γ,d} \|Φ\|_{\cC^{m,γ}} \, n^{-(m+γ)} (\log n)^{3m/2}.
  \]
  We present a numerical test for a classical analogue that confirms the predicted convergence rate and the logarithmic correction, directly validating the asymptotic theory. Based on this expansion, we obtain three major advances: a quantum central limit theorem for the fluctuations of quantum neural network operators, a method to construct optimal interpolation geodesics between quantum channels via Kubo-Ando means, and a systematic understanding of how fractional smoothness limits the acceleration of quantum neural network approximations. The numerical test further demonstrates that the theoretical rates are sharp and that logarithmic enhancements are unavoidable. Altogether, our work builds a rigorous bridge between classical approximation theory, fractional calculus, and quantum machine learning, offering both theoretical insight and practical tools for designing and analyzing quantum neural networks in finite dimensions.

</details>


### [2] [A Quantum Computing Approach to Track Reconstruction in Strip-Type Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12821)
*Seungyeob Jwa,Hyunyong Kim,Jangho Kim,Minseok Oh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究探索利用量子退火（quantum annealing）解决条状气体探测器中的粒子径迹重建问题，将两个重建子问题建模为二次无约束二元优化（QUBO）问题，并在DAMSA探测器模拟数据上验证其可行性。结果表明，在处理低堆积（low pileup）双光子信号事件时，量子处理单元（QPU）的径迹重建精度接近基于卡尔曼滤波（Kalman filter）的方法，为量子-经典混合重建方法在更复杂场景下的应用提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 条状气体探测器中存在虚假击中（ghost hits）和多重击中组合问题，使得模式识别转化为组合优化问题（combinatorial optimization problem），传统的重建方法在处理此类问题时面临计算复杂度挑战。本研究旨在利用量子退火技术来高效解决这一组合优化问题。

Method: 将粒子径迹重建中的两个子问题——单光子径迹的击中点选择和跨探测器层的簇三重态（cluster triplet）筛选——分别建模为二次无约束二元优化（quadratic unconstrained binary optimization, QUBO）问题。第二个子问题允许在单个量子处理单元（QPU）提交中处理多个径迹候选。采用模拟的DAMSA探测器事件进行测试，对三重态关联任务进一步利用基于图连通性（graph connectivity）的关联规则连接有效簇三重态以构建径迹候选。

Result: 在单径迹击中点选择任务中，基于QPU的重建在位置分辨率和角度分辨率上均接近基于卡尔曼滤波（Kalman filter）的重建结果。在同时关联任务中，QPU样本成功提取出有效的簇三重态。在DAMSA事件拓扑（低堆积、轴子致双光子信号主导）下，QUBO公式能够复现局部重建决策。

Conclusion: 本研究表明量子退火可用于条状气体探测器中粒子径迹重建的组合优化子问题，且结果与经典方法相当。这为在更复杂的径迹追踪环境中进一步研究量子与经典计算相结合的混合重建方法提供了实践基础。

Abstract: This study investigates the use of quantum annealing for particle track reconstruction in strip-type gaseous detectors. In such detectors, ghost hits and multiple hit combinations can turn pattern recognition into a combinatorial optimization problem. We formulate two reconstruction subproblems as quadratic unconstrained binary optimization problems. The first subproblem selects detector hits associated with a single photon track inside a localized candidate region. The second subproblem selects cluster triplets from different detector layers so that multiple track candidates can be handled within a single quantum processing unit(QPU) submission. The proposed formulations are tested using simulated DAMSA detector events. For the single track hit selection task, the QPU based reconstruction gives position and angular resolutions close to those obtained with a Kalman based reconstruction. In the simultaneous association task, valid cluster triplets are first extracted from the QPU samples and then connected using an association rule based on graph connectivity to construct track candidates. The DAMSA event topology studied here has low pileup and is dominated by the two photon signal from axion-like particle(ALP) decay. In this setting, the results show that the QUBO formulations can reproduce local reconstruction decisions. This provides a practical basis for further studies of reconstruction methods that combine quantum and classical computing in more complex tracking environments.

</details>


### [3] [Categorical Tensor-Graph Semantics for Quantum Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12128)
*Naihong Hu,Ruining Li,Futao Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从范畴张量图语义（categorical tensor-graph semantics）的视角，在有限维希尔伯特空间范畴（FHilb）中系统研究了量子计算协议。通过将传统希尔伯特空间形式主义替换为拓扑框架，直接将算法功能编码为图形骨架，重新诠释了伯恩斯坦-瓦齐拉尼（Bernstein-Vazirani）和西蒙（Simon）算法，形式化了三能级量子比特（qutrit）版本的德意志-约萨（Deutsch-Jozsa）算法和单次Grover算法，并通过互补弗罗贝尼乌斯结构（complementary Frobenius structures）实现CNOT门，追溯了贝尔态（Bell state）、GHZ态和W态的图论起源，最终为自动化量子电路优化提供了可组合、可扩展的图论工具包。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统希尔伯特空间形式主义依赖高维矩阵运算，掩盖了量子算法功能背后的结构本质。有必要发展一种更直观、结构性的描述框架，以揭示算法核心机制并支持自动化电路优化。

Method: 在有限维希尔伯特空间范畴（FHilb）中建立张量图语义（tensor-graph semantics）拓扑框架，将算法功能直接映射到图形骨架上。利用拓扑变换提炼算法核心数学本质；通过互补弗罗贝尼乌斯结构（complementary Frobenius structures）实现CNOT门；对量子纠缠态（Bell态、GHZ态、W态）进行图论简化表示。

Result: 成功以拓扑方式重新诠释了Bernstein-Vazirani算法和Simon算法；形式化了qutrit适配的广义Deutsch-Jozsa算法和广义单次Grover算法，并给出其图形表示；展示了CNOT门的图论实现方案；给出了Bell态、GHZ态和W态制备协议的图论简化形式。

Conclusion: 本文通过将张量范畴理论（tensor category theory）与实际量子算法设计相结合，提供了一套可组合、可扩展的图论工具包，对跨量子硬件生态系统（evolving quantum hardware ecosystem）的自动化电路优化具有关键支撑作用。

Abstract: This paper systematically investigates quantum computing protocols from the intuitive perspective of categorical tensor-graph semantics within the category FHilb. While conventional Hilbert-space formalisms conceal the structural nature of quantum algorithms behind high-dimensional matrix operations, the topological framework developed herein directly encodes algorithmic functionalities to their graphical skeletons. We provide a comprehensive topological reinterpretation of the Bernstein-Vazirani and the Simon algorithms, demonstrating how topological transformations distill their core mathematical essence and clarify the operational mechanism of oracles. Going beyond standard qubit models, we formalize the qutrit-adapted generalized Deutsch-Jozsa algorithm as well as the generalized single-shot Grover algorithm, explicitly laying out their graphical representations. We further implement CNOT gates via complementary Frobenius structures, trace the diagrammatic genesis of quantum entanglement including Bell and GHZ states, and present a diagrammatic simplification for W-state preparation protocol. By bridging tensor category theory with practical quantum algorithmic design, this work furnishes composable, scalable diagrammatic toolkit essential for automated circuit optimization across the evolving quantum hardware ecosystem.

</details>


### [4] [Sparse anisotropic positive maps for qutrit entanglement: exact indecomposability and PPT geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12470)
*Massimiliano F. Sacchi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍并分析了一个精确可解的双参数稀疏双随机正映射族（sparse bistochastic positive maps），用于三能级系统（qutrits）中纠缠的检测。该映射通过两个参数独立调控相干通道，完整刻画了正性（positivity）、完全正性（complete positivity）和不可分解性（indecomposability）的相图，并构造了对应的PPT纠缠态（PPT entangled states）及暴露面（exposed faces），最终给出了一个最优精化（optimal refinement）方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 正但不完全正的映射（positive but not completely positive maps）提供了一种超越部分转置正性判据（positive-partial-transpose criterion, PPT criterion）的直接纠缠检测方法。然而，以往缺乏一个解析可解且能同时研究正性、不可分解性、PPT纠缠、最优性与凸几何性质的统一框架。本文旨在构建这样一个框架。

Method: 引入一个双参数$w$和$z$的稀疏双随机正映射族，其中两个相干通道被独立调节。稀疏结构使得完整的相图可解析求解：正性在方形区域$0\le w,z\le2/3$上成立，完全正性在更小的方形$0\le w,z\le1/3$上成立，不可分解性在$w,z\ge1/3$的角域内一个四分之一圆之外丧失。在端点$W_*=W(2/3,2/3)$构建了一个秩类型(5,5)的四参数PPT边缘态族（edge states），推导了其解析检测区域。

Result: 不可分解区域由显式构造的PPT纠缠态认证，该态适配于相同的见证几何结构（witness geometry）。$W_*$对应的射线被证明是PPT锥（PPT cone）的暴露面。虽然$W_*$本身不是最优的，但给出了一个显式的最优精化，其检测区域严格更大。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个解析可解的三能级系统框架，使得正性、不可分解性、PPT纠缠、最优性与暴露凸几何可以在单一体系内同时研究。

Abstract: Positive but not completely positive maps provide one of the most direct ways to detect entanglement beyond the positive-partial-transpose (PPT) criterion. We introduce and analyze an exactly solvable two-parameter family of sparse bistochastic positive maps on qutrits, in which two coherence channels are independently tuned by parameters $w$ and $z$. The sparse structure makes the full phase diagram analytic: positivity holds exactly on the square $0\le w,z\le2/3$, complete positivity on the smaller square $0\le w,z\le1/3$, and decomposability is lost precisely outside a quarter circle in the corner $w,z\ge1/3$. The indecomposable region is certified by explicit PPT entangled state adapted to the same witness geometry. At the endpoint $W_*=W(2/3,2/3)$ we construct a four-parameter family of PPT edge states of rank type $(5,5)$, derive their analytic detection region, and show that the corresponding rays are exposed faces of the PPT cone. Finally, although $W_*$ is not optimal, we give an explicit optimal refinement whose detection region on this family is strictly larger. The result is an analytically tractable qutrit setting in which positivity, indecomposability, PPT entanglement, optimality, and exposed convex geometry can be studied in a single framework.

</details>


### [5] [The Infinitesimal Structure of Quantum Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12559)
*Luca Barbieri-Viale*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过将量子态空间光滑、正则嵌入到高阶对偶数代数（dual number algebras）$\mathcal{Q}_N \equiv \mathbb{R}[\varepsilon]/(\varepsilon^{N^2-1})$中，建立了一个严格统一的几何框架，使得每个量子态被忠实地表示为非约化概型点（non-reduced scheme-theoretic point），并证明非线性矩阵对易子在此框架下映射为平坦、线性的代数流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为量子态空间建立一个严格而统一的几何框架，解决传统表述中非线性动力学带来的复杂性，从而为高维量子运动学提供更简洁的几何图景。

Method: 构造从量子态空间到高阶对偶数代数 $\mathcal{Q}_N \equiv \mathbb{R}[\varepsilon]/(\varepsilon^{N^2-1})$ 的光滑、正则嵌入（smooth, regular embedding），利用截断环族（truncated rings）将每个量子态表示为非约化概型点。

Result: 在该截断环族框架下，控制 Liouville-von Neumann 动力学的非线性矩阵对易子（matrix commutators）被整体映射为平坦、线性且刚性的代数流（flat, linear, and rigid algebraic flows）。

Conclusion: 幂零对偶数代数（nilpotent dual algebras）为高维量子运动学（quantum kinematics）提供了一个简洁的几何景观（pristine geometric landscape）。

Abstract: This paper establishes a rigorous, unified geometric framework for quantum state spaces by constructing smooth, regular embeddings into higher-order dual number algebras $\mathcal{Q}_N \equiv \mathbb{R}[\varepsilon]/(\varepsilon^{N^2-1})$, wherein every quantum state is faithfully represented as a non-reduced scheme-theoretic point. We show that under this unified family of truncated rings, the non-linear matrix commutators governing the Liouville-von Neumann dynamics map globally onto flat, linear, and rigid algebraic flows, establishing nilpotent dual algebras as a pristine geometric landscape for higher-dimensional quantum kinematics.

</details>


### [6] [Entropy Transport in Programmable Quantum Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12581)
*Radhika Joshi,Yuli V. Nazarov,Mohammad H. Ansari*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了驱动量子比特结（driven qubit junctions）如何实现物理熵输运（entropy transport）的可编程控制，发现两量子比特结在更低驱动功率下具有更强的熵转移能力，并揭示了共振驱动下的相干熵流贡献和负微分熵导（negative differential entropy conductance）两种非直观效应，为量子反馈控制与制冷等应用提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索驱动量子比特结能否实现对物理熵输运的可编程控制，并比较不同量子架构（单量子比特结与两量子比特结）在熵传导（entropy conductance）方面的性能差异。

Method: 通过比较两种简单的量子架构——驱动单量子比特结（driven single-qubit junction）与驱动两量子比特结（driven two-qubit junction）——分析其熵传输特性，并考察熵流（entropy current）的相干贡献与负微分熵导效应。

Result: 两量子比特结在熵转移能力上优于单量子比特结，且所需驱动功率显著更低；两种结均在共振驱动条件下表现出显著的相干熵流贡献，以及增加热偏置（thermal bias）会抑制熵流进入探测库（probe reservoir）的负微分熵导现象。

Conclusion: 量子逻辑架构（quantum logic architectures）可作为熵输运的可编程器件，并为量子反馈控制（quantum feedback control）、库保护（reservoir protection）及驱动量子电路中的制冷（refrigeration）等方向提供了可能的实现路径。

Abstract: We show that driven qubit junctions enable programmable control of physical entropy transport, with entropy conductance governed by quantum dynamics rather than by reservoir parameters alone. By comparing two simple quantum architectures -- a driven single-qubit junction and a driven two-qubit junction -- we find that the two-qubit junction enhances entropy transfer while requiring substantially lower driving power than its single-qubit counterpart. We further reveal two non-intuitive effects in both junctions: a sizable coherent contribution to the entropy current that emerges only under resonant driving, and negative differential entropy conductance, where increasing the thermal bias suppresses entropy flow into the probe reservoir. These results identify quantum logic architectures as programmable devices for entropy transport and suggest routes toward quantum feedback control, reservoir protection and refrigeration in driven quantum circuits.

</details>


### [7] [Ancilla-Depth Phase Diagrams for Quantum Reference-Frame Comparison](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12947)
*Maxim V. Churilov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了有噪量子参考系（quantum reference frames）在统计实验比较中的层级结构，证明了当辅助记忆（ancillary memory）维度r受限时，量子信道的模拟等价于因子Γ=BA⁻¹的r-正性（r-positivity），并推导了退极化信道（depolarizing channels）下的相边界、缺陷度量及物理转换成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在有噪量子参考系比较中，辅助存储维度如何影响统计实验的可模拟性，以及这种模拟与单一量子信道实现之间的本质区别。

Method: 基于有限维量子信道A和B（A可逆），建立精确模拟所有辅助r维辅助存储器（ancilla）的测量等价于因子Γ=BA⁻¹的r-正性。利用幺正且迹保持（unital, trace-preserving）的k-正性映射嵌入信道对，并通过退极化信道的具体构造推导相边界与闭式缺陷公式。

Result: 退极化源和目标信道D_a和D_b的相边界为：D_a ≻_r D_b ⇔ -1/(dr-1) ≤ b/a ≤ 1 (a≠0)；给出了受限层级r缺陷的闭式公式及到每个物理后处理的距离；量化了外部检测首次感知层级从k+1降到⌊k/m⌋+1的m级旁观者效应。

Conclusion: 该工作定量刻画了辅助存储受限下统计模拟与单信道实现之间的区分，并通过转置-退极化构造（transpose-depolarizing construction）证明该层级分离现象不局限于退极化因子。

Abstract: Comparing two noisy quantum reference frames as statistical experiments depends on the dimension of the ancillary memory available to the decision procedure. For finite-dimensional channels A and B with invertible A, we show that exact simulation of all measurements assisted by an r-dimensional ancilla is equivalent to r-positivity of the unique factor Gamma = BA^{-1}. The hierarchy can be realized by physical channel pairs: every unital, trace-preserving map that is k-positive but not (k+1)-positive embeds as the factor between the channels D_a and Gamma composed with D_a on an exact interval determined by the smallest Choi eigenvalue. For depolarizing source and target channels D_a and D_b, including negative and singular source parameters, the phase boundary is $\mathcal{D}_a \succeq_r \mathcal{D}_b \Longleftrightarrow -1/(dr-1) \leq b/a \leq 1$ for $a\neq 0$. We derive closed formulas for the restricted level-r deficiency and for the distance to every physical post-processing, $δ_{\mathrm{phys}}(\mathcal{D}_b\mid\mathcal{D}_a)=(1-1/d^2)\operatorname{dist}(b,I_a)$, where $I_a=\operatorname{conv}\{a,-a/(d^2-1)\}$. The largest physical conversion cost hidden from all tests through level k is $(d-k)/[d(d^2-1)]$. An untouched m-level spectator changes the first detecting external level from k+1 to $\lfloor k/m\rfloor+1$. A transpose--depolarizing construction shows that the separation is not confined to depolarizing factors. The results quantify the distinction between ancilla-restricted statistical simulation and implementation by a single quantum channel.

</details>


### [8] [Maximal Classicalization of Finite-Group Quantum Reference-Frame Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12968)
*Maxim V. Churilov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于有限群G的酉表示U，表示完备性（representation completeness，即U包含所有不可约类型）等价于量子后处理（quantum post-processing）可普遍约化为经典卷积（classical convolution）的条件，并给出了最小辅助维度、条件期望距离、量子-经典差距的表征，以及无限紧致群上的稳定可视带重建（visible-band reconstruction）结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限量子参考令牌（finite quantum reference token）的群值失配（group-valued misalignment）场景中，信道退化的最优方案通常需要对所有量子后处理进行全局优化，这一问题的复杂性使得寻找更简单的约化条件成为必要。本文旨在揭示表示完备性是否以及如何充当这一约化的精确载体条件（carrier condition）。

Method: 基于群表示论（group representation theory）和量子信息论的数学框架，通过证明多个条件的等价性建立核心定理。利用Plancherel维数（Plancherel dimension）、条件期望距离（conditional-expectation distance）、有限线性规划（finite linear programs）和决策见证（decision witnesses）等工具进行分析，并结合确定性辅助编码（deterministic ancillary code）进行数值验证。

Result: 证明表示完备性是量子后处理普遍约化为经典卷积的精确载体条件；确定正交轨道（orthogonal orbit）和不变量校准种子（invariant calibration seed）所需的最小辅助维度；给出不完整载体的精确条件期望距离公式1-1/S(U)及显式的量子-经典缺陷差距；对不可约载体给出闭合形式的缺陷表达式，并以S₃群（三阶置换群）的二维忠实表示为实例，得到相对于经典卷积精确10%的缩减。

Conclusion: 表示完备性是量子后处理约化为经典卷积的充要条件。结果同时涵盖了共轭表示（conjugation representation）下的律可识别性（law identifiability）表征、无限紧致群（infinite compact groups）上的有限维障碍（finite-dimensional obstruction）与稳定可视带重建，为群值失配量子参考令牌的信道退化问题提供了完整的理论刻画。

Abstract: A finite quantum reference token with group-valued misalignment induces a random-unitary channel, but optimal degradation is generally an optimization over all quantum post-processings. For a unitary representation U of a finite group G, we prove that the following conditions are equivalent: U contains every irreducible type; one ancilla-assisted input has an orthonormal G-orbit; signed group measures embed isometrically into channels in diamond norm; and, for every pair of noise laws p,q, $\inf_{Λ\in\mathrm{CPTP}} \frac{1}{2}\|Φ_q^U-Λ\circΦ_p^U\|_\diamond =\min_{r\in\mathcal{P}(G)}\frac{1}{2}\|q-r*p\|_1$. Thus representation completeness is the exact carrier condition for universal reduction of quantum post-processing to classical convolution. We determine the minimum ancilla dimensions for an orthogonal orbit and for an invariant calibration seed. For an incomplete carrier, with visible Plancherel dimension S(U), we derive the exact conditional-expectation distance $\frac{1}{2}\|\operatorname{id}-Φ_u^U\|_\diamond=1-1/S(U)$ and an explicit quantum--classical deficiency gap. For irreducible carriers the deficiency is obtained in closed form; the faithful two-dimensional representation of $S_3$ yields an exact ten-percent reduction relative to classical convolution. We also characterize law identifiability through the conjugation representation, provide finite linear programs and decision witnesses, and establish both a finite-dimensional obstruction and stable visible-band reconstruction for infinite compact groups. Deterministic ancillary code reproduces the finite-group examples and numerical regression checks.

### [9] [The log log jam in Gaussian state tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12983)
*Sitan Chen,Weiyuan Gong,Qi Ye,Zhihan Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了连续变量系统（continuous-variable systems）中量子态层析（state tomography）的能量依赖性是测量方案本身的根本限制，而非分析方法的人为产物。研究表明：使用高斯测量（Gaussian measurements）的任何协议都必须付出 log log E 的样本复杂度代价，而使用高度纠缠的非高斯测量（non-Gaussian measurements）则可以完全避免能量依赖，实现与能量无关的学习效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续变量系统中量子态层析的样本复杂度（sample complexity）在无物理约束时可能无界，即使对于具有有限维描述的高斯态（Gaussian states），已知最优协议也仅能达到 log log E 的缩放速率。需要澄清这种能量依赖性是否源于现有分析方法的局限，抑或是测量方案本身固有的根本限制。

Method: 通过理论证明分析：(1) 证明任何使用高斯测量的协议——无论是否纠缠或自适应——都必须存在 log log E 依赖；(2) 刻画自适应轮数与能量依赖之间的光滑权衡(tradeoff)，并给出匹配该插值速率的协议；(3) 提出使用高度纠缠的非高斯测量，以 O(n²/ε²) 样本学习 n 模纯高斯态，与能量 E 无关；(4) 基于 Holevo 和 Helstrom 的单副本规范相位 POVM（single-copy canonical phase POVM），提出以 O(1/ε²) 样本学习单模纯高斯态的简单协议，同样与 E 无关。

Result: (1) 证实高斯测量协议的根本限制是 log log E 依赖，回答了此前多项工作的开放问题；(2) 发现自适应轮数与能量依赖之间存在光滑权衡，并给出匹配协议；(3) 高度纠缠的非高斯测量可实现与能量无关的纯高斯态学习；(4) 基于规范相位 POVM 的简单协议同样实现能量无关学习。

Conclusion: 研究结果阐明了能量在玻色子态层析（bosonic state tomography）中的角色，揭示了自适应（adaptivity）、纠缠（entanglement）与魔法（magic）在量子学习中引人入胜的相互作用。

Abstract: Unlike in finite dimensions, quantum information in continuous-variable systems has the peculiar feature that without imposing physical constraints, the sample complexity of state tomography can be unbounded. Remarkably, this is even the case for state-of-the-art protocols for learning Gaussian states, which have finite-dimensional descriptions: the best known rates scale with $\log \log E$, where $E$ is the energy of the system. We prove this is not an artifact of existing analyses, but a fundamental limitation of the measurements used. We show: (1) Any protocol that uses Gaussian measurements, even entangled or adaptively chosen ones, must incur a $\log \log E$ dependence. This answers an open question posed by a number of previous works. (2) There is a smooth tradeoff between the number of rounds of adaptivity and the energy dependence, and we give a matching protocol achieving this interpolated rate. (3) With highly entangled, non-Gaussian measurements, one can learn $n$-mode pure Gaussian states with $O(n^2 / ε^2)$ samples, independent of $E$. This answers an open question posed by Chen et al. (4) A simple protocol based on the single-copy canonical phase POVM of Holevo and Helstrom learns single-mode pure Gaussian states with $O(1/ε^2)$ samples, again independent of $E$.
  Our results clarify the role of energy in bosonic state tomography and shed new light on the intriguing interplay between adaptivity, entanglement, and magic in quantum learning.

### [10] [Fixed-Boost Wigner Noise: Strict Trace-Distance Contraction without Quantum Degradability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12994)
*Maxim V. Churilov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在固定洛伦兹助推（Lorentz boost）下，通过对不确定动量进行约化，可以严格收缩每对自旋态的迹距离（trace distance），但不会产生从较少收缩的一端可退化（degradable）的信道。文章刻画了由固定Wigner角与横向动量方向生成的反演对称信道锥（inversion-symmetric channel cone），其中包含Pauli族M_α；并通过优化与扰动分析表明，所有正噪声成员在CPTP后处理下两两不可比较，且非恒等成员无法嵌入时间齐次Pauli对角Lindblad半群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过固定观测者助推与不确定动量的约化，构建反演对称信道锥，刻画Pauli族M_α；利用迹距离比较与CPTP后处理优化，求解最优转换因子，并构造纯五分量动量态的窄波包极限实现。

Result: M_β比M_α使得所有自旋态对间的迹距离更严格地收缩；最佳线性后处理因子具有负的归一化Choi特征值，且所有正噪声成员在CPTP后处理下两两不可比较；非恒等成员无法嵌入时间齐次Pauli对角Lindblad半群。

Conclusion: 自旋可区分性的排序本身无法决定量子统计后处理序，表明相对论性退相干与标准信道序之间存在根本差异。

Abstract: A Lorentz boost acts on the canonical spin of a massive particle through a momentum-dependent Wigner rotation. We show that, for one fixed observer boost, reducing over an uncertain momentum can strictly contract every pairwise spin-state trace distance without producing a channel that is degradable from the less contracted one. For spin $1/2$, we first characterize the exact inversion-symmetric channel cone generated by a fixed Wigner angle and transverse momentum directions. Inside this cone lies the Pauli family $M_α=\operatorname{diag}(1-α,1-α,1-2α)$, $0\leqα<1/2$. For $0<α<β<1/2$, all trace distances between distinct spin states are strictly smaller after $M_β$ than after $M_α$, yet the unique linear post-processing factor has a negative normalized Choi eigenvalue. We solve the optimization over all physical converters exactly: $\frac{1}{2}\inf_{Λ\in\mathrm{CPTP}}\|Φ_β-Λ\circΦ_α\|_\diamond=\frac{α(β-α)}{2-3α}$, whereas the reverse deficiency is $β-α$. Thus the identity dominates the family, while all positive-noise members are pairwise incomparable under CPTP post-processing. The ideal construction is realized as the narrow-packet limit of pure, normalizable five-component momentum states, and explicit perturbation and finite-shot tomography bounds certify an open set of examples. Separately, every nonidentity member fails embedding in a time-homogeneous Pauli-diagonal Lindblad semigroup. Hence ordering all unassisted spin distinguishabilities does not determine the quantum statistical post-processing order.

### [11] [Quantum incompatibility of Born probabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12032)
*Esteban Castro-Ruiz,Nathan Cohen,Luis C. Barbado,Časlav Brukner*

TL;DR: 本文论证了当测量相对于非理想量子参考系（non-ideal quantum reference frames）进行时，量子态（quantum state）本身作为概率目录的假设不再成立——即使在无穷多次实验下，相对频率（relative frequencies）仍可能保持量子意义上的不确定性，并通过贝尔型定理（Bell-type theorem）证明了这种不确定性的不可归约性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子理论通常假设量子态本身是良定义的，但这一假设隐含地依赖于测量相对于理想、无限资源参考系（infinitely-resourceful reference frames）的进行。本文旨在揭示当参考系非理想时，该假设的失效及其物理后果。

Method: 通过分析非理想量子参考系下的测量过程，证明相对频率仍存在不可归约的量子不确定性；并进一步提出了基于脉冲零差探测（pulsed homodyne detection）的量子光学实验方案，以实现这种关系性测量（relational measurements）。

Result: 证明了相对频率的贝尔型定理（Bell-type theorem for relative frequencies），表明即使在无穷多次实验的极限下，概率本身也可以是不确定的；这种不确定性在量子力学意义上是不可归约的。

Conclusion: 研究结果促使量子态的概念需要被扩展到有限资源约束的情形下，预计对量子理论与广义相对论（general relativity）的界面尤其重要，因为时空有界区域内的资源和信息本质上是有限的。

Abstract: Quantum theory challenges the view that individual measurement outcomes are predefined and independent of the measurement context. Yet the quantum state itself -- the catalogue of probabilities for all possible measurements -- is usually assumed to be well defined. We argue that this assumption tacitly relies on measurements being performed relative to ideal, infinitely-resourceful reference frames. We show that, when measurements are made relative to non-ideal quantum reference frames, the probabilities themselves become indefinite: even in the limit of arbitrarily large number of runs, the relative frequencies may remain uncertain. The uncertainty is irreducible in a quantum-mechanical sense, as we show by proving a Bell-type theorem for relative frequencies. We further propose a quantum-optical implementation of these relational measurements based on pulsed homodyne detection. Our findings motivate an extension of the notion of the quantum state to regimes constrained by finite resources. We expect them to be especially relevant at the interface between quantum theory and general relativity, where the resources and information available in a bounded region of spacetime are fundamentally limited.

Abstract: The unification of quantum mechanics and general relativity remains one of the major open problems of theoretical physics. Here, we implement a toy model of this duality called the HaPPY code, a quantum error-correcting code in the form of a tensor network with hyperbolic entanglement patterns, on a trapped-ion quantum computer. We present the first experimental confirmation of the Faulkner-Lewkowycz-Maldacena formula in this model - a key test of the holographic correspondence. ### [13] [Entangling Power and Symmetries in the Quantum Rabi Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12053)
*Ian Low,Jens Koch,Sahel Ashhab*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过时间平均纠缠功率（time-averaged entangling power）作为算子级诊断工具，研究了量子拉比模型（quantum Rabi model）家族中的隐藏对称性（hidden symmetry）与显式U(1)对称性。分析发现，时间平均纠缠功率在非对称量子拉比模型（AQRM）的整数偏置点处出现峰值，对应隐藏对称性位置，而在杰恩斯-卡明斯模型（JC）的U(1)对称点处出现弱谷值，表明该诊断量可有效揭示光-物质系统中的对称性结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子拉比模型是光-物质相互作用中最简单但仍包含非平凡结构的基础有效哈密顿量。该家族中包含具有显式U(1)对称性的杰恩斯-卡明斯模型（Jaynes-Cummings model, JC）和具有依赖于参数的“隐藏”对称性（仅当偏置条件ε/ω∈ℤ时出现）的非对称量子拉比模型（asymmetric quantum Rabi model, AQRM）。需要一种算子级诊断工具来揭示并区分这些不同类型的对称性结构。

Method: 采用时间平均纠缠功率（time-averaged entangling power）作为算子级诊断量。由于振荡子希尔伯特空间（oscillator Hilbert space）是无穷维的，比较了两种有限输入系综：一是对福克空间截断（Fock-space truncation）后的哈尔平均（Haar average），二是在固定平均占据数n̅下的相干态平均（coherent-state average）。

Result: 两种诊断方案均在AQRM的整数偏置点（即隐藏对称性所在处）出现峰值。相反地，在JC点的显式U(1)对称性处出现弱谷值。时间平均纠缠功率对拉比家族中的隐藏对称性和U(1)对称性均有响应，且响应的正负符号反映了对称性如何重新组织谱展开。

Conclusion: 时间平均纠缠功率可以作为一种算子诊断工具（operator diagnostic），用于揭示光-物质系统中隐藏对称性与显式对称性的存在及其性质。

Abstract: The quantum Rabi model is a standard effective Hamiltonian in studies of light-matter interaction, capturing the simplest nontrivial setting in which a qubit couples to a single harmonic oscillator. Within the broader Rabi family, we focus on two special cases: the Jaynes-Cummings (JC) model, which carries an explicit $U(1)$ symmetry, and the asymmetric quantum Rabi model (AQRM), which possesses a parameter-dependent "hidden'' symmetry that appears only at integer bias, $\varepsilon/ω\in\mathbb{Z}$, and is not manifest in the Hamiltonian. We use the time-averaged entangling power as an operator-level diagnostic of these symmetry structures. Since the oscillator Hilbert space is infinite-dimensional, we compare two finite input ensembles: a Haar average after Fock-space truncation and a coherent-state average at fixed mean occupation $\bar{n}$. Both diagnostics show peaks at the integer-bias points of the AQRM, where the hidden symmetry resides. In contrast, the manifest $U(1)$ symmetry at the JC point instead gives a weak dip. Thus, the time-averaged entangling power responds to both the hidden symmetry and the $U(1)$ symmetry in the Rabi family, with the sign of the response indicating how the symmetry reorganizes the spectral expansion. These results demonstrate that the entangling power can serve as an operator diagnostic to reveal the presence and properties of hidden and manifest symmetries in light-matter systems.

### [14] [Thermally Activated Long-Range Entanglement from Non-Abelian Conservation Laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12710)
*Shuai Zeng*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在非阿贝尔守恒律（non-Abelian conservation law）约束下，局域热涨落（local thermal fluctuations）可被转化为无界操作资源，使系统在高温柔区间内产生随尺寸发散的蒸馏纠缠熵（distillable entanglement），从而颠覆了“热噪声抑制量子纠缠”的传统认知。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统认知认为热噪声会抑制量子纠缠。本文旨在探究非阿贝尔守恒律能否将局域热涨落转化为操作上有用的纠缠资源，从而在高温下实现可蒸馏纠缠。

Method: 针对有限范围SU(2)不变自旋链（$SU(2)$-invariant spin chains）的全局单态子空间，提出显式表示空间（representation-space）方案，分析热涨落产生的子系统自旋及其不可约表示（irreducible representations）；并结合精确可解二聚体链（dimer chain）与非可积链的精确对角化进行数值验证。

Result: 在有限高温柔区间内，蒸馏纠缠熵$E_{\mathrm{D}}$满足$E_{\mathrm{D}}\geq Y_N=\frac12\log_2 N+O_β(1)$；二聚体链在任意有限温度下$E_{\mathrm{D}}=\frac{1}{2}\log_2 N+C(T)+o(1)$，且存在交叉标度$T_*(N)\simΔ/\ln N$；非可积链的精确对角化结果与预测标度一致。

Conclusion: 当热化过程受到非阿贝尔守恒律约束时，加热（heating）能够激活系统尺寸发散的可蒸馏纠缠，在宏观二分（macroscopic bipartition）上产生有实用的量子纠缠资源。

Abstract: Thermal noise ordinarily suppresses quantum entanglement. We show that a strong non-Abelian conservation law can convert local thermal fluctuations into an unbounded operational resource. For a broad class of finite-range $SU(2)$-invariant spin chains restricted to the global-singlet sector, an explicit representation-space protocol yields $Y_N=\frac12\log_2 N+O_β(1)$, and hence $E_{\mathrm{D}}\geq Y_N$, throughout a finite high-temperature interval. Local thermal fluctuations produce subsystem spins $j\sim\sqrt N$, whose globally locked irreducible representations contain $\log_2(2j+1)\sim\frac12\log_2N$ ebits. An exactly solvable dimer chain exhibits a sharper effect: its zero-temperature state is unentangled across the cut, whereas every fixed $T>0$ produces $E_{\mathrm{D}}=\frac{1}{2}\log_2 N+C(T)+o(1)$, with crossover scale $T_*(N)\simΔ/\ln N$. Exact diagonalization of a nonintegrable chain is consistent with the predicted scaling. Thus heating can activate system-size-diverging distillable entanglement across a macroscopic bipartition when thermalization is confined by a non-Abelian conservation law.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.GA'></div>

# astro-ph.GA [[Back]](#toc)

### [15] [Discovery of a star sensitive to the spin of Sgr A*](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12664)
*K. Abd El Dayem,R. Abuter,N. Aimar,P. Amaro-Seoane,A. Berdeu,J. -P. Berger,G. Bourdarot,W. Brandner,A. Burkert,D. Calderon,C. Correia,J. Cuadra,R. Davies,D. Defrere,L. Delit,A. Drescher,F. Eisenhauer,L. Esteras Otal,M. Fabricius,H. Feuchtgruber,N. M. Foerster Schreiber,A. Foschi,P. Garcia,R. Garcia Lopez,A. Generozov,R. Genzel,S. Gillessen,F. Gonte,X. Haubois,S. F. Hoenig,M. Houlle,S. Joharle,A. Kaufer,J. Kammerer,P. Kervella,J. Kolb,L. Kreidberg,L. Labadie,S. Lacour,O. Lai,R. Laugier,J. -B. Le Bouquin,J. Leftley,B. Lopez,D. Lutz,F. Mang,A. Merand,F. Millour,M. Montarges,N. Morujao,H. Nowacki,M. Nowak,S. Oberti,J. Osorno,T. Ott,T. Paumard,C. Paladini,H. B. Perets,K. Perraut,G. Perrin,R. Petrov,P. O. Petrucci,T. Piran,N. Pourre,S. Rabien,D. C. Ribeiro,S. Robbe-Dubois,M. Sadun Bordoni,J. Sanchez Bermudez,D. Santos,R. Sari,J. Sauter,S. Scheithauer,J. Scigliuto,J. Shangguan,T. T. Shimizu,F. Soulez,J. Stadler,C. Straubmeier,E. Sturm,M. Subroweit,C. Sykes,L. J. Tacconi,P. Thevenet,I. Urso,F. Vincent,J. Woillez,G. Zins*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文报告发现一颗名为 S301 的暗弱主序星，其轨道周期为 8.7 年，近心点距离足够小，使得峰值速度达到 25000 km/s。通过当前近红外干涉测量和未来极大望远镜光谱观测，S301 的运动能够直接敏感于 Sgr A* 的自旋（spin），从而探测 Kerr 度规（Kerr metric）下的 β³ 阶相对论效应，并暗示其可能通过 Hills 机制（Hills mechanism）捕获而来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人马座 A*（Sgr A*）是距离最近的大质量黑洞（massive black hole, MBH），其周围恒星作为测试粒子（test particles）可探测引力势，但此前仅能测量到 β² 阶的史瓦西度规（Schwarzschild metric）修正（引力红移、横向多普勒效应、顺行进动）。为了探测 β³ 阶的 Kerr 度规自旋效应，需要一颗轨道近心点足够小、速度足够高的恒星。

Method: 通过长期天文观测，发现一颗暗弱主序星 S301（m_K = 19.3），其轨道周期为 8.7 年，轨道偏心率高，近心点距离极小，使得峰值速度达到 25000 km/s。利用当前近红外干涉测量（near-infrared interferometry）和未来极大望远镜（extremely large telescope, ELT）光谱测量来解析其轨道运动。

Result: S301 的轨道运动直接敏感于 Sgr A* 的自旋，能够探测 Kerr 度规下 β³ 阶的相对论修正。其高偏心率表明 S301 可能是在 Hills 机制（Hills mechanism）中双星被撕裂后被捕获的成员星。

Conclusion: S301 的发现为直接测量 Sgr A* 自旋提供了前所未有的机会，标志着从史瓦西度规（Schwarzschild metric）观测进入 Kerr 度规（Kerr metric）观测的新阶段，并揭示了该恒星可能的动力学起源。

Abstract: Residing in the center of the Milky Way, Sgr A* is the closest massive black hole (MBH). Its vicinity has allowed measuring individual stellar orbits around it. The stars act as test particles and probe the gravitational potential around the $4.3 \times 10^6 M_\odot$ MBH. These observations have determined the central mass to sub-percent precision, and the mildly relativistic motions of stars have given access to the dominant relativistic corrections, the gravitational redshift, the transverse Doppler effect, and the prograde precession imposed by the Schwarzschild metric nature of the potential. These effects are of order $β^2 = (v/c)^2$ (for velocity $v$ and speed of light $c$). The Kerr metric for a rotating black hole leads to corrections of order $β^3$. Here, we report the discovery of a faint main-sequence star ($m_K = 19.3$), S301, on a 8.7-year orbit and with small enough a pericenter distance, such that the star's peak velocity reaches $25000\,$km/s. Within the measurement capabilities of current near-infrared interferometry and future spectroscopy on an extremely large telescope, S301's motion is directly sensitive to the spin of Sgr A*. The high eccentricity of S301 suggests that it is the captured component of a binary that was torn apart via the Hills mechanism.

</details>

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [16] [Solitary waves of attracting SU(N) fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12484)
*Aysha Alsubaihi,Wayne J. Chetcuti,Frederic Chevy,Juan Polo,Luigi Amico*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了在一维环形晶格上具有吸引相互作用的 SU(N) 费米子中束缚态的形成、动力学及其对无序的鲁棒性，通过精确对角化和 Bethe ansatz 方法解析多体谱，并发现每组分单粒子下的束缚态动力学表现为具有重整化有效质量的多体量子行走，类似于经典孤子的保形运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解吸引相互作用 SU(N) 费米子系统中束缚态的形成与动力学行为，并检验其在无序条件下的稳定性，为多体量子行走和费米子孤立波（fermionic solitary waves）的动力学特征提供理论依据。

Method: 采用固定动量扇区的精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和 Bethe ansatz 精确结果作为指导，将多体能谱（many-body spectrum）按粒子组合成束缚复合体的可能分区解析为能带；通过密度-密度以及 N 体关联函数（N-body correlations）表征内部结构；并引入钉扎淬火协议（pinning quench protocol）和原位无序（on-site disorder）研究动力学与鲁棒性。

Result: 随吸引相互作用相对于单粒子跳跃（single-particle hopping）的增强，系统从色散传播（dispersive spreading）转变为动力学局域化（dynamical localization）；每组分单粒子下的束缚态动力学表现类似于具有重整化有效质量（re-normalized effective mass）的单粒子的多体量子行走（many-body quantum walk），这是经典孤子保形运动的量子对应。

Conclusion: 吸引相互作用 SU(N) 费米子在每组分单粒子条件下可支持形状保持的束缚态量子行走，该行为可作为费米子孤立波的动力学标识；同时，该系统在无序作用下仍保持一定的动力学鲁棒性。

Abstract: We study the formation, dynamics, and disorder robustness of bound states in attractively interacting SU(N) fermions on a one-dimensional ring lattice. Using exact diagonalization in fixed-momentum sectors and Bethe ansatz exact results as a guide, we resolve the many-body spectrum into bands related to the possible partitions of the particles into bound composites, and characterize their internal structure also through density-density and N-body correlations. A pinning quench protocol reveals a transition from dispersive spreading to dynamical localization as the attractive interaction increases relative to the single-particle hopping. We find that the bound state dynamics for one-particle per component occurs as a many-body quantum walk similar to that of a single particle with a re-normalized effective mass. Such a property, that is the quantum version of the shape-preserving motion of classical solitons, can provide the dynamical signature of the fermionic solitary waves. We probe the robustness of the fermionic bound-state dynamics under on-site disorder.

</details>


### [17] [Standard basis operator method for ground-state and temperature properties of single and two-component Bose-Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12718)
*Oliwier Urbański,Tomasz P. Polak*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文改进了三维单组分和双组分Bose-Hubbard模型的标准基算符（SBO）方法。单组分情况下，通过考虑更多在位态而非先前仅三种，显著提升了非零温度预测的定性与定量精度，并通过临界线附近自洽方程的渐近分析改进了数值计算性能。双组分情况下，SBO推广效果有限，仅能描述种内涨落而无法处理种间涨落，尽管如此仍预测了相图的非平凡变形及由化学势变化调控的一级相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 改进标准基算符（SBO）方法在三维Bose-Hubbard模型中的应用，克服先前工作仅考虑三种在位态的局限性，并提升数值计算效率与预测准确性。

Method: 采用改进的标准基算符（standard basis operator, SBO）方法，引入必要数量的在位态（on-site states），并对临界线附近的自洽方程进行渐近分析（asymptotic analysis）以优化数值计算。

Result: 单组分SBO方法在定性与定量上优于仅考虑三种在位态的先前工作，结果与蒙特卡洛（Monte-Carlo）、张量网络（tensor networks）、量子转子方法（Quantum Rotor Approach）及实验数据吻合；双组分SBO方法仅能处理种内涨落，无法描述种间涨落，但仍预测了相图变形及由化学势驱动的一级相变。

Conclusion: 单组分情况下改进的SBO方法有效提升了Bose-Hubbard模型的非零温度预测能力；双组分情况下SBO存在根本性局限，需进一步探索适用于处理种间涨落的替代方法。

Abstract: We formulate an improved standard basis operator (SBO) method for the single and two-component Bose-Hubbard model in three dimensions. In the first case, nonzero temperature predictions are qualitatively and quantitatively enhanced by taking into account necessary number of on-site states, not just three as in previous works. Performance of the final numerical calculations is also improved by asymptotic analysis of the self-consistent equations near the critical line. Obtained results are compared with Monte-Carlo, tensor networks, Quantum Rotor Approach and experimental data. In the two-component case, SBO generalizes rather poorly, being able to account for intra-species thermal and quantum fluctuations, but not the inter-species ones. Deeper reasons for this situation are discussed. Still however, non-trivial deformation of the phase diagrams is predicted, together with first-order phase transitions steered by the changes in chemical potential.

</details>

Wu,X. Wu,Y. Wu,Z. Wu,K. Wyllie,S. Xian,Z. Xiang,Y. Xie,T. X. Xing,A. Xu,L. Xu,M. Xu,R. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,S. Yadav,K. Yang,X. Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,K. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,F. Zangari,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,Q. Z. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,J. Zhao,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica,X. Zuo*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用LHCb实验采集的质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量13 TeV，积分亮度5.4 fb^{-1}）首次在强子对撞机上搜索了辐射轻子衰变 B^+→μ^+ν_μγ 和 B_c^+→μ^+ν_μγ。未观测到显著信号超出本底，在90%置信水平下设置了分支比上限，并首次实验研究了 B_c^+→μ^+ν_μγ 衰变过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 辐射轻子衰变（radiative leptonic decays）是研究B介子（B meson）内部结构与标准模型（Standard Model）轻子味守恒的重要探针，但目前B^+→μ^+ν_μγ和B_c^+→μ^+ν_μγ衰变在强子对撞机上尚未被搜索过，B_c^+→μ^+ν_μγ更从未被实验研究过。

Method: 基于LHCb实验在质心能量13 TeV、积分亮度5.4 fb^{-1}的质子-质子对撞数据，对候选事件进行本底扣除与信号拟合，寻找B^+→μ^+ν_μγ和B_c^+→μ^+ν_μγ衰变的显著信号超出。

Result: 未观察到两种信号衰变的事件超出本底。在90%置信水平下，设置B^+→μ^+ν_μγ（光子能量E_γ^* > 1 GeV）的分支比上限为4.0×10^{-6}，B_c^+→μ^+ν_μγ（E_γ^* > 1 GeV）的分支比上限为1.6×10^{-3}。

Conclusion: 该研究是首次在强子对撞机上搜索B^+→μ^+ν_μγ和B_c^+→μ^+ν_μγ衰变，也是迄今对B_c^+→μ^+ν_μγ衰变的首次实验探索。所设置的分支比上限为未来理论模型与实验测量提供了基准约束。

Abstract: A search for the radiative leptonic decays $B^+\toμ^+ν_μγ$ and $B^+_c\toμ^+ν_μγ$ is performed using proton-proton collision data collected with the LHCb experiment at a center-of-mass energy of $13~{\rm TeV}$, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $5.4~{\rm fb}^{-1}$. No evidence for an excess of events over background is observed for either signal decay. Upper limits at 90% confidence level are set on the branching fractions: \begin{align} {\cal{B}}(B^+\toμ^+ν_μγ)_{E_γ^\ast > 1\,\rm{GeV}} &< 4.0 \times 10^{-6},\\ {\cal{B}}(B_c^+\toμ^+ν_μγ)_{E_γ^\ast > 1\,\rm{GeV}} &< 1.6 \times 10^{-3}, \end{align} where the photon energy in the $B$-meson rest frame, $E_γ^\ast$, is required to be greater than $1~{\rm GeV}$. This constitutes the first search for these decays at a hadron collider and the first experimental investigation of the $B_c^+\toμ^+ν_μγ$ decay to date.

</details>


### [19] [Observation of pair production of longitudinally polarized $Z$ bosons in four-lepton final state with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12879)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 利用ATLAS探测器采集的质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量13.6 TeV，积分亮度164 fb⁻¹），通过两个同味反号轻子对重建候选事例，测量双Z玻色子极化分数。在共生区域内及四轻子不变质量的两个分区域中测量结果与标准模型预言一致。通过与13 TeV数据的统计组合，首次观察到两个同时纵向极化的Z玻色子产生过程，观测显著性和预期显著性分别为6.5倍和5.6倍标准差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双Z玻色子产生过程是检验电弱相互作用理论和标准模型（Standard Model）的重要探针，而同时纵向极化的Z玻色子对产生此前尚未被实验观测到，是当前粒子物理实验的一个关键未验证预言。

Method: 使用ATLAS实验采集的质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量√s=13.6 TeV，积分亮度164 fb⁻¹），通过两个同味反号轻子对（电子或缪子对）重建Z玻色子对（ZZ）候选事例。在包容性共生相空间（fiducial phase space）以及四轻子不变质量的两个分区域中测量双Z玻色子的极化分数（polarization fractions）。

Result: 双Z玻色子的极化分数测量结果与标准模型预言在不确定度范围内一致。通过与质心能量13 TeV的前期测量数据进行统计组合后，首次实现了两个同时纵向极化的Z玻色子产生过程的观测，观测显著性为6.5倍标准差，预期显著性为5.6倍标准差。

Conclusion: 首次观测到了两个同时纵向极化的Z玻色子产生过程，该结果在超过5倍标准差的显著性水平上验证了标准模型关于电弱相互作用中纵向极化矢量玻色子散射的预言。

Abstract: The production of two longitudinally polarized $Z$ bosons is measured using proton-proton collision data recorded by the ATLAS experiment at a center-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV and with an integrated luminosity of 164 fb$^{-1}$. The $ZZ$ candidate events are reconstructed using two same-flavor opposite-charge electron or muon pairs. The polarization fractions of the $Z$ boson pair are measured inclusively in the fiducial phase space and also in two regions of the four-lepton invariant mass, and the results are consistent with the Standard Model predictions. After a statistical combination with a previous measurement at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV, the first observation of the production of two simultaneously longitudinally polarized $Z$ bosons is obtained, with observed and expected significances of 6.5 and 5.6 standard deviations, respectively.

</details>

### [20] [A new model for the continuum spectra of AM CVn binaries and multi-messenger inference with normalizing flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12971)
*Nathan Steinle,Samar Safi-Harb,Austin MacMaster,Liliana Rivera Sandoval,Katelyn Breivik,Tyrone E. Woods,Tom Maccarone,Tom Wagg*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文针对银河系超致密双星（UCBs）中的AM CVn型双星，提出了一种从源参数到X射线、光学、紫外连续谱辐射的前向模型，并结合LISA引力波观测与双星族合成，预测约1/7000的AM CVn双星可实现LISA、CASTOR和AXIS的多信使联合探测。同时开发了基于卷积神经网络和归一化流的逆模型推断框架，在吸积体质量、供体质量、轨道周期和距离上实现了较高精度的参数重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来电磁望远镜（如NewAthena、CASTOR、AXIS类任务）和毫赫兹引力波探测器（如LISA）有望发现大量银河系超致密双星（UCBs），而AM CVn型双星作为其中重要的传质系统，其形成、演化和可观测特征仍存在不确定性，亟需理论工具的进步以应对未来的数据挑战。

Method: 方法包括三部分：一是建立AM CVn双星连续谱辐射的前向模型（forward model），该模型假设引力波驱动的传质，并包含吸积能量学、发射几何、吸收和仪器响应的物理参数化描述；二是将该模型与LISA观测及双星族合成输出结合，探索多信使特性；三是开发逆向模型（inverse model）框架，利用卷积神经网络（convolutional neural net）和归一化流（normalizing flows）从观测数据推断双星参数。

Result: 模型预测约每7000个AM CVn双星中有一个可实现与LISA、CASTOR和AXIS的联合多信使探测。逆向模型测试显示，推断的吸集体质量平均绝对分数误差为0.05 M☉，供体质量为0.26 M☉，轨道周期为0.1秒，距离为0.2秒差距；Spearman秩相关检验表明，除供体质量外，真实分布与预测分布高度相关。

Conclusion: 该工作为未来十年开展有效的多信使科学发现奠定了理论基础，支持后续关于详细双星天体物理学以及联合探测观测需求的研究。

Abstract: Future electromagnetic telescopes, such as $\textit{NewAthena}$, $\textit{CASTOR}$, and an $\textit{AXIS}$-like mission, along with milli-Hz gravitational-wave (GW) detectors such as $\textit{LISA}$, are expected to unearth the population of Galactic ultra-compact binaries (UCBs). Joint multi-messenger detections will probe the uncertain formation, evolution, and observables of mass-transferring UCBs such as AM CVns, but theoretical tools need to be advanced to anticipate future data challenges. Motivated by this, we present a new forward model for the continuum emission of AM CVn binaries that connects source binary parameters to X-ray, optical, and ultraviolet observables. The model assumes GW-driven mass transfer with physically motivated prescriptions for accretion energetics, emission geometry, absorption, and instrumental response. Combining this with $\textit{LISA}$ observations and the output of binary population synthesis enables exploration of the multi-messenger properties of AM CVns. Although uncertain, our model predicts that approximately one per $7000$ AM CVn binaries will permit a joint multi-messenger detection with $\textit{LISA}$, $\textit{CASTOR}$, and $\textit{AXIS}$. We also develop a framework for inferring binary parameters from the inverse model with a convolutional neural net and normalizing flows. Testing the trained flow with our synthetic AM CVn population, we find mean absolute fractional error on the inferred accretor mass of $0.05$ M$_{\odot}$, donor mass of $0.26$ M$_{\odot}$, orbital period of $0.1$ s, and distance of $0.2$ pc, while Spearman's rank shows strongly correlated true and predicted distributions except for the donor mass. These efforts lay a foundation for follow-up studies that will explore detailed binary astrophysics and observational requirements for effective multi-messenger scientific discovery in the coming decade.

</details>


### [21] [Supernova Neutrinos and the Origin of Biomolecular Homochirality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12813)
*Amirmasoud Jannat,Soroush Shakeri,Farhad Shahbazi*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出超新星中微子与星际分子云中手性分子之间的宇称破坏相互作用，通过远离平衡态的噪声诱导自催化系统放大手性偏差，产生超过10%的对映体过量（enantiomeric excess），为生物分子同手性（biomolecular homochirality）的起源提供天体物理机制，并与陨石化学分析结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释生物分子同手性（biomolecular homochirality）的起源——即天然氨基酸几乎全部为L型、糖类几乎全部为D型这一令人费解的现象，寻找一种能够产生初始手性偏差（chiral bias）的天体物理机制。

Method: 将超新星中微子与手性分子（chiral molecules）的宇称破坏相互作用（parity-violating interactions）引入远离平衡态（far-from-equilibrium）的噪声诱导自催化化学反应（autocatalytic chemical reactions）系统中，在伊藤微积分（Ito calculus）意义下求解随机方程，获得对映体过量（enantiomeric excess）概率分布的动力学演化。

Result: 尽管超新星中微子相互作用微弱，但该框架通过自催化与随机涨落（stochastic fluctuations）的放大机制，能够产生超过10%的对映体过量，与对陨石的最新化学分析结果吻合。通过对模型参数空间的扫描，识别出在星际分子云中产生同手性态（homochiral states）初始种子（initial seeds）的参数窗口。

Conclusion: 超新星中微子与手性分子的宇称破坏相互作用，结合自催化和随机涨落放大机制，可为地球上检测到的陨石手性偏差提供合理的天体物理来源，表明同手性种子（homochirality seeds）可能通过陨石撞击（meteorites）被运送到地球。

Abstract: We investigate the role of parity-violating interactions between supernova neutrinos and chiral molecules in nearby interstellar molecular clouds as a potential source of biomolecular homochirality. We introduce neutrino interactions into the autocatalytic chemical reactions in a far-from-equilibrium noise-induced system. These interactions create a directional bias between L and D enantiomers in the racemization reactions, which is amplified by autocatalysis and stochastic fluctuations. We solve the stochastic equations within the Ito sense to obtain the dynamics of the probability distribution of the enantiomeric excesses, offering an astrophysical scenario for the delivery of homochirality seeds to Earth by meteorites. In spite of the weak interactions of supernova neutrinos, our framework introduces an amplification mechanism to yield a considerable enantiomeric excess of more than $10\%$, in agreement with the latest chemical analysis of the meteorites. Moreover, we scan over the parameter space of the model, inferring from the observational values in order to explore the window of opportunity to generate the initial seeds of homochiral states in interstellar molecular clouds.

</details>


<div id='cs.ET'></div>

# cs.ET [[Back]](#toc)

### [22] [Reproducible Reservoir Computing with Thermally Driven Superparamagnets: Controlling Temperature Sensitivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12840)
*Zhengfei Chen,Alex Welbourne,Matthew O. A. Ellis,Dan A. Allwood,Eleni Vasilaki,Thomas J. Hayward*

Main category: cs.ET

TL;DR: 本文通过引入异质纳米点模式（heterogeneous nanodot patterns）来缓解超顺磁纳米点库计算基板（superparamagnetic nanodot reservoir computing substrates）因热激活效应（thermal activation effects）导致的温度敏感性，在5-35°C范围内实现了稳定的NARMA-10任务性能，为其实用化部署迈出关键一步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超顺磁纳米点库计算基板虽然具有超低能耗的潜力，但其动力学受热激活效应（thermal activation effects）主导，环境温度波动会导致任务性能显著下降，限制了其在实际环境中的部署。

Method: 通过模拟温度变化对超顺磁纳米点集合（superparamagnetic nanodot ensembles）磁化动力学（magnetization dynamics）的影响，量化温度对任务性能的影响；进而引入包含不同尺寸纳米点（不同特征热激活时间尺度）的异质纳米点模式（heterogeneous nanodot patterns），并利用库超参数（reservoir hyperparameters）调节性能与温度稳定性之间的权衡。

Result: 在NARMA-10任务上的基准测试（benchmark results）表明，优化后的异质性设计使库计算基板在5-35°C宽温度范围内保持稳定的性能，且最终性能几乎没有损失。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了通过异质纳米点设计提升超顺磁纳米点库计算系统温度鲁棒性的可行路径，是推动这类新型器件向实际部署应用的关键一步。

Abstract: Unconventional computing systems must demonstrate robust performance under real-world environmental conditions to enable practical deployments. We have recently proposed superparamagnetic nanodot ensembles driven by strain-induced magnetoelectric coupling as exciting candidates for use as ultra-low energy consumption reservoir computing substrates. However, because their dynamics are governed by thermal activation effects, these systems are intrinsically sensitive to ambient temperature fluctuations, leading to degraded task performance when operated outside the temperature range used during training. In this paper we simulate how temperature variations affect the magnetization dynamics of such superparamagnetic ensembles, and quantify how this affects task performance. We then show how heterogeneous nanodot patterns that incorporate different sizes of nanodots with different characteristic timescales for thermal activation mitigate this problem. Benchmark results on the NARMA-10 task show that introducing optimized heterogeneity stabilizes performance of the reservoirs across a wide range of ambient temperatures (5-35°C), with little loss of ultimate performance. We also characterize the trade-off between performance and temperature stability and show that it can be tuned via reservoir hyperparameters. Our study demonstrates a key step in making these novel devices suitable for real-world deployment.

</details>

### [23] [Expansion of the planetary Hamiltonian for small eccentricities and inclinations: a vector formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12003)
*Federico Mogavero*

Main category: math-ph

Method: 基于矢量形式（vector formalism）进行全新推导，将摄动函数（disturbing function）的长期部分及其他傅里叶谐波用系统不变平面（invariant plane）内向量的标量积（scalar product）表示。

Result: 成功证明摄动函数的长期部分及其他傅里叶谐波均可表示为不变平面内向量的标量积，并进一步利用轨道角动量矢量（angular momentum vector）和偏心率矢量（eccentricity vector）表达所有这些项。

Conclusion: 该矢量形式推导为行星哈密顿量的展开提供了一种更几何化的表述方式，有助于深化对轨道动力学结构的理解。

Abstract: We revisit the classical expansion of the planetary Hamiltonian for small eccentricities and mutual inclinations of the orbits, presenting a derivation based entirely on vector formalism. We demonstrate that the secular part of the disturbing function, as well as any other Fourier harmonic, can be expressed in terms of scalar products of vectors lying in the system's invariant plane. Furthermore, we show how to express any such term using the angular momentum and eccentricity vectors of the orbits.

### [24] [CORTET: Robust generation of simulation-ready cortical meshes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12157)
*Davood Shahsavari,Irina Grigorescu,Jiaxin Xiao,Nashira Baena,Aakash Saboo,Vanessa Kyriakopoulou,Alena Uus,Martin J. Bishop,Katherine R. Long,Emma C. Robinson*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出CORTET，一种全自动管线，可将胎儿MRI的三角化皮层表面转换为求解器就绪（solver-ready）的四面体网格（tetrahedral mesh），其最差单元质量满足严格稳定性目标，无需手动修复，并在近200个胎儿受试者中验证了网格质量，成功支撑了实际的形态弹性褶皱模拟（morphoelastic folding simulation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类大脑的折叠方式因人而异，这种自然变异干扰了神经发育障碍的影像生物标志物（imaging biomarker）搜索。基于物理学的模拟有助于确定导致这种变异性的因果机制，但模拟必须从大脑内部的实体四面体网格出发，而决定模拟能否运行的是网格中最差的单元而非平均单元。目前从胎儿MRI构建这类网格需要大量人工干预。

Method: CORTET是一个全自动管线，将三角化的皮层表面转换为求解器就绪的四面体网格。通过在同一输入表面上与通用四面体网格生成器进行基准比较，隔离管线本身的贡献与输入几何的影响。在覆盖褶皱期的近200个胎儿受试者队列中验证网格质量。

Result: 与通用四面体网格生成器相比，CORTET生成的网格在最差单元质量上满足严格稳定性目标，无需任何手动修复。从该管线直接获取的网格能够支撑真实胎儿受试者的数值稳定的形态弹性褶皱模拟。

Conclusion: CORTET实现了从胎儿MRI到模拟就绪四面体网格的全自动化流程，消除了当前流程中劳动密集的人工干预环节，为基于物理模拟研究大脑褶皱变异性及其与神经发育障碍的关系提供了可靠的计算工具。

Abstract: Every human brain folds differently, and such natural variation confounds the search for imaging biomarkers of neurodevelopmental disorders. Physics-based simulation can help determine the causal mechanisms that underpin this variability. Yet every simulation must be initiated from a solid tetrahedral mesh of the brain's interior, and it is the worst element in that mesh, not the average, that decides whether the simulation runs at all. Building that mesh from fetal MRI currently requires labour-intensive manual intervention. We therefore present CORTET (CORtical TETrahedral meshing): a fully automated pipeline that converts a triangulated cortical surface into a solver-ready tetrahedral mesh whose worst-element quality meets a strict stability target with no manual repair. By benchmarking against a general-purpose tetrahedral mesher on the same input surfaces, we isolate the pipeline's contribution from that of the input geometry, and we validate quality across a cohort of nearly 200 fetal subjects spanning the folding period. A mesh taken straight from the pipeline sustains a numerically stable morphoelastic folding simulation of a real fetal subject.

</details>


### [25] [Asymptotic forms of the Ursell edge waves on a gently sloping beach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12289)
*P. Zhevandrov,A. Merzon,M. I. Romero Rodríguez*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将Ursell束缚模的渐近表达式与标准WKB指数的逆傅里叶变换进行对比，引入Maslov正则算子（Maslov canonical operator）作为分析工具。

Result: 当小倾角参数alpha趋近于0时，Ursell束缚模的渐近行为恰好与Maslov正则算子的形式一致。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了Ursell束缚模与WKB-Maslov渐近理论的等价性，为小倾角海滩上的波动束缚问题提供了统一的渐近分析框架。

Abstract: It is shown that the asymptotics of the Ursell trapping modes on a sloping beach of small slope angle alpha coincide with the inverse Fourier transform of standard WKB exponentials, i.e., the Maslov canonical operator, as alpha tends to 0.

### [26] [A canonical two-scale Sonine fractional calculus induced by the Tricomi function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12534)
*Ivano Colombaro,Marc Tudela-Pi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Sonine核框架下引入了一类Tricomi型广义分数阶微积分（Tricomi-type generalized fractional calculus）。核心结果是：在允许的参数范围内，Tricomi分支是Stieltjes函数，其倒数为完全Bernstein函数，由此可导出Sonine分数阶微积分及其对应的Riemann-Liouville型和Caputo型导数。文中还证明了在Kummer类中，在固定自然渐近归一化后，Tricomi分支是唯一的Stieltjes代表，并给出了相应的Lévy–Khintchine表示、Volterra公式和标量Cauchy问题。所得到的算子具有两个独立渐近阶这一显著特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Sonine核框架下的广义分数阶微积分寻找新的、具有良好数学性质的函数类，特别是关注Tricomi分支的函数性质及其在分数阶微积分中的适用性。

Method: 基于Sonine核框架，引入Tricomi型广义分数阶微积分，利用Stieltjes函数和完全Bernstein函数（complete Bernstein function）的数学性质，构建Riemann-Liouville型和Caputo型导数，并借助Lévy–Khintchine表示、Volterra公式和标量Cauchy问题进行理论推导。

Result: 在所允许的参数范围内，Tricomi分支为Stieltjes函数，其倒数为完全Bernstein函数；在Kummer类中，固定自然渐近归一化后，Tricomi分支是唯一的Stieltjes代表；得到的算子展现出两个独立的渐近阶。

Conclusion: 本文建立的Tricomi型广义分数阶微积分在Sonine核框架下具有坚实的数学基础，算子的双渐近阶特征为其实际应用提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: We introduce a Tricomi-type generalized fractional calculus in the Sonine kernel framework. The key result is that the Tricomi branch is a Stieltjes function in the admissible parameter range, so its reciprocal is a complete Bernstein function. This fact induces a Sonine fractional calculus together with the canonical Tricomi integral and the associated Riemann--Liouville-type and Caputo-type derivatives. We also prove that, within the Kummer class, the Tricomi branch is the unique Stieltjes representative, once the natural asymptotic normalization is fixed, and we derive the corresponding Lévy--Khintchine representation, Volterra formulation, and scalar Cauchy problem. A distinctive feature of the resulting operators is the emergence of two independent asymptotic orders.

### [27] [A maximal Hohenberg-Kohn theorem for non-interacting systems via potential theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12852)
*Thiago Carvalho Corso*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了对于具有弱关联基态的薛定谔算符（Schrödinger operators），Hohenberg-Kohn 定理在形式有界外势（form-bounded external potentials）的最大类中成立当且仅当单粒子密度（single-particle density）在拟处处（quasi-everywhere）为正。进而为无相互作用系统和 Kohn-Sham 势的唯一性建立了该定理，并揭示了其核心机制是密度的（拟）唯一延拓性质而非多体波函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在在尽可能广泛的外势类中严格建立 Hohenberg-Kohn 定理的成立条件，并澄清其在连续体系中的基本机制。

Method: 利用弱关联正则态（weakly correlated regular states）的表征，其证明依赖于经典位势论（classical potential theory）。通过密度拟处处为正的条件与形式有界外势类的结合，建立了定理成立的充要条件。

Result: Hohenberg-Kohn 定理在形式有界外势的最大类中成立当且仅当单粒子密度拟处处为正；该条件对具有离散基态能量的无相互作用薛定谔算符的基态成立；从而建立了无相互作用系统的 Hohenberg-Kohn 定理及 Kohn-Sham 势的唯一性。

Conclusion: 在连续体系中，Hohenberg-Kohn 定理的根本机制是密度的（拟）唯一延拓（(quasi)-unique continuation）性质，而非多体波函数的唯一延拓。

Abstract: In this paper, we show that for Schrödinger operators with weakly correlated ground states, the Hohenberg-Kohn theorem holds within the maximal class of form-bounded external potentials if and only if the single-particle density is positive quasi-everywhere. Furthermore, we show that these conditions are satisfied for the ground state of non-interacting Schrödinger operators with a discrete ground state energy. Consequently, we establish the Hohenberg-Kohn theorem for non-interacting systems, and therefore the uniqueness of the Kohn-Sham potential, within the maximal class of Laplace form-bounded potentials. The key ingredient to establish these results is a characterization of weakly correlated regular states, whose proof relies on classical potential theory. Moreover, our proof reveals that, in the continuum setting, the fundamental mechanism underlying the Hohenberg-Kohn theorem is the (quasi)-unique continuation of the density rather than of the many-body wavefunction.

</details>


### [28] [Spending Operators and Weak Power-Port Decompositions for Path-Dependent Entropic Lagrangians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12860)
*Huilong Ren*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个路径依赖熵拉格朗日（Path-Dependent Entropic Lagrangian）框架，通过端点标定（endpoint calibration）与余循环可加性（cocycle additivity）唯一确定定向支出增量（oriented spending increment），并在Sobolev、有限能量分布（finite-energy distributional）和有界变差/散度测度（bounded-variation/divergence-measure）三种正则性下系统建立了弱扩散场中的空间功率分配（spatial power split）与通道终端变分（channelwise terminal variation）结构，最终整合为一个同步乘积空间上的增广热-扩散PDEL泛函，其允许的方向平稳性（admissible directional stationarity）导出了能量与热共轭、组分平衡、通量闭合、熵产生及两条终端功率路由通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 历史依赖熵（history-dependent entropic）公式需要为通道终端变分（channelwise terminal variation）和空间功率分配（spatial power split）提供精确含义，尤其是当扩散场较弱时该结构仍需保持有效。现有理论缺乏统一框架来系统处理这些要素。

Method: 通过端点标定与余循环可加性唯一确定定向支出增量；对分解的功率端口（power port）进行通道扩展以获取显式终端微分；在Sobolev、有限能量分布和有界变差/散度测度三种正则性下分别构建扩散分配（diffusion split）；利用自然对偶空间反例证明化学势加权残差不守恒，并用独立乘子恢复无加权平衡；将所有成分组装为一个同步乘积空间上的增广热-扩散PDEL泛函。

Result: 该泛函的允许方向平稳性产生了能量与热共轭（energetic and thermal conjugacy）、物种平衡（species balance）、通量闭合（flux closure）、熵产生（entropy production）以及两条终端功率路由通道。该构造还允许有限能量弱形式，并可特化为Cahn-Hilliard方程。

Conclusion: 所提出的路径依赖熵拉格朗日构造能够统一处理弱扩散场下的通道终端变分与空间功率分配，为历史依赖热力学扩散系统提供了一个自洽的变分框架，且具有向Cahn-Hilliard方程等具体模型特化的能力。

Abstract: History-dependent entropic formulations require a precise meaning for channelwise terminal variation and a spatial power split that remains valid for weak diffusion fields. This paper establishes both structures and places them in a single Path-Dependent Entropic Lagrangian construction. Endpoint calibration and cocycle additivity uniquely determine the oriented spending increment, while a channelwise extension of a decomposed power port yields explicit terminal differentials for scalar dissipation and potential-weighted fluxes. The diffusion split is formulated at Sobolev, finite-energy distributional, and bounded-variation/divergence-measure regularity. A natural-dual-space counterexample proves that chemical-potential-weighted residuals do not imply conservation, and an independent multiplier restores the unweighted balance. These ingredients are assembled in one augmented thermo-diffusion PDEL functional on a synchronized product space. Its admissible directional stationarity produces energetic and thermal conjugacy, species balance, flux closure, entropy production, and the two terminal power-routing channels. The same construction admits a finite-energy weak form and specializes to the Cahn--Hilliard equation.

</details>

### [29] [Analytical solution of the Eliashberg equations for strong-coupling superconductivity in hydrides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12213)
*Tomas J. Escamilla,Chumin Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文在戴拜模型（Debye model）框架下给出了各向同性埃利亚希伯格方程（Eliashberg equations）关于超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature）的解析解，该解在弱耦合与强耦合区域均与全自洽数值计算吻合，并在氢化物超导体（hydride superconductors）中预测的临界温度与从头算（ab initio）计算和实验数据呈现标度一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 富含氢材料在极端压力下实现室温超导的新发现，重新激发了人们对由埃利亚希伯格理论（Eliashberg theory）描述的声子介导配对机制的兴趣，该理论通过引入声子延迟效应（phonon retardation effects）推广了BCS框架。然而，埃利亚希伯格方程通常依赖于数值求解，本文旨在提供一种解析解以便更便捷、系统地分析超导临界温度。

Method: 在戴拜模型（Debye model）的设定下，对各向同性埃利亚希伯格方程（Eliashberg equations）进行解析求解，从而得到超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature）的表达式。随后将该解析解与全自洽数值计算结果、麦克米兰-艾伦-戴恩斯公式（McMillan-Allen-Dynes formula）以及实验数据进行比较验证。

Result: 解析解在弱耦合与强耦合区域均与全自洽数值计算结果吻合良好，正确重现了临界温度对电子-声子耦合参数（electron-phonon coupling parameter）的指数依赖和平方根依赖。应用于YH₆时，该解与实验及麦克米兰-艾伦-戴恩斯公式（McMillan-Allen-Dynes formula）的基准结果一致。在多种氢化物超导体（hydride superconductors）中，预测的临界温度与从头算（ab initio）计算和实验数据呈现标度一致性。

Conclusion: 所提出的埃利亚希伯格方程（Eliashberg equations）解析解在广泛耦合强度范围内有效，且对于氢化物超导体（hydride superconductors）的临界温度预测具有跨体系的标度一致性，表明该解析方法可作为研究声子介导超导的有效工具。

Abstract: The recent discovery of room-temperature superconductivity in hydrogen-rich materials under extreme pressures has renewed interest in phonon-mediated pairing mechanisms described by the Eliashberg theory, which generalizes the BCS framework by incorporating phonon retardation effects. In this article, we present an analytical solution to the isotropic Eliashberg equations for the superconducting critical temperature, formulated within the Debye model. This solution exhibits good agreement with fully selfconsistent numerical calculations across both weak- and strong-coupling regimes, correctly reproducing the exponential and square-root dependences on the electron-phonon coupling parameter. We further apply the solution to YH6, benchmarking against experiment and the McMillan-Allen-Dynes formula. More broadly, across a diverse set of hydride superconductors, the predicted critical temperature shows scaling consistency with ab initio calculations and experimental data.

</details>


### [30] [Systematic modulation of superconducting gap dynamics in YBCO|BNT|YBCO Josephson Junctions through THz field interaction and BNT ferroelectric barrier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12394)
*Sukhanidhan Singh,Muthukkumaran Karthikeyan,Geoffrey Chanda,Thanayut Kaewmaraya,Pairot Moontragoon,Guoxing Sun,Zongjin Li,Anucha Watcharapasorn*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究在YBa₂Cu₃O₇₋ₓ (YBCO)/Bi₀.₅Na₀.₅TiO₃ (BNT)/YBCO三层结中实现了稳健的约瑟夫森耦合，利用40 nm铁电BNT势垒层，并在太赫兹（THz）辐照下展示了增强的超导输运、明确的超流分支和标准的Fraunhofer干涉图样，证明BNT是一种适用于可调谐高温超导量子器件的势垒材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将铁电势垒集成到高温约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）中，为实现可调谐超导量子器件提供了一条潜在途径。当前研究旨在验证铁电BNT势垒能否在高温超导体系中支持本征的约瑟夫森耦合（Josephson coupling），并探索其在太赫兹辐照下的动态响应。

Method: 采用脉冲激光沉积（pulsed laser deposition）在SrTiO₃衬底上制备了YBCO/BNT/YBCO外延三层结，势垒为40 nm铁电BNT。通过宽带太赫兹辐照（0.5–2.5 THz）进行激发，利用扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy）、光学电导率测量、原子力显微镜（atomic force microscopy, AFM）和X射线反射率（X-ray reflectivity）等手段进行表征。

Result: 在1.5 THz（接近约瑟夫森等离子体共振频率）辐照下，BNT极化率在30 K时从33.4 µC/cm²增至46.4 µC/cm²；临界电流Ic(T)在60 K以下几乎保持恒定，并在1.5 THz激发下达到468.2 µA。YBCO/BNT/YBCO的超导能隙（Δ = 1.3 meV）大于纯YBCO（Δ = 1.05 meV），磁场的Ic(B)调制呈现典型的Fraunhofer干涉图样，电阻映射显示高低耗散交替的瓣状结构。

Conclusion: 约瑟夫森耦合是YBCO/BNT/YBCO结的本征特性，由BNT势垒的偶极特性和动态太赫兹响应所促成。BNT被确立为一种可行且可调谐的势垒材料，适用于下一代高温超导量子器件。

Abstract: The integration of ferroelectric barriers into high-temperature Josephson junctions offers a pathway to tunable superconducting quantum devices. Here, we demonstrate robust Josephson coupling in YBa2Cu3O7-x (YBCO)/Bi0.5Na0.5TiO3 (BNT)/YBCO trilayer junctions incorporating a 40 nm ferroelectric BNT barrier. Epitaxial trilayers were fabricated by pulsed laser deposition on SrTiO3 substrates and investigated under broadband terahertz (THz) irradiation (0.5-2.5 THz). At 1.5 THz, close to the Josephson plasma resonance, the BNT polarization increased from 33.4 to 46.4 uC/cm2 at 30 K, enhancing superconducting transport. The junctions exhibited a well-defined zero-voltage supercurrent branch, with the critical current Ic(T) remaining nearly constant up to 60 K and reaching 468.2 uA under 1.5 THz excitation, evidencing strong phase coherence. Scanning tunneling spectroscopy revealed an enhanced superconducting gap in YBCO/BNT/YBCO (Delta = 1.3 meV) compared with pure YBCO (Delta = 1.05 meV), while optical conductivity measurements showed a reduction in conductivity and gap with increasing temperature, consistent with BCS theory under THz excitation. Atomic force microscopy and X-ray reflectivity confirmed uniform morphology and sharp interfaces, excluding defect-mediated transport. Magnetic field modulation of Ic(B) exhibited a canonical Fraunhofer interference pattern, and resistance mapping revealed alternating lobes of high and low dissipation, indicating coherent Josephson tunneling. These results establish that Josephson coupling is intrinsic to the YBCO/BNT/YBCO junctions, enabled by the dipolar character and dynamic THz response of the BNT barrier. This study identifies BNT as a viable, tunable barrier material for next-generation high-Tc superconducting quantum devices.

</details>


### [31] [Pokrovsky--Talapov and Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless Phase Transitions in Bilayer Superconducting Films under an In-Plane Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12401)
*Yicheng Zhong,Yi Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文研究了面内磁场下约瑟夫森耦合双层超导薄膜的有限温相变，揭示了从零温到有限温下相对相位扇区（relative-phase sector）中由缺陷机制主导的两种不同熔化路径：Commensurate-Fulde-Ferrell（C/FF）态与Incommensurate-Bloch超导（IC/Bloch SC）态之间的Pokrovsky-Talapov（PT）转变线，以及由Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）型热熔化主导的涡旋通道切换行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解约瑟夫森耦合双层超导薄膜在面内磁场下的有限温相变行为，特别是层相位紧凑性（compactness）如何影响不同缺陷机制（soliton与vortex）的竞争与相图结构。

Method: 采用紧凑层相位模型（compact layer phases）描述约瑟夫森耦合双层超导薄膜，在面内磁场下分别分析零温与有限温情形。零温下分析相对相位扇区的PT型相变；有限温下识别两种不同的缺陷机制（PT孤子线和BKT熔化），并通过关联指数（correlation exponent）η=1/4刻画边界性质。

Result: 零温下相对相位扇区发生从Commensurate-Fulde-Ferrell（C/FF）态到Incommensurate-Bloch超导（IC/Bloch SC）态的PT型相变。有限温下，C-IC边界保持为PT孤子进入线，soliton密度呈ρ_sol ∝ (k_0 - k_0^c(T))^{1/2}的平方根onset；热熔化则属于BKT型，边界处关联指数η=1/4。涡旋通道在相图中切换：C/FF态中Josephson锁定制服基本层涡旋（elementary layer vortex），选择同涡旋性层对（same-vorticity layer-pair）BKT通道；IC/Bloch SC态的熔化则由基本层涡旋主导。

Conclusion: 有限温下紧凑层相位引入的两种缺陷机制导致了不同的相变行为：C-IC转变仍由PT型soliton进入描述，而熔化则由BKT型涡旋激发控制。涡旋通道的切换反映了Josephson耦合对不同超导态的调制作用，深化了对双层超导薄膜有限温相图的理解。

Abstract: We study finite-temperature phase transitions in a Josephson-coupled bilayer superconducting film with compact layer phases under an in-plane magnetic field. At zero temperature, where thermally excited layer vortices are absent, the relative-phase sector undergoes a Pokrovsky--Talapov (PT) commensurate--incommensurate (C--IC) transition from a commensurate Fulde--Ferrell (C/FF) state to an incommensurate Bloch superconducting (IC/Bloch SC) state. At finite temperature, compactness separates two distinct defect mechanisms. The C--IC boundary remains a PT soliton-entry line: interlayer Josephson vortex--antivortex-pair solitons enter with the square-root onset $ρ_{\rm sol}\propto [k_0-k_0^c(T)]^{1/2}$. Thermal melting is instead Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless (BKT)-like, with correlation exponent $η=1/4$ at the boundary, but the active vortex channel changes across the phase diagram. Josephson locking suppresses elementary layer vortices in the C/FF state and selects a same-vorticity layer-pair BKT channel, whereas elementary layer vortices control melting of the IC/Bloch SC state.

</details>


### [32] [Magnetothermopower and particle-hole symmetry in a cuprate strange metal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12442)
*Yu-Te Hsu,Matija Čulo,Thom Ottenbros,Yingkai Huang,Jake Ayres,Steffen Wiedmann,Mikhail I. Katsnelson,Nigel E. Hussey,Mikhail Titov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过测量过掺杂Bi2201单晶在高磁场下的磁热电功率，发现零场塞贝克系数可用玻尔兹曼输运理论描述，但磁场响应S(H)不符合该理论。实验数据表明存在两个不同粒子-空穴对称性的输运扇区：常规费米液体扇区和近粒子-空穴对称扇区，后者主导反常纵向磁输运。据此提出了费米液体岛嵌入补偿狄拉克液体的实空间模型，用于解释过掺杂铜氧化物中的奇异金属行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解过掺杂铜氧化物（overdoped cuprates）中奇异金属（strange metal）态的输运机制，特别是磁场下热电效应的反常行为与超导涨落（superconducting fluctuations）之间的关系。

Method: 对过掺杂(Bi,Pb)2(Sr,La)2CuO6+delta (Bi2201)单晶进行高达35 T磁场下的磁热电功率（magnetothermopower）测量，并结合已有的霍尔效应（Hall effect）和磁电阻（magnetoresistance）结果进行分析。

Result: 零场塞贝克系数S(T)符合玻尔兹曼输运理论，但磁场响应S(H)包含一个额外的贡献，其场强和温度依赖性与Tc以上短程超导序（short-range superconducting order）一致。数据揭示两个输运扇区：一个为常规粒子-空穴不对称的费米液体（Fermi-liquid, FL）扇区，另一个为近粒子-空穴对称的扇区。

Conclusion: 提出了一个实空间模型：不连通的费米液体岛嵌入一个由相位不相干的d波Bogoliubov准粒子组成的补偿狄拉克液体（compensated Dirac liquid）中。该模型统一了常规零场输运与反常磁热电功率及磁电阻现象，为理解过掺杂铜氧化物中的奇异金属性提供了具体框架。

Abstract: Here, we report magnetothermopower measurements on overdoped (Bi,Pb)2(Sr,La)2CuO6+delta (Bi2201) single crystals in magnetic fields up to 35 T. Whereas the temperature dependence of the zero-field Seebeck coefficient S(T) can be captured using Boltzmann transport theory, the field-dependent response S(H) cannot. Instead, the magnetothermopower contains a large additional contribution whose field and temperature dependence is consistent with the presence of short-range superconducting order well above Tc. Combined with earlier Hall and magnetoresistance results, these data imply that the overdoped cuprate strange metal contains two transport sectors with distinct particle-hole symmetry: a conventional particle-hole-asymmetric Fermi-liquid (FL) contribution governing the Hall effect and the zero-field thermopower, and a nearly particle-hole-symmetric sector dominating the anomalous longitudinal magnetotransport. We formulate a phenomenological real-space model in which disconnected FL islands are embedded in a compensated Dirac liquid of phase-incoherent d-wave Bogoliubov quasiparticles. This picture reconciles conventional zero-field transport with anomalous magnetothermopower and magnetoresistance and offers a concrete framework for thinking about strange metallicity in overdoped cuprates.

</details>

### [33] [Single-Shot High-Energy Muon and Particle Radiography with a Multi-GeV Laser-Wakefield-Accelerator-Driven Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12984)
*Kaixin Zhu,G. Jackson Williams,Roberto Versaci,Ela Rockafellow,Anna Cimmino,Jaron E. Shrock,Reed Hollinger,Gabriele M. Grittani,Jiří Šišma,Ari Sloss,Nikola Durand,Nischal Tripathi,Jay Jablonski,James King,Gerardo Palma,Zach Rautio,Bryan Sullivan,Shoujun Wang,Frederica Sorkin,Sina Zahedpour,Ping Zhang,Bo Miao,Andrew Yandow,Mayank Gupta,Scott W. Hancock,Scott C. Wilks,Vincent Tang,David Warner,Jorge J. Rocca,John Harton,Howard M. Milchberg,Brendan A. Reagan*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次展示了利用激光尾波加速器（laser-wakefield accelerator）产生的1–10 GeV的μ子、π介子和中子束流进行单发粒子射线照相（single-shot particle radiography）。实验在约15米距离外对穿过铅屏蔽、建筑墙壁和卡车的测试物体成像，并通过闪烁体探测器确认了μ子的存在。模拟表明透射束的高能成分几乎全部为μ子，单发注量（fluence）相当于在地平线附近积分超过8小时宇宙射线μ子。该工作确立了基于激光尾波加速器驱动源的单发高能粒子射线照相技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能粒子射线照相（如μ子成像）在探测厚重屏蔽体内部结构方面具有重要应用，但传统宇宙射线μ子成像需要较长的积分时间，而加速器产生的μ子源往往体积庞大、成本高昂。本文旨在利用激光尾波加速器产生的高能μ子、π介子和中子束流，实现单发（single-shot）快速成像，克服现有技术的时间限制。

Method: 实验采用激光尾波加速器（laser-wakefield accelerator）产生能量范围为1–10 GeV的束流，包含μ子（muons）、π介子（pions）和中子（neutrons）。测试物体放置在距离束流源约15米处，穿过致密铅屏蔽（lead shielding）、建筑墙壁和一辆卡车进行成像。使用大体积闪烁体探测器（scintillator-based detectors）记录粒子衰变事件，并通过时间延迟与μ子寿命（muon lifetime）的一致性来直接确认束流中的μ子成分。同时结合模拟分析透射束的高能成分。

Result: 实验成功实现了对测试物体的单发成像，穿过致密铅屏蔽、建筑墙壁和卡车后仍能获得有效图像。闪烁体探测器记录的衰变事件时间延迟与μ子寿命一致，直接证实了束流中μ子的存在。模拟结果显示，透射束的高能成分几乎完全由μ子组成，体现了其高穿透性（highly penetrative nature）。单发注量相当于在地平线附近积分超过8小时宇宙射线μ子的注量。

Conclusion: 该工作首次证明了基于激光尾波加速器驱动源的单发高能粒子射线照相技术的可行性，为快速穿透厚重屏蔽体进行成像提供了新途径。激光尾波加速器产生的μ子束流在单发条件下即可达到传统宇宙射线μ子成像数小时的积分效果，有望在核安全、材料检测及国防等领域发挥重要作用。

Abstract: We report the first demonstration of single-shot particle radiography using a 1-10 GeV laser-wakefield-generated beam of muons, pions, and neutrons. The test objects were imaged ~15 m from the beam source, through dense lead shielding followed by the walls of a building and a truck. The muon content of the beam was directly confirmed using large volume scintillator-based detectors, which recorded particle decay events with timing delays consistent with the muon lifetime. Simulations confirm that the high energy component of the beam transmitted through the test object is nearly entirely composed of muons, directly showing their highly penetrative nature, with a single-shot fluence equivalent to >8 hours of integration of cosmic ray muons near the horizon. Our work establishes single-shot high-energy particle radiography with a laser-wakefield-accelerator-driven source.

### [34] [A critical consideration of X-ray detectors based on Ga2O3: excitation, carrier transport mechanisms and performance standardization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12638)
*Alfred Moore,Daniel A Lamb,Lijie Li,Oliver Fox,Kawal Sawhney,Ciaran Llewelyn,Jon E Evans,Saqib Rafique,Tiantian Chai,John Harrington,Zabeada Aslam,Andrew P Brown,Rik Drummond-Brydson,Yaonan Hou*

TL;DR: 本文针对Ga₂O₃基X射线探测器在器件工作机制和性能基准测试方面存在的问题，利用可调能量单色同步辐射X射线束对β-Ga₂O₃:Si肖特基探测器进行了系统研究，阐明了载流子激发和输运机制，并提出了正确的性能测量与分析协议。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究基于外延生长的β-Ga₂O₃:Si材料制备了平面肖特基探测器，利用同步辐射束线（synchrotron beamline）上的能量可调单色X射线束（energy-tuneable monochromatic X-ray beams）进行测量，以澄清器件激发与载流子输运机制，并正确基准化器件性能。

Result: 阐明了β-Ga₂O₃:Si肖特基探测器的激发和载流子输运机制，并获得了经过正确基准测试的器件性能指标。

Abstract: X-ray detection underpins a wide range of applications in medicine, security, industrial inspection, scientific research for non-destructive imaging and material analysis. The rapid development of Ga2O3-based X-ray detectors offers a promising pathway toward next-generation detectors with high sensitivity, low noise, and harsh environment applications, benefiting from its intrinsic material properties such as high density, wide band gap energy, and high thermal-chemical stability. However, the underlying device operating mechanisms, including both carrier excitation and transport processes, have not yet been adequately studied, largely due to the misuse of X-ray sources in previous studies. Besides, benchmarking of device characteristics has been problematic due to experimental or data analysis issues, as well as misunderstandings of the applied equations associated with parameter definitions. In this work, we have designed and performed an instructive research work based on epitaxial beta-Ga2O3:Si and its planar Schottky detectors, measured with energy-tuneable monochromatic X-ray beams on a synchrotron beamline, clarifying the device excitation and carrier transport mechanisms with properly benchmarked device performance. In the end, we propose a set of protocols for correctly measuring and analysing the device performance. The proposed protocols are broadly applicable and can be readily extended to other semiconductor X-ray detectors.

### [35] [Influence of compaction pressure on the impedance of Gadolinium Doped Ceria electrolytes for IT-SOFCs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12719)
*Renato A. N. de Oliveira,Celeste Z. A. Aquino,Magna Monteiro Schaerer,Rafael Galiza Yoshimura,Liliana Mogni,Maurico Arce,Diego G.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在49至140 MPa范围内系统变化等静压压实压力（isostatic compaction pressure）制备致密GDC陶瓷片，经1350°C保温四小时相同热条件烧结；采用电子束蒸镀法沉积铂电极，并利用电化学阻抗谱（EIS）在宽温域内表征电学性能。

Conclusion: 压实压力通过调控微观结构影响GDC多晶电解质的宏观电导行为，这为优化IT-SOFC电解质制备工艺提供了依据。

Abstract: Gadolinium doped ceria (GDC) is one promising oxygen-ion conducting ceramic electrolyte for intermediate-temperature solid oxide fuel cells (IT-SOFCs), due to its high ionic conductivity at reduced operating temperatures, favorable defect chemistry, and compatibility with a broad range of electrode materials [1,2]. Despite extensive understanding of its intrinsic ion transport mechanisms, the influence of ceramic processing parameters on the effective electrical behavior of polycrystalline GDC electrolytes remains an active topic for investigation [3-5]. In particular, processing steps that govern green body formation and sintering can strongly affect microstructural features such as density, grain size, grain boundary character, and residual porosity, which in turn determine the macroscopic conductivity [4-6]. In this work, dense GDC ceramic pellets were fabricated under systematically varied isostatic compaction pressures ranging from 49 to 140 MPa, followed by sintering at 1350 C for four hours under identical thermal conditions. Platinum electrodes were deposited on both sides of the pellets by electron-beam deposition, and the electrical properties were characterized by electrochemical impedance spectroscopy (EIS) over a wide temperature range. The results demonstrate a dependence of the impedance with respect to compaction pressure.
