### [36] [The Limitations of Cosmological Collider Analyses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12010)
*Oliver H. E. Philcox*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过结合CosmoFlow数值预测与Planck双谱重建数据，系统评估了标量宇宙学对撞机（scalar cosmological collider）的观测可行性。研究发现：在弱混合（weak mixing）近似下，除低质量区间的双交换和三交换构型外，对撞机信号因微扰性（perturbativity）限制而无法被观测到；增大混合至非微扰（non-perturbative）但幺正（unitary）的值虽可产生更大双谱，但会扭曲信号并破坏因式分解（factorization）。作者认为，强混合（strong mixing）分析是从当前和未来数据中获得有意义约束的必要途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学对撞机特征（cosmological collider features）的结构虽由暴胀对称性（symmetries of inflation）决定，但其振幅先验未知，仅受幺正性（unitarity）等物理原理限制。本文旨在评估标量宇宙学对撞机信号的观测可行性。

Method: 采用CosmoFlow生成精确数值预测，并结合Planck双谱重建（bispectrum reconstruction）的观测数据。在Goldstone标量与标量扇区之间的弱二次混合（weak quadratic mixing）极限下进行分析，并进一步扩展到非微扰（non-perturbative）但保持幺正（unitary）的混合值。

Result: 弱混合极限下，微扰性限制使得除低质量区间内双交换和三交换构型外，其余对撞机信号不可观测。增大混合至非微扰值虽可产生更大双谱，但会阻尼信号振幅并平移对撞机振荡（collider oscillations），同时破坏双谱因式分解为自由振幅与固定形状的结构。

Conclusion: 强混合分析虽面临理论预测与观测搜索的困难，却是从当前和未来数据中获取对标量宇宙学对撞机有意义的约束条件所必需的。

Abstract: Massive fields exchanged during inflation source cosmological collider features in the correlators of primordial curvature fluctuations. While their structure is fixed by the symmetries of inflation, the amplitude of such signatures is a priori unknown, though bounded by physical principles such as unitarity. We assess the observational viability of the scalar cosmological collider by combining precise numerical predictions derived using CosmoFlow with observational data from Planck bispectrum reconstructions. Working in the limit of weak quadratic mixing between the Goldstone and scalar sectors (as assumed by all previous searches), we find that perturbativity restricts the collider signals to be unobservably small, except for double- and triple-exchange configurations at low masses. Larger bispectra can be generated by increasing the mixing to non-perturbative (but still unitary) values: however, this distorts the signal, damping its amplitude and shifting the collider oscillations. Furthermore, strong mixing breaks the factorization of the bispectrum into a free amplitude and a fixed shape, and complicates both theoretical predictions and observational searches. Despite the challenges, we argue that strong mixing analyses are necessary to obtain meaningful constraints on the scalar cosmological collider from current and upcoming datasets.

</details>


### [37] [Solar System Probes for Scalar Field Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12144)
*Edmund Ghampson,Oem Trivedi,Robert J. Scherrer,Alfredo Gurrola*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文针对标量场暗物质（scalar field dark matter）模型，发展了三种太阳系及本地银河系尺度的探测手段：柯伊伯带天体（KBO）遭遇标量团块时产生的ADAF-like耀斑、原子钟对基本常数振荡变化的搜索、以及致密标量团块的微引力透镜效应。研究给出了灵敏度估计和零探测界限，表明Gaia级天体测量可探测质量约在10⁻²太阳质量以上的致密标量团块，未来实验可进一步扩展至更低质量和更弱耦合区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标量场暗物质（scalar field dark matter）是传统粒子暗物质的一个有力替代方案，尤其是在超轻场（ultralight fields）形成相干振荡或致密自引力团块时。当前尚缺乏对这些模型在太阳系和本地银河系尺度上的系统性探测研究。

Method: 发展了三种互补的探测方法：(1) 利用标量团块与柯伊伯带天体（Kuiper Belt Objects）相遇时产生的ADAF-like耀斑；(2) 通过原子钟（atomic clock）搜索基本常数的振荡变化；(3) 利用天体测量微引力透镜（astrometric microlensing）效应探测致密标量团块。基于上述方法推导了简单的灵敏度估计和零探测界限。

Result: 给出了标量团块占比、时钟耦合参数以及致密透镜丰度等方面的零探测界限。Gaia级天体测量可探测质量约在10⁻²太阳质量（M_⊙）以上的致密标量团块，灵敏度达到百分量级；未来天体测量和原子钟实验可将探测范围扩展至更低质量和更弱耦合区域。

Conclusion: 所提出的三种太阳系及本地银河系探测探针具有互补性，能够对标量场暗物质模型提供有效的约束；未来实验有望显著提升探测能力，覆盖当前手段尚无法触及的参数空间。

Abstract: Scalar field dark matter provides us with a well motivated alternative to conventional particle dark matter, especially when ultralight fields form coherent oscillations or compact self gravitating clumps. Here we develop three complementary Solar System and local Galactic level probes of such models. These probes pertain to ADAF-like flares from scalar clump encounters with Kuiper Belt Objects, atomic clock searches for oscillatory variations of fundamental constants and astrometric microlensing by compact scalar clumps. We derive simple sensitivity estimates and null detection bounds on the scalar clump fraction, clock couplings and compact lens abundance. Our results show that Gaia-like astrometry can probe compact scalar clumps at the percent level near $M_s\gtrsim10^{-2}M_\odot$, while future astrometric and clock experiments can extend the reach to lower masses and weaker couplings.

</details>


### [38] [Testing the Direction of Dark Sector Interaction Using Late-Time Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12283)
*Anil Kandel,Phongpichit Channuie,Ertan Güdekli,Farruh Atamurotov*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用DESI DR1/DR2的重子声学振荡测量、宇宙计时器测量、压缩CMB似然以及三种Ia型超新星数据集（Pantheon⁺、DES-Dovekie、Union3），对唯象相互作用暗能量ξIDE模型进行参数约束。分析表明，ξIDE模型虽略提高哈勃常数并部分缓解哈勃张力，但ξ参数接近ΛCDM预测值，暗能量状态方程参数w_X倾向于大于−1（类精质场行为），而相互作用参数组合ξ+3w_X为负值，对应暗能量向暗物质的能量转移，但当前数据仅给出弱于1.52σ的相互作用信号；贝叶斯证据始终倾向于ΛCDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验唯象相互作用暗能量（ξIDE）模型是否能在多种观测数据联合约束下优于标准ΛCDM模型，并评估其对哈勃张力（Hubble tension）的缓解程度及暗区相互作用的统计显著性。

Method: 采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）分析，通过dynesty包中的嵌套采样（nested sampling）算法结合宇宙学推断代码SimpleMC进行参数约束。数据集包括DESI DR1/DR2的重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation, BAO）测量、宇宙计时器（cosmic chronometer, CC）测量、压缩CMB似然以及Pantheon⁺、DES-Dovekie和Union3三种Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernova）编译。

Result: 与ΛCDM相比，ξIDE模型预测略高的哈勃常数，部分缓解哈勃张力但未完全消除；耦合参数ξ始终约束在ΛCDM预测值附近，无统计显著偏离；除CMB+DESI DR1+CC组合外，暗能量状态方程参数w_X偏好大于−1，显示类精质场（quintessence-like）行为；相互作用参数组合ξ+3w_X在所有数据集组合中均为负值（暗能量→暗物质能量转移），最强偏好来自CMB+DESI DR2+CC+Union3组合，结果为ξ+3w_X=−0.035±0.023，仅偏离非相互作用极限1.52σ。

Conclusion: 当前观测数据仅提供微弱的暗区相互作用指示；基于Nσ统计量的模型比较显示对相互作用情景的支持较弱，而贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence）始终更倾向于ΛCDM模型。

Abstract: In this work, we constrain the phenomenological interacting dark energy $ξ$IDE model using baryon acoustic oscillation measurements from DESI Data Release 1 and Data Release 2, combined with cosmic chronometer measurements, compressed CMB likelihoods, and three different Type Ia supernova compilations: Pantheon$^+$, DES-Dovekie, and Union3. We constrain the parameters of the $ξ$IDE model using a Markov Chain Monte Carlo analysis, using the nested sampling algorithm implemented in the \texttt{dynesty} package through the cosmological inference code \texttt{SimpleMC}. Compared to $Λ$CDM, the $ξ$IDE model favors slightly higher values of the Hubble constant, leading to a reduction in the Hubble tension. However, the tension is not completely resolved for any dataset combination. The parameter $ξ$ is consistently constrained to values close to its $Λ$CDM prediction, indicating no statistically significant deviation from the standard cosmological scenario. Similarly, except for the CMB + DESI DR1 + CC dataset combination, the dark energy equation-of-state parameter prefers values of $w_{\rm X}>-1$, showing a preference for quintessence-like behavior and providing evidence for dynamical dark energy. The interaction parameter combination, $ξ+3w_{\rm X}$, is found to be negative for all dataset combinations, corresponding to energy transfer from dark energy to dark matter. The strongest preference is obtained for the CMB + DESI DR2 + CC + Union3 dataset combination, yielding $ξ+3w_{\rm X}=-0.035\pm0.023$, which corresponds to a deviation of only $1.52σ$ from the non-interacting limit. Therefore, the current data provide only a weak indication of a non-zero dark-sector interaction. Model comparison based on the $Nσ$ statistic shows weak evidence in favor of the interacting scenario, while Bayesian evidence consistently prefers the $Λ$CDM model.

</details>


### [39] [Exploring Hu-Sawicki-like modified gravity with Genetic Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12745)
*Chiara De Leo,Elisa Fazzari,Matteo Martinelli,Savvas Nesseris*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文采用基于遗传算法（GA）的机器学习方法，围绕Hu-Sawicki类f(R)引力模型重构解析微扰，并利用DESI DR2重子声学振荡（BAO）数据和Pantheon+ Ia型超新星样本进行背景宇宙学检验。结果表明，在当前背景数据约束下，该类模型仅允许与ΛCDM存在极为有限的偏差，晚期宇宙中修正引力效应虽略有增强，但被有效抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Hu-Sawicki类f(R)引力模型能否在与ΛCDM模型存在可观测偏差的同时，通过当前背景宇宙学数据的检验，从而检验修正引力理论在宇宙学尺度上的可行性。

Method: 采用基于遗传算法（Genetic Algorithms, GA）的机器学习方法，将\texttt{GATO} GA代码与\texttt{CANDI}宇宙学代码接口化。GA生成的每个f(R)函数先通过理论可行性条件检验（包括稳定性、标准物质主导时期恢复、广义相对论极限和变色龙屏蔽机制（chameleon screening mechanism）），再经由\texttt{CANDI}重构背景宇宙学，并与DESI DR2 BAO数据和Pantheon+ Ia型超新星样本进行对比。

Result: 偏差在晚期宇宙最大（此时低曲率使修正引力效应更显著），在高红移处迅速被抑制。Om(z)诊断显示仅与恒定ΛCDM行为存在极微小偏离。重构f(R)函数对应的有效暗能量态方程（equation of state）演化微弱，呈现从类quintessence到类phantom（phantom-like）的轻度转变。

Conclusion: 在Hu-Sawicki类模型的微扰框架下，当前背景宇宙学数据仅允许与ΛCDM存在极为有限的偏差，该类模型难以产生足够大的可观测信号以区别于标准宇宙学模型。

Abstract: We investigate whether viable Hu-Sawicki-like $f(R)$ models can produce deviations from $Λ\mathrm{CDM}$ that can be tested against current background cosmological data. We adopt a machine-learning approach based on Genetic Algorithms (GA) to reconstruct analytical perturbations around the Hu-Sawicki class of models. We develop a pipeline that interfaces the \texttt{GATO} GA code with the \texttt{CANDI} cosmology code. Each $f(R)$ function generated by the GA is first tested against theoretical viability conditions, including stability, the recovery of a standard matter-dominated epoch, the General Relativity limit, and chameleon screening mechanism. Viable candidates are then passed to \texttt{CANDI} to reconstruct the corresponding background cosmology and are tested against DESI DR2 BAO measurements and the Pantheon+ Type Ia supernova catalogue. %\newline The deviations we find are largest at late times, where the lower curvature makes modified-gravity effects more relevant, and are rapidly suppressed at higher redshift, in agreement with the imposed matching to the matter-dominated era. To further quantify deviations from the standard cosmological model, we compute the $Om(z)$ diagnostic. It shows only a very small departure from the constant $Λ\mathrm{CDM}$ behaviour. The effective dark energy equation of state associated with the reconstructed $f(R)$ function also evolves only weakly, showing a mild transition from an effective quintessence-like nature to an effective phantom-like regime. Overall, our results indicate that, within perturbations around the Hu-Sawicki class of models, current background data allow only limited deviations from $Λ\mathrm{CDM}$.

### [40] [Models with Non-minimal Coupling in Primordial Universe and Cosmological Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12974)
*Alireza Talebian,Hassan Firouzjahi,Fereshteh Felegary*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了暴胀场与引力之间的非最小耦合（non-minimal coupling）模型，在Jordan框架中分析标量谱指数（spectral index）$n_s$与张量标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）$r$的观测预言。针对单项式势（monomial potential）$V(φ) \propto φ^n$，发现负耦合常数$ξ$系统性压低$r$，且四次模型$V(φ) = λφ^4/4$在$ξ\lesssim -0.1$时与ACT DR6数据高度一致，表明非最小耦合可有效调和Planck与ACT的观测结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暴胀场与引力之间的非最小耦合是暴胀宇宙学中的一般性贡献（generic contribution），但其在Jordan框架中的动力学细节以及观测预言尚未被充分研究。本文旨在系统考察非最小耦合对$n_s$和$r$的影响。

Method: 在Jordan框架中直接分析动力学，而非传统的Einstein框架变换。关注势能（potential force）与耦合诱导的摩擦（coupling-induced friction）之间的竞争，研究系统在扩展的常数-滚（constant-roll）阶段中的行为，并以单项式势$V(φ) \propto φ^n$为例进行参数扫描。

Result: 负$ξ$系统性压低$r$；$n_s$的偏移依赖于幂次$n$：$n \geq 4$时$n_s$随$|ξ|$增大，$n < 4$时$n_s$减小。四次模型$V(φ) = λφ^4/4$在$ξ\lesssim -0.1$时与ACT DR6数据吻合良好，且其$n_s(ξ)$依赖关系与其他单项式情形明显不同。

Conclusion: 非最小耦合模型能够有效调和Planck与ACT的观测结果，为解释当前的宇宙微波背景（CMB）观测约束提供了一个统一的框架。

Abstract: A non-minimal coupling between gravity and the inflaton field is a generic contribution in inflationary cosmology. In this work, we consider models of inflation with a non-minimal coupling $-ξφ^2 R$ and study their observational predictions for the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ and the spectral index $n_s$. Unlike the conventional approach of working in the Einstein frame, we perform the analysis in the Jordan frame where the underlying dynamics, particularly the competition between the potential force and the coupling-induced friction, are more transparent. For suitable values of $ξ$, the system exhibits an extended constant-roll regime, in which this friction counteracts the potential force. Focusing on monomial potentials $V(φ) \propto φ^n$, we find that negative $ξ$ systematically reduces $r$ in the $(n_s, r)$ plane, while the shift in $n_s$ depends on the power $n$: for $n \geq 4$, the spectral index increases with $|ξ|$, whereas for $n < 4$, it decreases. Notably, the quartic model $V(φ) = λφ^4/4$ with $ξ\lesssim -0.1$ shows good agreement with the ACT DR6 data and exhibits a distinct $n_s(ξ)$ dependence compared to other monomial cases. Our results demonstrate that non-minimally coupled models can effectively reconcile Planck and ACT observations, providing a unified framework for interpreting current CMB constraints.

</details>


### [41] [Model-Independent Indication for a Localized Anomaly in the Late-Time Expansion History](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13009)
*Shibendu Gupta Choudhury,Purba Mukherjee,Eleonora Di Valentino,Anjan A Sen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究利用模型无关的样条重构方法，基于DESI DR2重子声学振荡数据和DES Dovekie Ia型超新星数据重建宇宙晚期膨胀历史，发现红移区间0.3≲z≲0.6处存在与Planck 2018 ΛCDM模型的局域偏差，最大显著度约3.5σ（z≃0.47）。该特征在多种重构方法、数据集组合及声视界校准下保持稳健，且模拟分析表明其非重构偏差所致。若经未来观测确认，该局域特征可能指向未认识的晚期宇宙新物理或早期与晚期宇宙探测之间的微妙不一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索宇宙晚期膨胀历史是否存在偏离标准ΛCDM模型（Lambda Cold Dark Matter model）预测的结构，尤其是在红移（redshift）区间0.3≲z≲0.6内可能存在的局域偏差。

Method: 采用模型无关的样条重构（spline reconstruction）方法重建宇宙学距离，基于最新的DESI DR2重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation, BAO）测量数据和DES Dovekie Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernova）汇编数据。通过改变重构方法、数据集组成和声视界（sound-horizon）校准进行稳健性检验，并辅以模拟（mock）分析评估重构偏差。

Result: 在红移区间0.3≲z≲0.6内识别出一个局域性偏离，最大显著度约3.5σ，峰值位于z≃0.47。该特征在多种方法学和数据集变化下持续存在，且模拟分析显示重构无偏、异常非来源于重构偏差或不确定性误校准。

Conclusion: 该局域特征若经未来观测确认，可能指向未被认识的晚期宇宙新物理（late-time physics），或揭示早期与晚期宇宙宇宙学探测（cosmological probes）之间的微妙不一致。

Abstract: We investigate the late-time expansion history of the Universe using a model-independent spline reconstruction of cosmological distances based on the latest DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) measurements and the DES Dovekie Type Ia supernova compilation. Comparing the reconstructed expansion history with the prediction of the Planck 2018 $Λ$CDM model, we identify a localized deviation over the redshift interval $0.3\lesssim z\lesssim0.6$, reaching a maximum significance of approximately $3.5σ$ at $z\simeq0.47$. We demonstrate that this feature persists under substantial variations of the reconstruction methodology, dataset composition and sound-horizon calibration. Mock analyses further show that the reconstruction is unbiased and that the observed anomaly is unlikely to arise from reconstruction bias or miscalibrated uncertainties. If confirmed by future observations, this localized feature could point to previously unrecognized late-time physics or reveal subtle inconsistencies between early and late Universe cosmological probes.

### [42] [Interpreting the Newly Observed $Ξ(1720)$ State in the Spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ $Ξ$ Spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12712)
*K. Azizi,Y. Sarac,H. Sundu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用两点QCD求和规则（two point QCD sum rule）对低能自旋-3/2 Ξ重子谱进行了分析，计算了1S、1P、2S和2P组态的质量，其中2S组态的质量（1727.52 ± 42.39 MeV）与BESIII实验观测到的Ξ(1720)共振质量在误差范围内一致，支持将该共振态归类为Ξ重子的首个径向自旋-3/2激发态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BESIII合作组报告了Ξ(1720)共振态的观测结果，其质量约为1721 MeV，并具有偏好的量子数J^P = 3/2^+。该实验发现促使作者利用QCD求和规则方法对低能自旋-3/2 Ξ重子谱进行理论分析，以确定该共振态的理论归属。

Method: 采用两点QCD求和规则（two point QCD sum rule）方法，对低能自旋-3/2 Ξ重子谱进行了分析。研究考虑了四种可能的低能级组态：1S、1P、2S和2P，分别对应基态、第一轨道激发、第一径向激发和第二轨道激发。

Result: 计算得到四个组态的质量分别为：1S态1527.53 ± 111.38 MeV，1P态1615.30 ± 50.98 MeV，2S态1727.52 ± 42.39 MeV，2P态1803.71 ± 64.50 MeV。其中2S态的质量与BESIII实验值（1721.0 ± 5.2_stat. ± 3.4_syst. MeV）在误差范围内一致。

Conclusion: 理论分析支持将Ξ(1720)共振态归为Ξ重子的首个径向自旋-3/2激发态（即2S组态）。该结论为BESIII实验发现提供了理论支持，并增进了对Ξ重子谱结构的理解。

Abstract: We analyze the low lying spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ $Ξ$ spectrum by means of the two point QCD sum rule approach. The analysis is motivated by the BESIII observation of the $Ξ(1720)$ resonance, reported with mass $1721.0\pm5.2_{\mathrm{stat.}}\pm3.4_{\mathrm{syst.}}~\mathrm{MeV}$ and favored quantum numbers $J^P=\frac{3}{2}^{+}$. In this framework, we include the $1S$, $1P$, $2S$ and $2P$ configurations as possible low lying spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ cascade states. The extracted masses are $1527.53\pm111.38~\mathrm{MeV}$, $1615.30\pm50.98~\mathrm{MeV}$, $1727.52\pm42.39~\mathrm{MeV}$ and $1803.71\pm64.50~\mathrm{MeV}$ for the $1S$, $1P$, $2S$ and $2P$ states, respectively. The mass obtained for the $2S$ configuration agrees with the BESIII value within uncertainties and favors the assignment of $Ξ(1720)$ as the first radial spin-$\frac{3}{2}$ excitation of the $Ξ$ baryon.

### [43] [Naturally quality-safe GeV axion with charm coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12956)
*Bo-Qiang Lu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种GeV标度QCD轴子（axion）模型，通过将Peccei-Quinn（PQ）标量耦合到粲夸克（charm quark）来解决结构同位旋问题（structural isospin problem），使轴子质量窗口位于$m_φ\sim 3$–4 MeV范围，并满足所有实验、天体物理和宇宙学约束，同时预测了可被CMB-S4和Belle II检验的独特信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GeV标度的QCD轴子面临一个结构同位旋问题：PQ标量（Peccei-Quinn scalar）与轻夸克（$u,d,s$）的耦合会破坏$\mathrm{SU}(2)$同位旋对称性，产生不可接受的$\pi^0$–$\pi^\pm$质量分裂（约15%），因此需要解决这一理论不一致性。

Method: 将PQ标量耦合到粲夸克（charm quark）而非轻夸克，从而完全消除同位旋破坏；通过将标量质量$m_φ$降低到3–4 MeV，使粲夸克汤川耦合（charm Yukawa coupling）$\kappa_c\propto m_φ$进入微扰区域（$\kappa_c<1$）。

Result: 模型得到的衰变常数$f_a\sim\text{GeV}\ll M_{\rm Pl}$可解决轴子品质问题（axion quality problem）：即使是最低维度（$d=6$）的普朗克压低的算符，也仅给出$m_{\rm PQ}/m_a\sim 10^{-14}$，无需额外对称性。模型预测$m_φ\sim 3$ MeV时出现独特的负有效中微子代数（negative $ΔN_{\rm eff}\sim -0.1$），可通过CMB-S4检验；$B\to Kσ$企鹅图（penguin）的分支比约为$2\times 10^{-5}$，与Belle II报告的$B^+\to K^+ν\barν$信号（$2.3\pm0.7)\times 10^{-5}$一致。

Conclusion: 在$m_φ\sim 3$–4 MeV的可行窗口内，该模型满足所有十类实验、天体物理和宇宙学约束；$B_s$混合约束有待专用格点计算（lattice calculation）进一步确认。

Abstract: The GeV-scale QCD axion -- where Peccei-Quinn (PQ) symmetry is broken by the QCD condensate at $f_a\sim\mathcal{O}(1)$~GeV -- faces a structural isospin problem: the PQ spurion coupling to light quarks ($u,d,s$) breaks $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ isospin, generating an unacceptable $\sim 15\%$ $π^0$--$π^\pm$ mass splitting. We show that coupling the PQ scalar to the charm quark instead eliminates this violation entirely, and lowering $m_φ\sim 3$--$4$~MeV makes the charm Yukawa $κ_c\propto m_φ$ perturbative ($κ_c<1$). The resulting $f_a\sim\text{GeV}\ll M_{\rm Pl}$ solves the axion quality problem: even the lowest-dimension $d=6$ Planck-suppressed operator gives $m_{\rm PQ}/m_a\sim 10^{-14}$, without any additional symmetry. The model predicts a distinctive {\it negative} $ΔN_{\rm eff}\sim -0.1$ for $m_φ\sim 3$~MeV, testable by CMB-S4. The $B\to Kσ$ penguin predicts $\mathrm{BR}\sim 2\times 10^{-5}$, consistent with the Belle~II evidence for $B^+\to K^+ν\barν$ at $(2.3\pm0.7)\times 10^{-5}$~\cite{BelleII:2024knv}. All ten classes of experimental, astrophysical, and cosmological constraints are satisfied in the viable window $m_φ\sim 3$--$4$~MeV, with the $B_s$ mixing constraint pending a dedicated lattice calculation.

</details>


### [44] [Stochastic Tsunamis: Diffuse Scalar Background from Black Hole Formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12013)
*Arturo de Giorgi,Joerg Jaeckel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的机制：大质量天体在形成黑洞（black hole）时，其周围静态标量场（scalar field）配置会突然失去源，以爆发形式向外传播形成“标量海啸（scalar tsunami）”，这些爆发在宇宙历史中累积产生一个遗存随机弥散标量背景（stochastic diffuse scalar background），其频谱峰值位于1-10³ Hz范围。该机制将实验对标量质量（scalar mass）的敏感度扩展至m_φ ≲ 10⁻¹³ eV，比此前考虑的单次瞬变事件提高了十个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的研究关注大质量天体周围标量场的静态配置，但未曾系统探讨天体坍缩成黑洞时静态配置突然释放所导致的累积效应。本文旨在提出并量化这类事件在宇宙历史中形成的弥散标量背景，并评估其对未来实验的探测潜力。

Method: 作者提出“标量海啸”这一新机制，基于大质量天体（如通过核心坍缩超新星形成黑洞的天体）其周围标量场静态构型在源消失后变为动力学爆发这一物理过程，计算了此类爆发的累积谱，并将其与未来实验的灵敏度进行比较。

Result: 计算得到该遗存随机弥散标量背景的频谱峰值位于1-10³ Hz频段；该机制将实验对标量质量m_φ的敏感度扩展至≲ 10⁻¹³ eV，比此前通过单个瞬变事件（individual transient events）所能达到的敏感度提高了约十个数量级。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种产生弥散标量背景的新机制，并显著扩展了未来实验对极轻标量场的探测能力，为寻找超轻标量粒子（ultralight scalar particles）提供了新的途径。

Abstract: Massive astrophysical objects can source huge static configurations of a scalar field. When such an object ends up forming a black hole, for instance, via a core-collapse supernova, the scalar field loses its source abruptly; then the static configuration becomes dynamical and propagates away in a burst, a "scalar tsunami". These bursts accumulate over cosmological history, forming a relic stochastic diffuse scalar background peaked in the $1-10^3~\text{Hz}$ range. We propose this as a novel mechanism for the generation of such a background, compute its spectrum, and compare it with the sensitivity of future experiments. We show how this extends the experimental sensitivity to scalar masses $m_φ\lesssim 10^{-13}~\text{eV}$, ten orders of magnitude larger than those accessible via individual transient events previously considered.

</details>


### [45] [An anomaly-free baryonic completion of the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12009)
*Karim Benakli,Mark Goodsell,Arno Goudeau*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个规范重子数对称性（gauged baryon-number symmetry）的无反常完备化（anomaly-free completion），引入扩展重子对称性 \(U(1)_{\tilde B}\)，结合隐伏区（secluded sector）与多种约束条件（如对称性破缺、暗物质候选者、耦合常数统一等）确定模型结构，并通过数值工具扫描到包含重子 \(Z'\) 玻色子、轻赝标量粒子及中性暗物质候选者的可行参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model）中重子数（baryon number）是偶然对称性（accidental symmetry），但其可被规范化为一个全局对称性，然而直接规范重子数会导致反常（anomaly）无法消除。因此，本文旨在构造一个无反常的规范重子数对称性完备化方案，并进一步探索该模型在满足多种物理约束条件下的可行结构。

Method: 作者将标准模型场上的重子数电荷扩展为 \(U(1)_{\tilde B}\)，引入一个隐伏区（secluded sector）以承载反常抵消所需的额外费米子。通过要求反常抵消、对称性自发破缺、奇异态合理衰变、无稳定彩色残留、受 \(Z_2^{\rm DM}\) 宇称保护的中性暗物质候选者以及改善的高能标规范耦合统一（gauge-coupling unification），逐步收紧模型结构。最终利用 SARAH 生成可重整化模型，并借助 SPheno、MicrOMEGAs、SModelS 和 HiggsTools 等工具进行能谱与唯象学分析。

Result: 研究识别出可行的参数空间区域，其中包含：一个重的重子 \(Z'\) 玻色子、一个更重的隐伏区、一个满足 relic 密度与直接探测限制的中性暗物质候选者，以及相较于标准模型有所改善的规范耦合演化。暗物质 relic 丰度由与邻近隐伏态的共同湮灭（co-annihilation）或湮灭为扩展标量区中的轻赝标量粒子（light pseudoscalar）来决定。

Conclusion: 仅凭反常抵消可允许一大类解，但结合对称性破缺、奇异态衰变、彩色残留避免、暗物质约束与规范耦合统一等要求后，模型结构被严格限制。最终构造的模型需通过额外标量场和 Yukawa 相互作用扩展最小隐伏费米子区，并产生一个在暗物质唯象学中起关键作用的轻赝标量粒子。

Abstract: We construct an explicit anomaly-free completion of a gauged baryon-number symmetry. The new gauge factor is \(U(1)_{\tilde B}\): when restricted to the Standard Model fields its charge \({\tilde B}\) coincides with ordinary baryon number, whereas in the full theory it becomes an extended baryonic symmetry acting on both the Standard Model and a secluded sector. We show that anomaly cancellation alone leaves a broad class of solutions, but that requiring consistent symmetry breaking, viable decays of the exotic states, the absence of stable coloured relics, a neutral dark matter candidate protected by a \(Z_2^{\rm DM}\) parity, and improved high-scale gauge-coupling unification strongly constrains the structure of the model. These requirements necessitate enlarging the minimal secluded fermion sector by additional scalar fields and Yukawa interactions, giving rise to a light pseudoscalar that plays an important role in the dark matter phenomenology. We implement the resulting renormalisable model in SARAH and analyse its spectrum and phenomenology with SPheno, MicrOMEGAs, SModelS, and HiggsTools. We identify viable regions of parameter space containing a heavy baryonic Z', an even heavier secluded sector, a neutral dark matter candidate compatible with relic-density and direct-detection constraints, and improved gauge-coupling evolution relative to the Standard Model. In these regions, the relic abundance is determined either by co-annihilation with nearby secluded states or by annihilation into light pseudoscalars from the extended scalar sector.

</details>


### [46] [Three-Loop QCD Corrections to Scattering Amplitudes of a Higgs Boson and Three Partons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12033)
*Xin Guan,Bernhard Mistlberger,Michael S. Ruf*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为高精度LHC唯象学提供关键输入量，特别是涉及希格斯玻色子与强子喷注（hadronic jet）的散射或产生过程，如希格斯+喷注的产生截面计算。

Method: 采用重顶夸克有效理论（heavy-top quark effective theory of QCD），利用积分-by-部分恒等式（integration-by-parts identities）并通过代码Blade实现，使用规范微分方程（canonical differential equations）计算主积分（master integrals）。

Result: 得到了以广义多对数函数（generalized polylogarithms）表示的紧凑解析表达式，适用于数值计算。观察到三圈阶下次领头颜色贡献在数值上与领头颜色项同等显著。

Conclusion: 所得振幅是精确LHC唯象学的关键组成部分，例如可用于涉及希格斯玻色子和强子喷注的产生截面等过程。

Abstract: We present helicity amplitudes at three loops in the heavy-top quark effective theory of QCD for the scattering of a Higgs boson and three light partons with full-color dependence. To obtain these results, we use integration-by-parts identities implemented in the code Blade and evaluate the master integrals using canonical differential equations. We obtain compact analytic expressions in terms of generalized polylogarithms suitable for numerical evaluation. We observe that sub-leading color contributions at three loops are numerically as significant as leading-color terms. Our amplitudes are key ingredients for precision LHC phenomenology, for example in production cross sections involving a Higgs boson and a hadronic jet.

### [47] [Static-Recoil Factorization in Heavy-Baryon Chiral EFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12037)
*Ziyu Dong,Teng Ma,Chengjie Yang,Zizheng Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种基于反冲道（recoil-channel）分波本征算符的on-shell重重子（heavy-baryon）展开方法，通过静态-反冲因子化（static--recoil factorization）系统地生成涉及高自旋共振（higher-spin resonances）的重重子扇区中的非冗余局域算符，并利用冯·诺依曼交替投影（von Neumann alternating projections）的线性代数约化处理味结构与全同粒子约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将重重子手征微扰论（heavy-baryon χPT）推广到高自旋共振时会引入非物理的低自旋混合成分，导致路径积分投影计算代价高昂，因此需要一种能够避免这些冗余成分的on-shell实现方案。

Method: 基于反冲道分波本征算符（recoil-channel partial-wave eigenoperators）开发on-shell重重子展开方法，实现静态质量依赖与反冲结构的分离，并在振幅空间（amplitude space）直接分配手征阶数（chiral order）。通过静态-反冲因子化系统生成非冗余局域算符，并采用基于冯·诺依曼交替投影的线性代数约化方法施加味结构与全同粒子约束。

Result: 该方法有效消除了非物理低自旋混合，实现了重子扇区中涉及高自旋共振的非冗余局域算符的系统生成，并成功通过线性代数约化提取了共同的物理子空间（common physical subspace）。

Conclusion: 该框架不仅适用于所讨论的具体问题，还可广泛推广到一般非相对论有效场论（nonrelativistic effective field theories）中。

Abstract: Extending heavy-baryon \(χ\)PT to higher-spin resonances introduces unphysical lower-spin admixtures, leading to costly path-integral projections. To resolve this, we develop an on-shell implementation of the heavy-baryon expansion based on recoil-channel partial-wave eigenoperators. These eigenoperators separate the static mass dependence from recoil structures and assign chiral order directly in amplitude space. The resulting static--recoil factorization systematically generates non-redundant local operators for heavy-baryon sectors involving higher-spin resonances. Flavor structures and identical-particle constraints are imposed through a new linear-algebraic reduction that uses von Neumann alternating projections to extract the corresponding common physical subspace. Beyond this specific application, the framework can be broadly applied to general nonrelativistic effective field theories.

</details>

### [48] [Analytical and numerical solutions to the non-diffusive Stefan problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12102)
*Matthew Van Ham,Minghan Xu,Samuel Huberman*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用麦克斯韦-卡塔尼奥-韦尔诺特（Maxwell–Cattaneo–Vernotte, MCV）方程对小斯蒂芬数（Stefan number, Ste ≪ 1）极限下的一维双曲斯蒂芬问题（hyperbolic Stefan problem）进行建模，通过摄动级数展开（perturbation series expansions）得到近似解，并提出两种修正策略处理渐近发散问题。结果表明界面轮廓呈抛物线形状，且热弛豫时间（thermal relaxation time）越大，早期双曲效应越明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典扩散斯蒂芬问题无法描述有限热传播速度下的相变过程，需引入双曲型热传导模型（如MCV方程）以捕捉早期瞬态双曲效应（hyperbolic effect）。小斯蒂芬数极限下的解析处理为理解这类非线性移动边界问题提供了理论切入点。

Method: 将时间表示为固液界面位置（solid-liquid interface position）的函数，对MCV方程进行摄动级数展开，得到解析近似解。首先在相变界面处考虑扩散传热的框架下推导一种解，随后提出两种修正策略：一是重标度内解（rescaled inner solution）与外解（outer solution）组合为合成解（composite solution），二是采用尺寸依赖的热物理系统参数（size-dependent thermo-physical system parameters）以更好地捕捉界面处的双曲效应。

Result: 界面轮廓呈现类似抛物线的形状，与扩散斯蒂芬问题的结果一致；热弛豫时间越大，早期双曲效应越显著。参数研究表明，模型误差随斯蒂芬数（Ste）的变化与摄动展开的理论截断误差（truncation error）一致；更大的无量纲热弛豫时间（τ̃）会放大早期双曲效应从而增加模型误差；更大的热扩散率（α）则延长双曲效应显著的时间区间，同样导致模型误差增加。

Conclusion: 基于MCV方程的小Stefan数摄动解能够有效描述双曲斯蒂芬问题中的移动边界行为，两种修正策略可缓解渐近发散问题；双曲效应在早期时间占主导，其影响程度和持续时间分别由τ̃和α控制。

Abstract: In this work, the Maxwell--Cattaneo--Vernotte (MCV) equation is used to model the one-dimensional hyperbolic Stefan problem in the limit of a small Stefan number (Ste $\ll$ 1). The solutions are approximated with perturbation series expansions using a reformulation in which time is expressed as a function of the solid-liquid interface position. The first proposed solution is derived in a framework that considers diffusive heat transfer at the phase change interface, for analytic tractability. Two rectification strategies are proposed to address the asymptotic divergence present in this formulation: a rescaled inner solution which is then combined with the outer solution to yield a composite solution, and size-dependent thermo-physical system parameters for better capture of hyperbolic effects at the phase change interface. The resulting interface profiles exhibit a characteristic parabolic-like shape, consistent with diffusive Stefan problem findings, with pronounced early-time hyperbolic effects at larger thermal relaxation times. Parametric studies are done over three pertinent variables in the dimensionless system: the Stefan number ($\mathrm{Ste}$), the dimensionless thermal relaxation time ($\widetilde τ$), and the thermal diffusivity ($α$). The studies suggest that model error scales with the Stefan number in accordance with the theoretical truncation error of the perturbation expansion. Additionally, larger values of $\widetilde τ$ amplify early-time hyperbolic effects, thereby increasing model error, while larger $α$ extends the relative temporal domain over which these hyperbolic effects remain significant, also corresponding to an increase in model error.

</details>


### [49] [Engineering Two-Dimensional Hybrid-Order Topological Insulators via Trilayer Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12314)
*Lizhou Liu,Cheng-Ming Miao,Qing-Feng Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种层间工程方案，在耦合三层陈系统中实现二维混合阶拓扑绝缘体（hybrid-order topological insulator），该体系同时具有一阶（手性边缘态）和二阶（角态）拓扑相，并通过层间隧穿实现边缘态杂化与能隙打开。混合阶相在质量型无序下保持鲁棒，层间杂化被确立为一种最小且普适的工程策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有拓扑绝缘体研究多聚焦于单一阶数（一阶或高阶）的拓扑相，而同时存在一阶与二阶拓扑态的混合阶体系尚未被充分探索。该工作旨在通过层间工程在少层陈系统中实现两种拓扑序的共存。

Method: 从三个独立的量子反常霍尔层（陈数$\mathcal{C}_{1/2/3}=+1/-1/+1\)出发，引入层间隧穿（interlayer tunneling）耦合，使边缘态杂化并打开体带隙，从而同时支持手性边缘态与零维角态。通过拓扑相图映射分析混合阶相的稳定性，并测试质量型无序（mass-type disorder）的影响。

Result: 在相同体带隙内成功实现了手性边缘态（一维）与角态（零维）的共存，即混合阶拓扑相。该相在质量型无序下仍保持鲁棒，相图明确了混合阶相的参数区域。

Conclusion: 层间杂化（interlayer hybridization）是一种最小且普适的策略，可用于在拓扑平台中工程化实现边缘态与角态的共存，为混合阶拓扑绝缘体的设计提供了新路径。

Abstract: We propose an interlayer-engineering scheme to realize a two-dimensional hybrid-order topological insulator, characterized by the coexistence of first-order and second-order topological phases, in a coupled trilayer Chern system. Starting from three quantum anomalous Hall layers with Chern numbers $\mathcal{C}_{1/2/3}=+1/-1/+1$ in the decoupled limit, interlayer tunneling hybridizes their edge states into a single chiral edge mode, while simultaneously opening a gap that supports corner states. Consequently, the system exhibits the coexistence of one-dimensional chiral edge states and zero-dimensional corner states within the same bulk gap, a hallmark of the hybrid-order topology. Furthermore, we map out the topological phase diagram, and show that the hybrid-order phase is robust against mass-type disorder. Our results identify interlayer hybridization as a minimal and broadly applicable strategy for engineering coexisting edge and corner states within a topological platform.

</details>


### [50] [Topological characterization of multifold band degeneracies in Altland-Zirnbauer symmetry classes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13016)
*Askar Iliasov,Zoltán Guba,Tsuneya Yoshida,Apoorv Tiwari,Tomáš Bzdušek*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于节点流形（nodal manifold）链接拓扑来刻画多重点简并（multifold band degeneracy）的新方法，克服了传统包围球面（enclosing sphere）范式因谱隙缺失而无法直接应用同伦分类的障碍，并在所有十种Altland-Zirnbauer（AZ）对称类中完成了对最小模型的表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，拓扑能带简并使用定义在能谱有隙的包围球面上的不变量来刻画，这一方案对于所有十种AZ对称类中的最小简并已基本完成，但高阶简并（higher-order degeneracies）几乎仅在晶体对称保护下被研究。本文旨在刻画那些稳定性仅来源于局域在动量空间中的AZ对称性的通用n重能带简并，并解决包围球面范式在此类情形下遭遇的基本障碍。

Method: 作者将传统包围球面范式的障碍转化为诊断工具：两个(n-1)重简并轨迹（degeneracy loci）在包围球面上的交点处互补谱隙（complementary spectral gaps）得以恢复，从而可分别用常规能带不变量加以刻画。由此建立双向对应关系：多重点简并的拓扑保护等价于节点流形在包围球面上的鲁棒链接（robustly linked），而一个节点流形上的循环（cycle）的能带不变量编码了其与另一节点流形循环的链接数（linking numbers）。

Result: 得到了n重简并的余维数（codimension）随n二次增长的结果，表明此类多重点简并出现在结合物理动量与调谐参数或合成维度的参数空间中。对所有十种AZ对称类的最小模型进行了表征，并在有显式参数化的情况下计算了能带不变量。

Conclusion: 该工作将多重能带拓扑（multifold band topology）重新表述为动量空间中链接节点流形的拓扑，所提出的方法为具有任意能带数的模型中多重能带简并的通用表征奠定了基础。

Abstract: Topological band degeneracies are conventionally characterized by invariants defined on enclosing spheres over which the energy spectrum remains gapped. This program has been completed for minimal degeneracies in all ten Altland-Zirnbauer (AZ) symmetry classes, whereas higher-order degeneracies have been studied almost exclusively under crystalline-symmetry protection. In this work, we characterize generic n-fold band degeneracies whose stability derives solely from AZ symmetries acting locally in momentum space. We find that their codimension grows quadratically with n, placing such multifold nodes in parameter spaces that combine physical momenta with tuning parameters or synthetic dimensions. However, the enclosing sphere paradigm faces a fundamental obstruction: two (n-1)-fold degeneracy loci intersecting at the n-fold band node pierce every enclosing sphere, implying that no uniform spectral gap (and thus no standard homotopy classification) exists. Here, we turn this obstruction into the diagnostic itself. On the nodal manifolds where the two loci intersect the enclosing sphere, complementary spectral gaps are restored, allowing us to characterize each with conventional band invariants. This enables us to establish a two-way correspondence: (1)~the multifold node is topologically protected whenever the nodal manifolds are robustly linked on the enclosing sphere, and (2)~band invariants on cycles of one nodal manifold encode their linking numbers with cycles of the other. We carry out this characterization for minimal models of all ten AZ classes, computing the band invariants wherever an explicit parametrization is available. Our results recast multifold band topology as the topology of linked nodal manifolds in momentum space, while our methods provide the foundation for a general characterization of multifold band degeneracies in models with arbitrarily many bands.

</details>


### [51] [Quantum anomalous Hall effect with tunable Chern numbers induced by d-wave sublattice-staggered altermagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12320)
*Lizhou Liu,Qing-Feng Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个最小自旋紧束缚模型（spinful tight-binding model），在正方晶格上通过d波子晶格交错交替磁性（d-wave sublattice-staggered altermagnetism）驱动量子反常霍尔效应（quantum anomalous Hall effect），实现了可调陈数（Chern number）𝒞=±1和𝒞=±2的绝缘相，并给出了完整的相图、能带反转分析以及边缘态和量子化电导平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在补偿磁体（compensated magnets）中实现量子反常霍尔效应是一个具有挑战性的问题；现有途径往往需要复杂的能带工程或特定材料平台。本文旨在提供一种更简单的实现路径。

Method: 作者在正方晶格上构造了一个最小自旋紧束缚模型，引入由泡利矩阵τ_z描述的A、B子晶格间交错排列的交换场（exchange field），即d波子晶格交错交替磁性。通过调控交错交换强度（staggered exchange strength）和子晶格交错势（sublattice-staggered potential）来系统分析其拓扑性质。

Result: 模型产生的绝缘相具有可调陈数𝒞=±1和𝒞=±2；确定了完整的相图；在布里渊区（Brillouin zone）的X和Y点识别出谷分辨的能带反转（valley-resolved band inversions）；演示了手性边缘态（chiral edge states）以及量子化的两端电导平台（quantized two-terminal conductance plateaus）。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种通过d波子晶格交错交替磁性在补偿磁体中实现量子反常霍尔效应的简单途径。

Abstract: We construct a minimal spinful tight-binding model on a square lattice, where a $d$-wave sublattice-staggered altermagnetism drives the quantum anomalous Hall effect. Here the exchange field is staggered between the two sublattices, where it takes opposite signs on $A$ and $B$ described by the Pauli matrix $τ_z$. The resulting insulating phases host tunable Chern numbers $\mathcal{C}=\pm1$ and $\mathcal{C}=\pm2$, controlled by the staggered exchange strength and the sublattice-staggered potential. We determine the complete phase diagram, identify valley-resolved band inversions at the $X$ and $Y$ points in the Brillouin zone, and demonstrate chiral edge states together with quantized two-terminal conductance plateaus. Our work provides a simple route to realizing the quantum anomalous Hall effect in compensated magnets via a $d$-wave sublattice-staggered altermagnetism.

*Lizhou Liu,Qing-Feng Sun,Ying-Tao Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文理论上证明，在二维拓扑绝缘体薄膜中，通过引入层分辨的d波交变磁（altermagnetism）项，可在保持体带隙不变的情况下诱导出二阶拓扑绝缘体相，并产生局域化的角态，建立了一条无需体自旋分裂即可实现高阶拓扑的鲁棒路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一种在不改变体带隙且不引入体自旋分裂的前提下，在二维拓扑绝缘体薄膜中实现高阶拓扑绝缘体相的新机制。

Method: 在二维拓扑绝缘体薄膜中引入层分辨的d波交变磁项，上下层符号相反，使系统保持$\mathcal{PT}$对称性和体带自旋简并，同时打开螺旋边缘态（helical edge states）的能隙并产生局域化角态（corner states）。采用非零的镜面分级绕数（mirror-graded winding numbers）刻画高阶拓扑相，并通过有效边缘理论证明角态源于狄拉克质量畴壁（Dirac mass domain walls）。

Result: 系统在保持体带隙不变和体带自旋简并的条件下，成功诱导出二阶拓扑绝缘体相；通过解析方法确定了相边界并构建了相应的拓扑相图。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一条无需体自旋分裂即可实现高阶拓扑的稳健路径，为交变磁体系中的高阶拓扑相研究提供了新思路。

Abstract: We theoretically demonstrate a second-order topological insulating phase induced by compensated altermagnetism, while keeping the bulk gap unchanged, in a two-dimensional topological insulator film. By introducing a layer-resolved out-of-plane $d$-wave altermagnetic term with opposite signs on the top and bottom layers, the system preserves $\mathcal{PT}$ symmetry and maintains spin degeneracy in the bulk bands, while simultaneously gapping the helical edge states and generating localized corner states. The resulting higher-order phase is characterized by nonzero mirror-graded winding numbers, and an effective edge theory shows that the corner states arise from Dirac mass domain walls. We further determine the phase boundaries analytically and construct the corresponding topological phase diagram, establishing a robust route to higher-order topology without bulk spin splitting.

### [53] [Domain wall motion in ferromagnetic nanowires driven by a localized Gaussian thermal gradient](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12347)
*M. A. Jafar Pikul,M. A. S. Akanda,M. T. Islam*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过随机朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特（Langevin Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert）方程，研究了单轴铁磁纳米线中磁畴壁（domain wall, DW）在激光局部高斯温度分布下的动力学行为。结果表明，DW速度随激光峰值温度线性增加、随激光-DW距离增加而减小，且与吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）呈非线性关系；运动主要由磁振子自旋转移矩（magnonic spin-transfer torque）驱动，而非熵矩（entropic torque）。激光宽度与激光-DW距离可独立调控DW响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 明确局部热驱动磁畴壁运动的微观机制，为自旋电子赛道存储器（spintronic racetrack-memory device）中的热控制策略提供物理基础。

Method: 基于随机朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特（stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert, sLLG）方程，在单轴铁磁纳米线上施加激光光斑的局部高斯温度分布（localized Gaussian temperature profile），数值模拟磁畴壁动力学。

Result: 磁畴壁速度随激光峰值温度线性增大，随激光与畴壁距离增大而减小；速度与吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）呈非线性关系，原因是阻尼增强热磁振子激发（thermal magnon excitation）但同时缩短磁振子传播长度（magnon propagation length）。由于畴壁初始位于激光加热区域之外，其位置处温度梯度实际为零，因此熵矩（entropic torque）可忽略，运动主要由磁振子自旋转移矩（magnonic spin-transfer torque）驱动。激光宽度与激光-畴壁距离可各自独立调控畴壁响应。

Conclusion: 本研究阐明了局部热驱动磁畴壁运动的物理机制，指出磁振子自旋转移矩是主要驱动力，并识别出激光宽度与激光-畴壁距离两个独立调控参数，为自旋电子赛道存储器的热管理策略提供理论指导。

Abstract: We investigate magnetic domain wall (DW) dynamics in a uniaxial ferromagnetic nanowire under the localized Gaussian temperature profile of a laser spot using the stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation. The DW velocity increases linearly with peak laser temperature and decreases with increasing laser to DW distance. The velocity varies nonlinearly with Gilbert damping because damping strengthens thermal magnon excitation but shortens the magnon propagation length. The DW initially lies away from the laser-heated region, so the temperature gradient at its position is effectively zero and the entropic torque is negligible. The DW motion is therefore mainly driven by magnonic spin-transfer torque. We analyze laser temperature, laser to DW distance, damping, uniaxial anisotropy, and laser width. The analysis shows that laser width and laser to DW distance independently control the DW response. These findings may clarify the mechanism of localized thermally driven DW motion and guide thermal control strategies in spintronic racetrack-memory devices.

### [54] [Effect of the local field and dipole-dipole interaction on the spontaneous ordering of dipole moments in bismuth monolayers with an orthorhombic structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12542)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索正交相铋单层在自发偶极矩出现时的晶格不稳定性机制，并揭示其可能存在的铁电与反铁电相变行为。

Method: 采用两种互补方法：(1) 通过铋原子的极化率（polarizability）并考虑局域洛伦兹-洛伦兹场（Lorentz-Lorenz field）计算晶格位点偶极矩；(2) 分析非极性对称晶格的振动谱（vibrational spectrum），识别对应铁电和反铁电不稳定性的两类软光学声子模。

Result: 第一种方法表明正交相铋单层可能存在多种反铁电和铁电相；第二种方法揭示了两种分别对应铁电和反铁电不稳定性的软光学声子模；同时展示了Born有效电荷与铁电相极化方向的关系，以及其在偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interaction）下导致极化光学声子频率降低中的作用。

Conclusion: 正交相铋单层存在由自发偶极矩驱动的铁电和反铁电晶格不稳定性，Born有效电荷对铁电相中的极化方向和声子频率行为具有重要影响。

Abstract: Using two complementary approaches, the instability of bismuth monolayers with an orthorhombic structure with respect to the emergence of spontaneous electric dipole moments at the crystal lattice sites has been studied. The first approach, based on determining the dipole moments of lattice sites through the polarizability of bismuth atoms and taking into account the local Lorentz-Lorenz field, suggests the possibility of the existence of several antiferroelectric and ferroelectric phases in orthorhombic bismuth monolayers. Using the second approach, the vibrational spectrum of a nonpolar symmetric lattice has been analyzed, and two types of soft optical modes corresponding to the ferroelectric and antiferroelectric instabilities of the monolayers have been revealed. The relationship of the Born effective charges to the polarization direction in the ferroelectric phase, as well as their role in the reduction of the frequency of the polar optical phonon, which characterizes the lattice deformation in the ferroelectric phase due to the dipole-dipole interaction, has been shown.

### [55] [Geometric Spin-Orbit Coupling Resolves the Contradictory CISS Effect in Chiral Single Molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12720)
*Shu-Zheng Zhou,Xi Sun,Kai-Yuan Zhang,Hua-Hua Fu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过引入几何自旋-轨道耦合与环境退相干的理论框架，系统研究了四种手性单分子中的手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）效应，发现CISS仅在中等退相干区间显著，在强相干和强退相干区间被完全抑制，从而统一了先前相互矛盾的实验观测结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验发现，同一类手性单分子体系中，部分研究报告了显著的自旋极化CISS效应，而另一项高精度重复测量（近千次独立测试）却未检测到明显CISS信号。这些相互矛盾的结果对手性单分子层面CISS效应的真实性提出了质疑，亟需一个统一的理论框架来解释上述分歧。

Method: 作者构建了一个融合几何自旋-轨道耦合（geometric spin-orbit coupling）与环境退相干（environmental decoherence）的理论框架，对四种具有不同几何构型和尺寸的手性单分子体系中的CISS效应进行了系统的理论计算与分析。

Result: CISS效应在强相干区间和强退相干区间被完全抑制，仅在中等退相干区间显现出可观测的自旋极化。在强相干区间，电子-电子相互作用和电子-振动耦合均能增强CISS效应：前者在大分子中更有效，后者在较小分子中作用更显著。升温会进一步增强自旋极化。

Conclusion: 该机制统一了相互矛盾的实验观测，揭示了CISS效应如何从规则螺旋（helical symmetric）手性演变为不规则螺旋（point-symmetric或axially symmetric）手性，为跨不同分子构型或对称性类别的单分子体系中的CISS现象提供了统一的理论基础。

Abstract: Some studies have reported clear chirality-induced spin selectivity (CISS) effect in four classes of chiral single molecules with remarkable spin polarization. In contrast, a recent high-precision measurement involving nearly a thousand individual tests failed to detect significant CISS signals in the same molecular systems (J. Am. Chem. Soc. 2025, \textbf{147}, 25043). These conflicting results cast doubt on whether CISS truly occurs in these chiral systems at the single-molecular level. To resolve this discrepancy, we develop a theoretical framework incorporating geometric spin-orbit coupling and environmental decoherence, enabling systematic study of the CISS in four chiral single molecules with distinct geometries and sizes. Our calculations show that the CISS effect is completely suppressed in both strong-coherence and strong-decoherence regimes, but becomes pronounced in the intermediate-decoherence regime, where observable spin polarization emerges. In the strong-coherence regime, both electron-electron interaction and electron-vibration coupling enhance the CISS effect: the former is more effective in large molecules, whereas the latter plays a more significant role in smaller ones. Increasing temperature further enhances spin polarization. The proposed mechanism unifies contradictory experimental observations and reveals how the CISS effect evolves from regular helical (helical symmetric) to irregular helical (point-symmetric or axially symmetric) chirality. This framework thus provides a basis for unifying CISS phenomena across single-molecule systems, regardless of their specific molecular configurations or symmetry classes.

</details>


### [56] [Dynamical Generation of Rectified Electric Current](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12741)
*Jin-Xin Hu,Congjun Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个适用于周期性系统的动态驱动整流（rectification）通用理论框架，该框架基于有限频率驱动打破时间平移对称性并注入能量，从而产生二阶非线性整流电流。整流电流有两个来源：（i）有限频率下杂质散射修正的分布函数；（ii）源于动态混合贝里曲率（dynamical mixed Berry curvature）的时域反常速度。将该理论应用于受面外振荡电场作用的翘曲磁性系统，所产生电流被表征为非线性磁电旋磁效应（nonlinear magnetoelectric gyrotropic effect），并可用于探测非共面反铁磁体中的奈尔序（Néel order）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 整流（rectification）是一种将交变驱动转换为直流的基本非线性输运过程。现有理论在静态极限下禁止任何稳态电流，而动态驱动下的整流机制尚未得到统一的通用理论描述，因此需要构建一个能够涵盖有限频率效应的普适框架。

Method: 提出了一个通用理论框架，其中动态外驱动与周期性系统的任意明确定义算符耦合。该理论区分了两个整流电流来源：（i）有限频率下杂质散射修正的分布函数贡献；（ii）由动态混合贝里曲率（dynamical mixed Berry curvature）导致的时域反常速度（time-domain anomalous velocity）贡献。

Result: 在翘曲磁性系统（buckled magnetic system）中，施加面外振荡电场（out-of-plane oscillating electric field）产生了被称为非线性磁电旋磁效应（nonlinear magnetoelectric gyrotropic effect）的电流。该整流电流对磁序（magnetic order）敏感，因此可作为非共面反铁磁体中奈尔序（Néel order）的可行电学探针。

Conclusion: 提出的理论框架适用于驱动频率远低于光学跃迁能隙（optical transition gap）的情形。研究结果揭示了动态驱动下整流过程的两个独立微观起源，并为利用电学手段探测反铁磁序提供了新途径。

Abstract: Rectification is a fundamental nonlinear transport process that converts an alternating drive into a direct current. In this work, we propose a general theoretical framework for electric current rectification triggered by a dynamical external drive that couples to an arbitrary well-defined operator of a periodic system, and which in the static limit forbids any steady current. In the dynamical regime, the finite frequency $Ω$ of the time-varying drive breaks time-translation invariance and injects energy into the system, enabling a second-order {\it nonlinear rectified} current that has no static counterpart. This rectification process has two distinct origins: (i) an impurity-scattering-modified distribution function at finite frequency, and (ii) a time-domain anomalous velocity stemming from a dynamical mixed Berry curvature. Both contributions persist when the driving frequency lies well below the optical transition gap. Applying our general theory to a buckled magnetic system subject to an out-of-plane oscillating electric field, we characterize the generated current as a {\it nonlinear magnetoelectric gyrotropic effect} and predict that the induced rectified current is sensitive to the magnetic order, thereby offering a feasible electrical probe of Néel order in non-coplanar antiferromagnets.

</details>


### [57] [What Is the Real-Time Atomistic Mechanism Behind Chirality-Induced Spin Selectivity in Donor-Chiral Bridge-Acceptor Molecules?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12819)
*Shu-Zheng Zhou,Xi Sun,Kai-Yuan Zhang,Hua-Hua Fu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个量子动力学模型，通过引入几何自旋轨道耦合（geometric spin-orbit coupling）机制，揭示了轴向手性分子中手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）的微观起源，并定量解释了局域在光激发供体-手性桥-受体分子中观测到的高自旋极化现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS, chiral-induced spin selectivity）已在光激发供体-手性桥-受体（D-Bχ-A）分子中被实验观测到，但其在手性系统中的微观机制尚不清楚。

Method: 发展了一个精确映射联萘型桥二聚体原子结构的量子动力学模型，并引入了几何自旋轨道耦合（geometric spin-orbit coupling）机制，以揭示轴向手性系统中CISS的内在起源。

Result: 光激发电子沿扭转路径传输时，几何自旋轨道耦合强度超过轻原子固有耦合一到两个数量级，产生可观测的高自旋极化。自旋极化包含两个分量：沿手性轴和垂直于手性轴的CISS相关极化，二者均为轴向手性内在属性，无需外场或自旋超交换传递；非阿贝尔曲率修正项为手性轴方向提供了严格的数学定义。计算得到的极化分量、手性依赖性和相对幅度（30-40%）与时间分辨电子顺磁共振测量定量吻合。

Conclusion: 该几何自旋轨道耦合框架为轴向手性分子中的CISS提供了自洽且普适的物理图像，并为手性自旋电子器件的设计提供了明确的理论指导。

Abstract: Chiral-induced spin selectivity (CISS) has been experimentally observed in photo-excited donor-chiral bridge-acceptor (D-Bχ-A) molecules [Science 382, 197-201 (2023)]. However, the microscopic mechanism underlying CISS in such chiral systems remains elusive. Here we develop a quantum dynamical model that precisely maps the atomic structure of binaphthyl-type bridge dimers in isolated D-Bχ-A molecules and introduce a geometric spin-orbit coupling (SOC) mechanism to unveil the intrinsic origin of CISS in axially chiral systems. During photo-excited electron transport along the twisted pathways, the geometric SOC coupling strength exceeds the intrinsic coupling of light atoms by one to two orders of magnitude, readily producing observable high spin polarizations. The resulting spin polarization comprises two components: the CISS-associated polarizations along and perpendicular to the chiral axis are intrinsic to axial chirality, requiring neither external fields nor spin-superexchange transfer, while a non-Abelian curvature correction provides a rigorous mathematical definition of the chiral axis direction. Our calculated polarization components, chirality dependence, and relative magnitudes (30-40\%) quantitatively match time-resolved electron paramagnetic resonance measurements. This geometric SOC framework offers a self-consistent and general physical picture of CISS in axially chiral molecules and provides explicit theoretical guidance for the design of chiral spintronic devices.

</details>

### [58] [Group Theory and the CFT Distance Conjecture: $\mathcal{N}=2$ Tensionless Strings Have No (Co)Weight](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12014)
*Florent Baume,Fabio Mantegazza*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文系统研究了四维大N N=2超共形场论（Superconformal Field Theories, SCFTs）在共形流形（conformal manifold）无限远点处的Hagedorn行为，发现Hagedorn温度由仿射或有限Cartan邻接矩阵的最大特征值决定，并将理论分为仿射型和ADE型两类普适类（universality classes），同时给出了CFT距离猜想（CFT Distance Conjecture）下指数增长率的上下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索四维N=2超共形场论在共形流形无限远点处的高能态指数增长行为（Hagedorn behavior），并试图建立其与李代数（Lie algebra）结构、普适类分类以及CFT距离猜想之间的联系。

Method: 基于可拉格朗日描述（Lagrangian description）的四维大N N=2超共形场论，利用其quiver形状对应的李代数和仿射/有限Cartan邻接矩阵（Cartan adjacency matrix）的最大特征值，分析整体自由极限下的Hagedorn温度，并推广到部分自由极限情形。

Result: 整体自由极限下，Hagedorn温度由仿射或有限Cartan邻接矩阵的最大特征值决定，形成两类普适类：仿射类（包括N=4超Yang-Mills的orbifold和orientifold投影）共享同一温度；ADE类温度由对偶Coxeter数（dual Coxeter number）决定。同时获得了CFT距离猜想预测的指数增长率的上下界，当quiver只有一个规范节点时下界被饱和。

Conclusion: 这些结果适用于所有具有经典规范对称性的大N N=2 quiver理论，包括带有超过双基本表示（bifundamental representations）物质的理论；还讨论了弦论构造和全息对应（holographic implications），并指出方法可推广到超对称性更低的更广泛理论族。

Abstract: We perform a systematic survey of the Hagedorn behaviour at infinite-distance points in the conformal manifold of four-dimensional large-$N$ $\mathcal{N}=2$ Superconformal Field Theories admitting a Lagrangian description. Many properties of these theories can be understood in terms of the Lie algebra encoding the shape of their quiver. We find that in the overall-free limit, the Hagedorn temperature is determined by the largest eigenvalue of an affine or finite Cartan adjacency matrix. This defines two types of universality classes of theories sharing the same high-energy exponential growth of states characteristic of string-like spectra. The first and largest is the affine case, corresponding to orbifold and orientifold projections of $\mathcal{N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills, and all share the same temperature. The others fall into universality classes following an ADE classification with a temperature set by the dual Coxeter number, and can be obtained by deforming the affine case. Our results apply to all large-$N$ $\mathcal{N}=2$ quivers with any classical gauge symmetry, including those with matter charged beyond bifundamental representations. We further discuss the string-theoretic construction of these theories and some of the holographic implications, as well as how our methods extend to broad families of theories with less supersymmetry. We also consider limits where only part of the theory becomes free, and find lower and upper bounds on the exponential rate predicted by the CFT Distance Conjecture. Both these bounds and the Hagedorn temperature are set by the same eigenvalue, and when the quiver has a single gauge node the lower bound is saturated, giving a natural explanation for the three universality classes recently found in the literature.

</details>


### [59] [The Hitchhiker's Guide to Tensionless String Limits in 4d SCFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12019)
*José Calderón-Infante,Angel M. Uranga,Irene Valenzuela*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过膜模型研究4d N=2,1超共形规范理论在弱耦合无穷远极限下的普适类，将其与AdS对偶中的涌现弦类型联系起来，发现三种普适类由双标度极限中重合的NS5-膜数量决定，并描述了对应的世界sheet理论及三种张力趋零的弦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解4d超共形场论（SCFT）共形流形上弱耦合无穷远极限中普适类（universality classes）的出现及其与AdS体对偶中涌现弦（emergent string）类型之间的关系。

Method: 对具有单规范群（simple gauge group）的超共形规范理论进行完整分类，利用Hanany-Witten构造显式构建所有模型（包括非爱因斯坦体对偶的情况）。通过轨道折叠/定向影投影（orbifold/orientifold projections）联系同一普适类中的理论，并在双标度极限（double-scaling limit）中分析NS5-膜系统，描述对应的世界sheet理论（worldsheet theory）。

Result: 发现弱耦合无穷远极限中的三种普适类由双标度极限下重合的NS5-膜数量决定；所有同一普适类中的理论源自同一母理论，且共享相同的闭弦背景；识别出三种张力趋零弦（emergent tensionless strings）：10d IIB型弦、一种亚临界弦（subcritical string）以及一种此前未知的新型弦。

Conclusion: 普适类的起源可从共形场论角度理解；该分析方法可推广至多规范因子理论乃至准共形规范理论，并用于构建部分弱耦合极限相关的SCFT网络。

Abstract: We study the appearance of universality classes in overall weak-coupling infinite-distance limits in the conformal manifold of 4d ${\cal N}=4,2,1$ superconformal gauge theories at large $N$ and their relation to the type of weakly-coupled emergent string in the AdS bulk dual using brane models. We focus on the complete set of theories with simple gauge group, and provide explicit Hanany-Witten constructions for each of them, including those that have non-Einstein bulk duals. This establishes that the three universality classes found in arXiv:2410.07309 are determined by the number of NS5-branes becoming coincident in a suitable double-scaling limit required to obtain the SCFT. Furthermore, all theories within a given universality class descend from the same parent theory by performing orbifold/orientifold projections (with possibly a small number of extra flavors), which are subleading effects at large $N$. This explains the origin of the universality classes from a CFT perspective. Moreover, we argue that theories in the same universality class share the same closed-string background -- generated by the double-scaled NS5-brane system -- in which the backreaction of D-branes is expected to generate the AdS throat holographically dual to the SCFT. We describe the corresponding worldsheet theories, and find that the three kinds of emergent tensionless strings correspond to the 10d type IIB string, a subcritical string previously studied in a related context, and a novel kind of string which we characterize in detail. Our tools are not limited to this set of SCFTs, but can be naturally applied to more general theories, and allow us to study interpolating models yielding a network of SCFTs related by partial weak-coupling limits. We explicitly discuss the generalization of our results to large classes of theories with more than one gauge factor and even to some quasi-conformal gauge theories.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文证明了球对称带电黑洞视界外模空间游走的精确上界，在电荷不低于渐近值的区域，该上界为$\frac{\pi}{2\sqrt{k_N}}$；并利用该界排除了一篇关于弱引力猜想证明中的潜在漏洞。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该结果强化了对弱引力猜想的理论支持，尤其在扰动玻色弦理论的框架下，填补了先前证明中的一个缺口。

Abstract: We prove sharp bounds on the moduli space excursion that is possible outside the event horizon of a spherically symmetric charged black hole. In regions where the black hole charge $Q (φ)$ is no less than its asymptotic value, we prove that the total moduli space excursion is less than $\fracπ{2\sqrt{k_N}}$ where $k_N$ is the rationalized Newton constant. We also show that the moduli space excursion in a specified direction in which $Q (φ)$ is non-decreasing satisfies the same bound. Applying our bound to electrically charged black holes, we rule out a potential loophole in a recent proof [arXiv:2401.14449] of the Weak Gravity Conjecture in perturbative bosonic string theory.

### [63] [Low-Temperature Holographic Conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12064)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用有效二维作用量来捕获尺度 $1/C$ 上 Schwarzian 模式（Schwarzian modes）的量子涨落效应；同时从四维引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）直接估算电导率的一圈（one-loop）贡献。

Result: 发现量子修正后的电导率呈现非单调温度依赖：随温度降低而下降，在 $CT_{\mathrm{min}}\simeq 0.023$ 处达到最小值，之后在 $CT\ll 1$ 区间以 $1/\sqrt{CT}$ 形式增长。二维有效描述与四维一圈计算在 $CT\gg 1$ 区间定性一致。

Conclusion: 量子修正显著改变了全息电导率在低温区域的行为，两种互补的计算方法在各自适用区间相互印证，揭示了全息框架下量子涨落对输运性质的重要影响。

Abstract: We revisit holographic electrical conductivity in the regime of very low temperatures where quantum fluctuations in the throat of the near-extremal, asymptotically AdS$_4$ dual black brane are strongly coupled. We treat the fluctuations via an effective two-dimensional action capturing the effects of the Schwarzian modes at the scale $1/C$. Our main result is a non-monotonic temperature dependence: the quantum-corrected conductivity decreases as the temperature is lowered, reaches a minimum at $(CT_{\mathrm{min}}\simeq 0.023)$, and grows as $(1/\sqrt{CT})$ for $(CT\ll 1)$. We further estimate the one-loop contribution to the conductivity directly from the four-dimensional gravitational path integral and find qualitative agreement with the effective two-dimensional description in the regime $(CT\gg 1)$. We find that quantum corrections substantially modify the low-temperature behavior of the holographic conductivity in both approaches.

### [64] [Computational homological methods for integrable field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12142)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将积分掉谱曲线的过程实现为循环$L_\infty$-代数的同伦转移（homotopy transfer）；构造$\mathbb{C}P^1$上除子扭化Dolbeault复形的强形变收缩（strong deformation retracts），使转移后的$L_\infty$-结构具有可计算性。

Conclusion: 该计算框架能够系统地将四维拓扑场论简化为二维可积场论，并以主手征模型验证了方法的正确性，为通过同调方法构造更多二维可积系统提供了显式的代数工具。

Abstract: We develop explicit computational tools for the recent homological approach to the construction of $2$-dimensional integrable field theories on $Σ$ from $4$-dimensional semi-holomorphic Chern-Simons theory on $Σ\times C$. In this framework, the operation of integrating out the spectral curve $C$ is realized by homotopy transfer of a cyclic $L_\infty$-algebra associated with the $4$-dimensional theory with prescribed singularities and boundary conditions. We construct explicit strong deformation retracts for divisor-twisted Dolbeault complexes on $C=\mathbb{C}P^1$ and use them to make the transferred $L_\infty$-structure computationally accessible. As an application, we study the choice of meromorphic $1$-form corresponding to the principal chiral model with a Wess-Zumino term. ### [65] [Low-temperature Quantum-corrected Holographic Transport with Momentum Relaxation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12066)
*Suman Das,Sabyasachi Maulik,Leopoldo A. Pando Zayas,Jingchao Zhang*

Conclusion: 近极端黑膜视界附近的Schwarzian量子涨落会在输运系数中产生普适的低温增强特征，其中非单调温度依赖性与关联材料中广泛观测到的行为高度相似，表明近视界量子引力（near-horizon quantum gravity）可能在凝聚态体系输运现象中留下可识别的印记。

Abstract: We determine the quantum corrections to transport arising from fluctuations of the near-AdS${}_2$ throat of near-extremal black branes in holographic models with momentum relaxation. By computing the shear viscosity and electrical conductivity at both zero and finite chemical potential, we uncover a universal low-temperature enhancement of transport generated by Schwarzian quantum fluctuations. Specifically, transport coefficients extracted from retarded Green's functions increase throughout the regime $C T \ll 1$. For operators with Schwarzian scaling dimension $Δ>1$, this enhancement is preceded by a universal minimum at a characteristic temperature $T_{\rm min} \propto C^{-1}$, leading to a non-monotonic temperature dependence strikingly similar to that observed in many correlated materials. In contrast, for the case $Δ=1$, relevant for the electrical conductivity, the transport coefficient evolves monotonically toward a constant value. Our results identify universal signatures of near-horizon quantum gravity in the transport properties of holographic quantum matter.

### [66] [Composite worldline instantons and the nonperturbative particle decay in constant external electric and magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12083)

Result: 在指数主导近似下，复合世界线瞬子方法在不同极限中得到的结果与自能虚部法和波函数重叠法给出的结果一致。

Conclusion: 复合世界线瞬子方法可用于估算外电场和磁场中质子衰变率（指数主导近似下）。此外，终态粒子的纠缠效应（entanglement of particles in the final state）可能对衰变过程有影响，但本文仅作简要提及。

Abstract: In this paper, we discuss the validity of the composite worldline instanton approach for the nonperturbative decay of charged particles in constant electric and magnetic fields. It is shown that the instanton results in the leading exponential approximation in the different limits agree with the ones obtained by the imaginary part of the self-energy in the external field and by overlap of the wave functions. We comment on the possible application of our results for the estimation of the decay rate of the proton in the external electric and magnetic field in the leading exponential approximation. The effects of entanglement of the particles in the final state are briefly mentioned.

</details>

Method: 通过将世界sheet σ-模型等价重写为Liouville场论耦合类时间背景荷场及边际变形；分析变形算子的不可归一化性及其与谱流扇区ω=2的关联；在半经典大k极限下比较中心荷行为。

Its role is to control the winding number violation in scattering amplitudes. In the semiclassical (large $k$) limit, the central charge of the Liouville factor tends to that of the dual CFT$_2$, namely $c\simeq 6k$. This may appear very similar to what occurs in the Liouville-type description of the dual deformed orbifold CFT$_2$, where a twist-2 deformation operator dressed with a non-normalized field also appears. ### [69] [Superconductive or superfluid condensation in curved spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12133)
*Leonardo Modesto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将Bogoliubov变换表达为幺正压缩算符，证明了弯曲时空量子场论的幺正性，并指出S矩阵是压缩算符与out-希尔伯特空间S矩阵的乘积（两者均幺正）。由此发现，Bogoliubov in-真空态等价于BCS态（费米子）或玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚基态（玻色子），重力将真空转化为电子-正电子凝聚态。通过逆向工程重构了黑洞（或Rindler）背景下量子场论的有效哈密顿量及质量间隙函数，该函数随温度近似线性增长。研究表明，霍金态恰好是一个BCS态，纠缠熵满足面积律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弯曲时空中的量子场论（quantum field theory in curved spacetime）长期面临幺正性（unitarity）是否被破坏的问题，尤其是在黑洞蒸发过程中。本文旨在严格证明一般弯曲时空中量子场论的幺正性，并澄清Bogoliubov变换、S矩阵幺正性与真空结构之间的内在联系。

Method: 将Bogoliubov变换表示为作用于初始与最终希尔伯特空间（Hilbert spaces）之间的幺正压缩算符（unitary squeezing operator），从而将弯曲时空中的S矩阵分解为该压缩算符与out-希尔伯特空间（通常为闵可夫斯基空间）中S矩阵的乘积。利用两个因子均为幺正算子，直接导出整体S矩阵的幺正性。进一步，通过逆向工程（reverse engineering）重构了黑洞或Rindler背景下量子场论的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）。

Result: Bogoliubov in-真空态对于费米子恰好是BCS态（Bardeen–Cooper–Schrieffer state），对于玻色子是玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose–Einstein condensate, BEC）超流基态；霍金态（Hawking state）精确为一个BCS态。质量间隙函数（mass gap function）随温度近似线性增长，随着黑洞质量减小，电子-正电子在越来越高的温度下凝聚成超导态。纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）满足面积律（area law）。

Conclusion: 重力（或加速力）能够从真空中产生一个多粒子系统，该系统不稳定并倾向于形成库珀对（Cooper pairs）的新基态，从而将真空转化为电子-正电子凝聚态。在此框架下，量子场论始终幺正演化，粒子解释在黑洞蒸发的每个阶段都得以保持。幺正性与面积律的同时成立为理解黑洞信息悖论（black hole information paradox）提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We provide a proof of unitarity for quantum field theory in a general spacetime. Our argument expresses the Bogoliubov transformations in terms of a unitary squeezing operator relating the initial and final Hilbert spaces. The $S$-matrix in curved spacetime is thus the product of the squeezing operator and the $S$-matrix in the out-Hilbert space (typically Minkowski). Since both factors are unitary, their product is unitary. It follows that the Bogoliubov in-vacuum is described by a BCS-like state (Bardeen--Cooper--Schrieffer): (i) for fermions, it is exactly the BCS state, but with electrons and positrons in place of electrons with opposite spin; (ii) for bosons, it is the Bose--Einstein condensate (BEC) superfluid ground state. Thus, gravity, or an accelerating force, creates from the vacuum a many-particle system unstable towards forming a new ground state of Cooper pairs. Technically, gravity converts the vacuum into an electron-positron condensate, with respect to which quantum field theory evolves unitarily. By reverse engineering, we reconstruct the effective Hamiltonian of QFT in a black hole (or Rindler) background, together with a simple formula for the mass gap function, which grows approximately linearly with the temperature. Hence, electrons and positrons condense into a superconducting state at increasingly higher temperatures as the black hole mass decreases. Unitarity and the particle interpretation are preserved at every stage of evaporation. The Hawking state is exactly a BCS state. Finally, we compute the entanglement entropy and derive the area law.

</details>


### [70] [Non-Abelian $A_4$ vortices in $SO(3)$ gauge theory and non-invertible symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12366)
*Yoshihiko Abe,Tetsutaro Higaki,Kazuya Murakami,Muneto Nitta,Ryo Yokokura*

<details>

Method: 采用(3+1)维可重整化SO(3)规范-希格斯理论，希格斯场取自旋-3（spin-3）表示，将规范群破缺至四面体群A₄。利用非阿贝尔基本群π₁(SO(3)/A₄)≃Ã₄（二元四面体群）对涡旋进行分类，并通过数值方法求解轴对称涡旋解，计算其holonomy和张力。

Result: 获得了两类显式轴对称涡旋解，其holonomy分别对应A₄的二阶和三阶共轭类；数值张力表明系统在希格斯与规范玻色子质量比变化时呈现I型、II型和BPS-like行为；涡旋由Ã₄的共轭类分类，而红外观则由A₄的共轭类标记；光滑涡旋在红外极限下退化为A₄离散规范理论的Gukov–Witten面算子。

Conclusion: 本文为离散规范理论中的非可逆缺陷（non-invertible defects）提供了可重整化的紫外完备化，建立了非阿贝尔涡旋与Gukov–Witten面算子之间的对应关系，为理解规范场论中高维缺陷的微观结构奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We construct finite-tension non-Abelian vortex solutions in a renormalizable $(3+1)$-dimensional $SO(3)$ gauge theory Higgsed to the tetrahedral group $A_4$ by a Higgs field in the spin-3 representation. Since the vacuum manifold is $SO(3)/A_4$, the vortices are characterized by the non-Abelian fundamental group $π_1(SO(3)/A_4)\simeq \widetilde{A}_4$, the binary tetrahedral group. We obtain explicit axisymmetric vortex solutions carrying holonomies corresponding to the order-two and order-three conjugacy classes of $A_4$, determine their tensions numerically, and show that they exhibit type-I, type-II, and Bogomol'nyi--Prasad--Sommerfield-like behavior depending on the Higgs and gauge boson mass ratios. The vortices are classified by conjugacy classes of $\widetilde{A}_4$, while their infrared descriptions are labeled by conjugacy classes of $A_4$. We further demonstrate that the smooth finite-tension vortices reduce in the infrared to Gukov--Witten surface operators of the $A_4$ discrete gauge theory, thereby establishing a finite-energy ultraviolet completion of non-invertible defects in a renormalizable gauge-Higgs theory.

Result: 只有渐近于N=4真空的解可行，对应N=2 SCFT中的线缺陷；SO(2)×ISO(3)群下得到红外为N=2 SCFT、紫外为六维N=(0,2)场论的解；SO(2)×SO(3)×SO(3)群下发现连接两个N=4真空的线缺陷解。

In gauged supergravity with $SO(2)\times ISO(3)$ gauge group, we find similar solutions with the $N=2$ SCFT appearing in the IR while the UV field theories correspond to six-dimensional $N=(0,2)$ field theories arising from M5-branes wrapped on a hyperbolic space $H^2$. The solution with $SO(2)\times SO(3)$ symmetry is also uplifted to eleven dimensions via a consistent truncation on $H^2\times S^4$. Finally, for gauged supergravity with $SO(2)\times SO(3)\times SO(3)$ gauge group that admits two $N=4$ supersymmetric $AdS_5$ vacua, we find a solution describing a line defect that interpolates between these two vacua as well as a solution with only one asymptotic $AdS_5$ geometry.

### [72] [Off-shell equivalence in quantum field theory and gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12644)
*Iberê Kuntz,Stefano Liberati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于Vilkovisky–DeWitt有效作用量发展了一套操作性判据，用于判断量子理论在场重定义（field redefinitions）下何时保持离壳（off-shell）等价，区分了局部、分支与全局等价，并指出metric f(R)引力与其辅助场形式在路径积分中施加约束时才是等价的量子理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准等价定理（equivalence theorem）是壳（on-shell）结果，无法判断量子描述在离壳（off-shell）情形下是否等价；而在引力、宇宙学和非平衡量子场论中，离壳等价性至关重要。本文旨在为这一问题建立操作性判据。

Method: 以Vilkovisky–DeWitt有效作用量（Vilkovisky–DeWitt effective action）为核心，通过将位形空间（configuration-space）张量与可容许探针（admissible probes）配对构造标量可观测量（scalar observables）来检验等价性，使判据对可观测量类别敏感。

Result: 区分了局部（local）、分支（branchwise）和真正全局（genuinely global）等价三类情形。以metric f(R)引力和标量场论为例证明：metric f(R)引力与其辅助场重新表述仅在路径积分中强制施加辅助约束时才是相同量子理论；将度量和标量视为独立积分变量量子化对应的标量-张量作用量则定义不同的量子理论。

Conclusion: 表观的量子不等效可追溯为不同量子对象之间的比较，而非实际等价的失效。该工作为场重定义和辅助变量扩展（auxiliary-variable extensions）下的局域与全局等价提供了普遍且精确的概念。

Abstract: Field redefinitions connect many formulations of the same physics, but the standard equivalence theorem is an on-shell result and cannot be used to decide when two quantum descriptions are equivalent off shell. This paper develops an operational criterion for that problem in terms of the Vilkovisky--DeWitt effective action. The central idea is that equivalence should be tested on scalar observables built by pairing configuration-space tensors with admissible probes. This makes the criterion sensitive to the observable class under consideration and separates the usual on-shell notion of equivalence from the stronger off-shell notions needed in gravity, cosmology and non-equilibrium quantum field theory. Metric $f(R)$ gravity and a scalar field theory example serve as prototypes, showing how the formal criterion distinguishes local, branchwise and genuinely global equivalence. In particular, we show that metric $f(R)$ gravity and its auxiliary-field reformulation yield the same quantum theory when the auxiliary constraint is enforced in the path integral. This is distinct from quantizing the corresponding scalar--tensor action with the metric and scalar treated as independent integration variables, which defines a different quantum theory. Apparent quantum inequivalences can then be traced to comparisons between different quantum objects, rather than to a failure of actual equivalences. This leads to general and precise notions of local and global equivalence under both field redefinitions and auxiliary-variable extensions.

</details>


### [73] [Quantum States Prepared by Wormholes: Long-Wavelength Deviations from Bunch-Davies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12772)
*George Lavrelashvili,Jean-Luc Lehners*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了由酒杯虫洞（wineglass wormholes）介导的婴儿宇宙（baby universes）成核过程，分析了这些虫洞几何所准备的张量与标量探针场涨落的量子态，发现其在大尺度上偏离Bunch-Davies真空，导致角功率谱产生偏移和振荡，从而为宇宙学观测提供可检验信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索酒杯虫洞在渐近反德西特或平直时空中介导婴儿宇宙成核时，所准备的量子涨落态的性质，以及这些涨落如何影响后续暴胀阶段的可观测宇宙学信号。

Method: 研究了酒杯虫洞几何所准备的张量与标量探针场涨落的量子态。虫洞由轴子（axionic）或磁荷（magnetic charges）支撑，并在电荷趋于零的极限下经历拓扑相变，过渡到无边瞬子（no-boundary instantons）。

Result: 短波长模式复现了Bunch-Davies真空，但大尺度模式出现偏离。这些偏离依赖于虫洞电荷，会导致后续暴胀阶段产生的角功率谱（angular power spectrum）出现小幅偏移和振荡。在电荷趋于零的极限下，标量和张量涨落对Bunch-Davies态的偏离均被压制，表明拓扑相变是平滑的。

Conclusion: 酒杯虫洞介导的婴儿宇宙成核过程会在暴胀可观测信号中留下特征性印记，且该效应在电荷消失的极限下平滑过渡到无边构型，为宇宙早期量子引力效应提供了潜在的可检验预言。

Abstract: Wineglass wormholes mediate the nucleation of baby universes out of an asymptotically Anti-de Sitter or flat spacetime. Upon materialization, the new universe naturally undergoes an inflationary phase. Here we study the quantum state of tensor and probe scalar field fluctuations that these wormhole geometries prepare, finding that they reproduce the Bunch-Davies vacuum for short-wavelength modes but lead to deviations from Bunch-Davies on large scales. These deviations, which depend on the charge of the wormhole, cause a small shift as well as oscillations in the angular power spectrum generated by an ensuing inflationary phase, and thus provide a distinctive cosmological observable.
  The wormholes are supported by either axionic or magnetic charges. In the limit of vanishing charge, they undergo a topological transition after which they contain no-boundary instantons. We find that the small-charge limit suppresses deviations from the Bunch-Davies state for both scalar and tensor fluctuations, indicating that the topological transition is smooth.

### [74] [On interacting non-Abelian antisymmetric tensor field models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12798)
*I. Buchbinder,N. Kozyrev*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过群流形上的维度约化（dimensional reduction on a group manifold）研究相互作用反称张量场模型（interacting antisymmetric tensor field models）的规范结构（gauge structure），发现其规范变换的可约性阶数（stages of reducibility）与对应的自由模型一致，而紧致流形尺寸相关的维度参数充当耦合常数（coupling constant）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决相互作用反称张量场模型中规范变换可约性（reducibility of gauge transformations）的未解决问题，考察维度约化后的相互作用模型与自由模型在可约性结构上的异同。

Method: 采用群流形上的维度约化方法，将高维理论约化为四维模型，引入紧致流形尺寸作为耦合常数，并分析规范变换的可约性阶数。

Result: 相互作用模型的可约性阶数与对应的自由模型完全相同。

Conclusion: 维度约化构造的相互作用反称张量场模型保留了自由理论在规范变换可约性方面的结构特征。

Abstract: We study the gauge structure of interacting antisymmetric tensor field models obtained by the dimensional reduction on a group manifold. In such models a dimensionful parameter related to the size of the compact manifold plays the role of a coupling constant. We focus on open issues of reducibility of the gauge transformations in these theories and show that stages of reducibility of the interacting models coincide with ones of corresponding free counterparts.

### [75] [Timelike Entanglement First Law and Linearized Field Equations in Higher Curvature Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12834)
*Mei-Hui Xiao,Guo-Ying Li,Song He,Jia-Rui Sun*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在Lovelock引力对偶的全息共形场论中，利用双Wick转动公式和Jacobson-Myers熵泛函，研究了类时纠缠第一定律。结果表明，在双曲子区域和低能热激发下，一个普适的重整化因子统一控制高阶曲率修正对熵和模哈密顿量变分的影响，且类时纠缠第一定律等价于围绕最大对称背景的线性化Lovelock引力场方程。

Result: 一个普适的 multiplicative 重整化因子统一控制高阶曲率修正对熵和模哈密顿量变分的贡献，满足$ΔS=Δ\langle H\rangle$。在可归一化扰动下，Jacobson-Myers泛函的变分退化为爱因斯坦引力的结果乘以相同因子，该因子重整化了线性化Lovelock引力场方程中的有效牛顿常数（effective Newtonian constant）。边界项在共形极限下消失。

Abstract: We investigate the timelike entanglement first law in holographic conformal field theories whose bulk dual is Lovelock gravity. Using the double Wick rotation formulation of timelike entanglement entropy together with the Jacobson-Myers entropy functional, we compute the linear variation of holographic timelike entanglement entropy for hyperbolic subregions. For cubic Lovelock gravity, we explicitly show that a single, universal multiplicative renormalization factor governs how higher curvature interactions enter the variations of both the entropy and the modular Hamiltonian, leading to $ΔS=Δ\langle H\rangle$ for low-energy thermal excitations. We then extend the analysis to Lovelock gravity of arbitrary order around the anti-de Sitter spacetime in the Fefferman-Graham gauge. For normalizable perturbations, the variation of the Jacobson-Myers functional reduces to the Einstein gravity's result multiplied by the same coupling-dependent factor that renormalizes the effective Newtonian constant in the linearized field equations of Lovelock gravity. We further show that the boundary contribution vanishes in the conformal limit for the class of perturbations considered. Consequently, the timelike entanglement first law is equivalent to the linearized field equations of Lovelock gravity about the maximally symmetric background, within the hyperbolic and perturbative regime considered in the present paper.

### [76] [Thermodynamic scaling and string dynamics in rotating holographic QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12906)
*Leila Shahkarami,Farid Charmchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-膨胀子（Einstein–Maxwell–dilaton）框架的全息QCD模型，研究了有限角速度对相结构和Schwinger对产生（Schwinger pair production）的影响。旋转通过一个boost构造引入，将静态背景变换为稳态旋转几何。研究发现：热力学相边界满足精确的标度关系（scaling relation），表明旋转热力学完全由静态解的boost变换决定；弦的禁闭-解禁闭（confinement–deconfinement）相变不再服从热力学标度关系，且随角速度增大，热力学禁闭但弦解禁闭的区域扩大；旋转降低了Schwinger效应的临界电场和势垒高度/宽度，从而增强正反粒子对产生。旋转在热力学部分仅通过标度律产生平凡效应，但在弦部分产生全新的物理效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-膨胀子（Einstein–Maxwell–dilaton）框架的全息QCD模型；通过boost构造从静态背景生成稳态旋转几何；使用巨势（grand potential）和响应函数（response functions）研究相图；通过有效弦张力（effective string tension）分析禁闭效应；采用势能分析方法（potential analysis approach）研究Schwinger效应。

Result: 热力学相边界满足精确的标度关系，旋转热力学完全由静态解的boost变换决定。弦的禁闭-解禁闭相变温度与化学势随旋转而降低，且其相边界不服从热力学标度关系，导致热力学禁闭但弦解禁闭的区域随角速度增大而扩大。旋转降低了Schwinger效应的禁闭临界电场和灾难性临界电场（catastrophic critical electric fields），抑制势垒高度和宽度，从而增强对产生。在解禁闭相中，旋转还产生一个世界sheet视界（worldsheet horizon），限制弦解的最大径向范围。

Conclusion: 旋转在热力学部分通过精确标度律产生平凡效应，但在弦部分产生全新的、非平凡的物理效应，表明全息QCD模型中旋转对禁闭和解禁闭相中不同层次物理的影响具有本质区别。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of finite angular velocity on the phase structure and Schwinger pair production in a holographic QCD model based on the Einstein--Maxwell--dilaton framework. Rotation is introduced through a boost construction that generates a stationary rotating geometry from the corresponding static background. We first study the thermodynamic phase diagram using the grand potential together with several response functions and show that all thermodynamic phase boundaries satisfy an exact scaling relation under rotation, implying that the rotating thermodynamic sector is completely determined by the corresponding static solution through a simple boost transformation. We then investigate confinement through the effective string tension and find that, consistent with the thermodynamic observables, rotation decreases the string confinement--deconfinement transition temperature and chemical potential. The corresponding phase boundary, however, no longer obeys the thermodynamic scaling relation. Consequently, the region in the phase diagram that is thermodynamically confined but string deconfined grows with angular velocity. We further study the Schwinger effect using the potential analysis approach. Rotation lowers both the confining and catastrophic critical electric fields and suppresses the height and width of the potential barrier, thereby enhancing pair production in both confined and deconfined phases. In the deconfined phase, rotation also generates a worldsheet horizon that limits the radial extent of connected string solutions and reduces both the maximum quark--antiquark separation and the deepest turning point of the energetically favored string. These results demonstrate that, while rotation acts trivially in the thermodynamic sector through an exact scaling law, it produces genuinely new effects in the string sector.

Abstract: In this note, starting from the exact counting formulae for 4D BPS black hole degeneracies in the cases of 1/2 BPS $\mathcal{N}=4$ and 1/8 BPS $\mathcal{N}=8$ solutions, expressed as Rademacher expansions for coefficients of modular and Jacobi forms respectively, we explicitly show how the number theoretic data in each Rademacher summand is encoded by a Segal-Bargmann heat kernel calculation in the de Alfaro-Fubini-Furlan (DFF) model of conformal quantum mechanics, thus demonstrating the holographic origin of the BPS Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, and all logarithmic and power law suppressed corrections to it. Hence, for the two classes of 4D BPS black holes under consideration, we have inferred the holographic CQM relevant for microscopic state counting from the exact number-theoretic degeneracy formulae and demonstrated the emergence of the near-horizon AdS$_2$ attractor geometry that is holographically dual to it.
