### [79] [Causality and realizability of local operations in quantum field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12976)
*Jan Mandrysch,Robin Simmons,Miguel Navascues*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子场论（QFT）中局部操作与因果性之间的关系。证明了存在无法通过FV方案任意逼近的因果通道，且判断FV复合实现性是不可计算问题。同时指出，随机位移类因果仪器可FV实现，并支持非 demolition 的测量与概率性逼近任意QFT操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Sorkin佯谬（Sorkin paradox）——在量子场论中，若将观察者可访问的局部操作与Kraus算子可定域化的量子仪器（quantum instruments）等同，会导致超光速通信（superluminal communication）。因此需要进一步约束QFT中允许的局部操作集合，以确保与爱因斯坦因果性（Einstein's causality）相容。

Method: 同时研究了两种保证因果性的QFT操作框架：Jubb和Oeckl提出的QFT仪器需满足的最小条件，以及Fewster和Verch提出的FV实现（FV-realizable）框架。在自由标量场（free scalar field）的QFT背景下，分析了因果通道的FV可实现性、可逼近性及计算复杂性。

Result: (1) 存在因果通道（causal channels）无法通过FV方案任意逼近。(2) 判断一个给定仪器能否通过组合若干FV操作实现，或远离可实现性，是一个不可计算问题（uncomputable problem）。(3) 一类广泛的因果仪器——测量通道为场算符随机位移（random displacements）者——是FV可实现的，可用于实现任何场正交分量的正算子取值测度（Positive Operator Valued Measure, POVM）的非 demolition 测量，并可概率性（heralded, probabilistic）逼近任意QFT操作（无论因果与否）。

Conclusion: FV框架在确保因果性的同时存在本质局限（不可逼近性与不可计算性），但随机位移类仪器作为FV可实现子集提供了丰富的操作能力，包括非 demolition 测量与概率性通用逼近，为局部QFT操作理论提供了可行的研究方向。

Abstract: In 1993, Sorkin noted, in the context of quantum field theory (QFT), that identifying the operations accessible to an observer acting in some spacetime region with quantum instruments whose Kraus operators are localizable therein leads to superluminal communication. This so-called Sorkin paradox can be resolved by further constraining the set of allowed local operations in QFT. In this spirit, Jubb and Oeckl identified the minimal conditions that QFT instruments must satisfy to be compatible with Einstein's causality. Independently, Fewster and Verch proposed a framework for local QFT operations that generalizes non-relativistic quantum measurement theory; remarkably, such FV-realizable instruments were shown to be causal. In this work, we study both approaches in the quantum field theory of the free scalar field. In this regard, we prove that there exist causal channels that cannot be arbitrarily well approximated through FV schemes. Moreover, deciding whether a given instrument is implementable or far away from being implementable by composing several FV operations is an uncomputable problem. On a more optimistic note, we show that a very wide class of causal instruments is FV-realizable: namely, those whose measurement channels are random displacements of the field operators. As we show, those suffice to implement any Positive Operator Valued Measure over a set of field quadratures in a non-demolition way (i.e., without perturbing any other commuting quadratures). Similarly, they allow approximating arbitrary QFT operations, causal or not, in a heralded, probabilistic way.

</details>


### [80] [Enhanced Correlations in Hawking Radiation from Near-Extremal Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12989)
*Suzanne Bintanja,Seolhwa Kim,Per Kraus*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过约化到s波并采用哈密顿形式，研究了由坍缩形成的近极端Reissner-Nordstrom黑洞中，由于近视界区域增强的引力反作用效应所导致的出射霍金辐射关联。推导出的有效耦合在低温下增长，产生的修正印记于无穷远处的关联函数；该有效作用量在AdS_2区域等价于标准的JT/Schwarzian描述，且当忽略度规涨落时结果回归霍金原始处理。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的霍金辐射计算忽略了度规的量子涨落，然而在近极端黑洞（near-extremal black hole）的低温极限下，引力反作用（gravitational backreaction）效应显著增强，可能对出射辐射的关联结构产生重要修正。因此，需要建立一种包含量子度规涨落的框架来系统计算这些修正。

Method: 将问题约化到s波，采用爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论（Einstein-Maxwell theory）耦合标量场的哈密顿形式。通过求解约束条件，得到包含量子级引力反作用效应的标量场有效作用量，其有效耦合为g = G/(πr_0^3 T_H)。该作用量在AdS_2区域等价于耦合了穿衣双局域算符（dressed bilocal operators）的JT/Schwarzian描述。

Result: 得到的有效作用量对自由场霍金态产生修正，这些修正印记于在零无穷远（null infinity）处测量的霍金辐射关联函数。该方法在树图层面再现了JT/Schwarzian描述的所有边界关联子，并复现了一些单圈结果。

Conclusion: 该框架通过约化标量作用量量子力学地包含了度规涨落，而非使用半经典期望值；当忽略度规涨落时，辐射计算显然回归到霍金的原始处理方法。

Abstract: We consider the formation of a near-extremal Reissner-Nordstrom black hole by collapse, and show how to compute correlations in the outgoing Hawking radiation due to enhanced gravitational backreaction effects in the near-horizon region. This is done by reducing to the s-wave and employing the Hamiltonian formulation of Einstein-Maxwell theory coupled to a scalar field. Solving the constraints yields an action for the scalar field that incorporates gravitational backreaction effects at the quantum level, governed by an effective coupling g = G/(πr_0^3 T_H) that grows at low temperature, as in recent Schwarzian-based analyses. This action produces corrections to the free field Hawking state which are imprinted on correlation functions of the Hawking radiation measured at null infinity. As part of our analysis, we show that this action evaluated in the AdS_2 region is equivalent, at the level of all tree-level boundary correlators, to the standard JT/Schwarzian description coupled to dressed bilocal operators. We also reproduce some one-loop results. In our approach, metric fluctuations are included quantum mechanically through the reduced scalar action, rather than through a semiclassical expectation value, and our computation of the radiation manifestly reduces to Hawking's original treatment when metric fluctuations are neglected.

### [81] [The Infraparticle Edge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13001)
*Soo-Jong Rey*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于软量子电动力学（soft QED）的量子仪器（quantum instrument），通过两次投影推导出带电粒子谱边（charged-particle spectral edge）。结果表明，包含软光子辐射的包容性能量分布（inclusive energy distribution）在阈值附近呈现幂律行为，指数由软环境（soft environment）的对角响应系数固定，其形式类似有能隙的非粒子谱（gapped unparticle spectrum）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子电动力学中带电粒子的谱函数在红外区域受到软光子辐射的显著修正。现有方法未能统一处理包含全部软光子信息的包容性分布（inclusive distribution）的非微扰结构及其与退相位（dephasing）之间的关系，因此需要一种基于量子仪器（quantum instrument）的严格框架来刻画谱边。

Method: 本文从软QED的量子仪器（quantum instrument）出发，对其施加两次投影：第一次对未分辨光子求迹，得到约化的硬过程通道（reduced hard-sector channel）；第二次将结果投影到总能量上，得到包容性能量分布（inclusive energy distribution）。其拉普拉斯指数由对角软强度（diagonal soft intensity）固定。通过保留相干核（coherence kernel），从同一个软环境（soft environment）的两个收缩（contractions）推导硬过程退相位（hard-sector dephasing）和谱边（spectral edge）。进一步对红外能量边缘量（infrared energy marginals）进行分类，推导有限分辨残差（finite-resolution residue），并证明红外可积扰动下的稳定性，分离出环境指数（bath exponent）与硬阈值指数（hard threshold exponent）。

Result: 对硬光子谱密度 ${\rm d} N_h(ω)=η_h{\rm d}ω/ω+{\rm d} N_{h,\mathrm{reg}}(ω)$，得到包容性分布 $ρ_{\mathrm{inc}}(s)\sim Cθ(s-m^2)(s-m^2)^{-1+η_h}$。对角系数 $κ_{aa}$ 固定端点指数（endpoint exponent），而 $\frac12(κ_{aa}+κ_{bb}-2\operatorname{Re}κ_{ba})$ 固定硬过程替代方案之间的退相位指数（dephasing exponent）。有限分辨残差为 $Z(μ)=(μ/Λ)^{η_h}$。对单电子谱测度（one-electron spectral measure），硬阈值因子是正则的（regular），谱边呈现有能隙非粒子谱（gapped unparticle spectrum）的局域幂律，其指数是未分辨光子扇区（unresolved photon sector）的响应系数。

Conclusion: 本文建立了软QED中包容性谱边（inclusive spectral edge）与退相位（dephasing）的统一非微扰框架，表明谱边的幂律指数完全由软环境（soft environment）的响应系数决定。该结构类似有能隙的非粒子谱（gapped unparticle spectrum），且在红外可积扰动下保持稳定，为处理含光子的量子过程提供了严格的解析工具。

Abstract: I derive the charged-particle spectral edge from the quantum instrument of soft QED. I use two projections of that instrument. Tracing over unresolved photons gives the reduced hard-sector channel. Pushing the outcomes to total energy gives the inclusive energy distribution. Its Laplace exponent is fixed by the diagonal soft intensity. For ${\rm d} N_h(ω)=η_h{\rm d}ω/ω+{\rm d} N_{h,\mathrm{reg}}(ω)$, I obtain $ρ_{\mathrm{inc}}(s)\sim Cθ(s-m^2)(s-m^2)^{-1+η_h}$. I retain the coherence kernel and derive hard-sector dephasing and the spectral edge from two contractions of one soft environment. The diagonal coefficient $κ_{aa}$ fixes the endpoint exponent, while $\frac12(κ_{aa}+κ_{bb}-2\operatorname{Re}κ_{ba})$ fixes the dephasing exponent between hard alternatives. I then classify infrared energy marginals, derive the finite-resolution residue $Z(μ)=(μ/Λ)^{η_h}$, prove stability under infrared-integrable perturbations, and separate the bath exponent from a hard threshold exponent. For the one-electron spectral measure, the hard threshold factor is regular. The resulting edge has the local power law of a gapped unparticle spectrum, while its exponent remains a response coefficient of the unresolved photon sector.

</details>

### [82] [Inclusive P-wave Quarkonium Decay Widths from Lattice QCD and pNRQCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13024)
*Nora Brambilla,Viljami Leino,Julian Mayer-Steudte,Panayiotis Panayiotou,Andrea Shindler,Antonio Vairo,Xiang-Peng Wang*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出将格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）与强耦合势非相对论量子色动力学（pNRQCD）相结合的理论框架，首次通过淬火格点QCD计算确定了双点色电关联函数（two-point chromoelectric correlator）的普适矩（universal moment），从而实现对P波重夸克偶素（heavy quarkonium）到轻强子（light hadrons）的遍举衰变宽度（inclusive decay widths）的第一性原理计算。该框架成功重现了χ_{cJ}(1P)的观测宽度，并对未测量的χ_{bJ}(nP)宽度给出了理论预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从第一性原理QCD出发计算遍举强子衰变宽度（inclusive hadronic decay widths）长期以来是一个悬而未决的难题。现有方法难以同时处理非微扰效应（nonperturbative effects）与微扰短距离贡献，尤其对于P波重夸克偶素的衰变过程缺乏系统性的第一性原理计算方案。

Method: 将格点QCD（lattice QCD）与强耦合势非相对论量子色动力学（pNRQCD, potential nonrelativistic QCD）相结合。在速度展开（velocity expansion）的首阶（leading order），所有非微扰效应（除波函数导数在原点平方外）被编码为一个单一的双点色电关联函数（two-point chromoelectric correlator）的普适矩（universal moment）。该矩通过淬火格点QCD计算并借助梯度流（gradient flow）匹配至\overline{\mathrm{MS}}重整化方案得到。

Result: 首次从淬火格点QCD计算确定了双点色电关联函数的普适矩。结合微扰短距离系数和波函数导数在原点平方，该框架成功重现了χ_{cJ}(1P)的观测宽度，并对尚未测量的χ_{bJ}(nP)宽度给出了理论预言。

Conclusion: 所提出的格点QCD结合pNRQCD框架为计算P波重夸克偶素遍举衰变宽度提供了第一性原理途径。该框架可自然推广至普通强子和奇特强子（exotic hadrons）的遍举衰变与产生过程。

Abstract: Inclusive hadronic decay widths remain a long-standing challenge for first-principles QCD. We present a framework combining lattice QCD with strongly-coupled potential nonrelativistic QCD (pNRQCD) to compute inclusive P-wave heavy quarkonium decays to light hadrons. At leading order in the velocity expansion, all nonperturbative effects, apart from the square of the derivative of the wavefunction at the origin, are encoded in a single universal moment of the two-point chromoelectric correlator, which we determine for the first time from a quenched lattice QCD calculation matched to $\overline{\mathrm{MS}}$ via the gradient flow. Combined with perturbative short-distance coefficients and the square of the derivative of the wavefunction at the origin, our result reproduces the observed $χ_{cJ}(1P)$ widths and, at the same time, provides predictions for the unmeasured $χ_{bJ}(nP)$ widths. The framework extends naturally to inclusive decays and production of ordinary and exotic hadrons.

### [83] [Lattice Configuration Generation with a Self-Learning Diffusion Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12587)
*Akio Tomiya*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需外部蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）预生成训练数据即可训练格点场扩散采样器（diffusion sampler）的自举（self-bootstrap）方法——SLDiffusion。该方法通过Metropolis-Hastings校正和自训练流程，在二维紧致XY模型上实现了与独立混合蒙特卡洛（Hybrid Monte Carlo）计算一致的采样结果，且积分自相关时间（integrated autocorrelation time）保持在2以下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于扩散（diffusion）的格点场采样器通常需要依赖外部蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）计算预先准备训练数据，这一过程计算成本高且限制了方法的可扩展性。本文旨在开发一种无需外部预训练数据、能够自举（self-bootstrap）训练的扩散采样器。

Method: 提出SLDiffusion框架：从β=0处的精确采样配置出发，在每个β和噪声水平下，使用带有固定学习得分（learned score）的周期高斯提议（periodic Gaussian proposal）进行Metropolis-Hastings校正，仅利用生成链中回放（replay）的配置来训练下一阶段的得分。在L=4上从β=0.30自训练至0.50，并在更大体积L=8和12上执行体积原生重训练（volume-native retraining）。

Result: 在二维紧致XY模型上，β=0.5时L=4,6,8,12的能量（energy）和涡旋密度（vortex density）与独立混合蒙特卡洛（Hybrid Monte Carlo）计算结果一致（误差在1.35σ以内）。体积原生重训练改善了提议位移（proposal displacement）和自相关（autocorrelation）。所有体积下能量和涡旋密度的积分自相关时间（integrated autocorrelation time）均低于2。

Conclusion: 结果表明，经过Metropolis校正的扩散采样器（Metropolis-corrected diffusion sampler）可以在无需预先从目标耦合（target coupling）中抽取配置的情况下完成自训练，为格点场理论的无监督采样提供了一种新范式。

Abstract: We show that a diffusion sampler for lattice-field configurations can be trained without preparing training data by an external Monte Carlo calculation. Starting from exactly sampled configurations at $β=0$, we construct a self-bootstrap sampler, SLDiffusion, in which periodic Gaussian proposals with a fixed learned score are Metropolis--Hastings corrected, at each $β$, against the same physical target at every noise level, and only replay configurations from the resulting chain are used to train the score at the next stage. In the two-dimensional compact XY model, self-training proceeds from $β=0.30$ to $0.50$ at $L=4$. At $β=0.5$, the energy and vortex densities for $L=4,6,8,12$ agree with independent Hybrid Monte Carlo calculations within $1.35σ$. Volume-native retraining at $L=8$ and $12$ improves both the proposal displacement and autocorrelation. The integrated autocorrelation times of the energy and vortex densities remain below two for all volumes studied. These results demonstrate that a Metropolis-corrected diffusion sampler can be self-trained without configurations drawn in advance from the target coupling.

### [84] [Swarming and Opinion Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12844)
*Rommel Tchinda Djeudjo,Dibakar Ghosh,Timoteo Carletti*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文提出一个耦合群体运动（collective motion）与观点动力学（opinion dynamics）的模型，其中空间运动由吸引-排斥作用（attraction-repulsion interactions）驱动，内部状态由Deffuant型观点模型（Deffuant-type opinion model）描述。研究发现观点动力学的置信阈值（confidence threshold）控制观点簇（opinion clusters）数量，而依赖观点的空间吸引力决定这些簇是空间合并还是分离。对于完全共识态，采用半解析方法推导了使用非线性吸引核时稳态群体分布半径的表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统（multi-agent systems）中，智能体不仅具有空间运动，还具有意见、偏好等内部状态（internal states），这些内部状态通过同伴交互而演化。理解内部状态如何影响集体运动、空间组织如何反过来影响内部动力学，是一个重要挑战。

Method: 建立耦合集体运动与观点动力学的模型。空间动力学由吸引-排斥相互作用控制，内部动力学由Deffuant型观点模型描述。

Result: 观点动力学的置信阈值（confidence threshold）在控制观点簇数量中起关键作用；依赖观点的空间吸引力强度决定这些簇是空间合并还是保持分离。对于完全共识态，采用半解析方法推导了使用非线性吸引核时稳态群体分布半径的表达式。

Conclusion: 该框架可能有助于研究集体决策（collective decision-making）、动物群体行为以及群体机器人（swarm robotics）中的协调策略。

Abstract: Collective dynamics in multi-agent systems provide a powerful framework for understanding how coherent group-level patterns can emerge from simple interactions between individuals. Such phenomena are observed in many natural and artificial systems, including animal groups, robotic swarms, and distributed decision-making processes. In many situations, agents are not only characterized by their spatial motion, but also by internal states, e.g., opinions or preferences, which evolve through interactions with peers. Understanding how these internal states influence collective motion, and how spatial organization in turn affects internal dynamics, remains an important challenge. In this work, we propose a model of coupled collective motion and opinion dynamics. The spatial dynamics are governed by attraction--repulsion interactions, while the internal dynamics are described by a Deffuant-type opinion model. Our results show that the confidence threshold of the opinion dynamics plays a key role in controlling the number of opinion clusters, whereas the strength of the opinion-dependent spatial attraction determines whether these clusters spatially merge or remain separated. In addition, for the full-consensus state, we derive the expression for the radius of the stationary swarm distribution when a nonlinear attraction kernel is used, using a semi-analytical approach. The proposed framework may be useful for studying collective decision-making, animal group behavior, and coordination strategies in swarm robotics.

### [85] [Self-Healing Coordination in Cognitive Swarm Agents with Bloch-Type Perceptual Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11960)
*Jyotiranjan Beuria*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于布洛赫型慢-快架构（Bloch-type slow-fast architecture）的非马尔可夫群体运动模型，通过将感知记忆嵌入慢-快闭环中，显著提升了认知群智能体（cognitive swarm agents）在障碍物干扰后的自愈协调能力（self-healing coordination），而仅解耦的慢速记忆组件则退化为无记忆控制器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的反应式群体运动模型通常直接将局部观测映射为运动指令，忽略了内部感知状态对断裂后恢复过程的影响。本文旨在探索布洛赫型慢-快架构是否能为认知群智能体提供自愈协调能力。

Method: 每个智能体携带一个有界的布洛赫型感知寄存器（bounded Bloch-type perceptual register），该寄存器与一个慢速调控状态（slow regulatory state）耦合，形成闭合的慢-快回路。该布洛赫更新是一种保持非负性的有效动力学（positivity-preserving effective dynamics），用于描述内部感知选择的演化，而非微观量子声称。在非周期性、富含障碍物的无人机迁移任务中，通过多种子消融实验（multi-seed ablations），将完整的慢-快架构与无记忆基线及部分反馈基线进行比较。

Result: 完整慢-快架构的主要功能影响体现在自愈能力上：在障碍物导致的群体碎片化后，闭合的慢-快回路加速了空间连通性的恢复。相比之下，解耦的慢速痕迹（uncoupled slow trace）表现类似无记忆控制器。

Conclusion: 基于布洛赫型慢-快架构的非马尔可夫群体运动模型能够有效增强认知群智能体在复杂环境中的自愈协调能力，而感知记忆必须通过闭环机制运作才能发挥功能价值。

Abstract: Reactive flocking models usually map current local observations directly to motion, leaving limited room for internal perceptual state to shape recovery after disruption. Building on a non-Markovian collective-motion model based on self-regulated perceptual dynamics, we ask whether the Bloch-type slow-fast architecture can support self-healing coordination in cognitive swarm agents. Each agent carries a bounded Bloch-type perceptual register coupled to a slow regulatory state. The slow state is not treated as a standalone memory store; here, perceptual memory is used operationally to denote history-dependent cue resolution within the closed slow-fast loop. The Bloch update is a positivity-preserving effective dynamics for internal perceptual alternatives, not a microscopic quantum claim. We evaluate the architecture in a non-periodic, obstacle-rich drone migration task with finite speed, bounded turning, collision avoidance, altitude regulation, and a fixed migratory drive. Multi-seed ablations compare the full slow-fast architecture with memoryless and partial-feedback baselines using recovery time, largest-cluster restoration, polar order, local coherence, collision risk, and path efficiency. Results show that the main functional impact is on self-healing: after obstacle-induced fragmentation, the closed slow-fast loop accelerates restoration of spatial connectedness, whereas an uncoupled slow trace behaves like a memoryless controller.

### [86] [Symmetry-Twisted Multi-Entropies: Order Parameters for 2D SPT Phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12023)
*Ramanjit Sohal,Michael Levin,Ruben Verresen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一对非局域序参量（nonlocal order parameters），用于检测和区分二维（2D）内部离散阿贝尔酉对称性保护的玻色型对称保护拓扑相（SPTs），通过有效模拟拓扑非平凡时空流形上的SPT路径积分（path integral）来提取拓扑不变量，揭示了多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）作为SPT定义性特征的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管对称保护拓扑相（symmetry-protected topological phases, SPTs）可以通过其纠缠性质（entanglement properties）加以区分，但在一维（1D）情形之外，如何直接从期望值（expectation values）中提取这一信息尚不清楚。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 提出一对非局域序参量，通过有效模拟拓扑非平凡时空流形上的SPT路径积分（path integral）来提取所需拓扑不变量（topological invariants）。这些序参量定义为对有限空间区域中固定数量系统副本（replicas）施加的对称性部分操作（partial symmetry）和置换操作（permutation operations）的期望值，对应于多体纠缠量——即多熵（multi-entropies）的对称性扭曲（symmetry-twisted）版本。

Result: 两个序参量分别检测对称保护的四体纠缠（four-party entanglement）和六体纠缠（six-party entanglement），并约束了可能的“虚假（spurious）”贡献。在不动点格点模型（fixed-point lattice models）中进行了分析性检验。

Conclusion: 结果表明多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）是SPTs的一个定义性特征（defining feature）。预期该方法可推广至费米子（fermionic）系统及更高维（higher-dimensional）系统。

Abstract: Although symmetry-protected topological phases (SPTs) can be distinguished by their entanglement properties, it has been unclear how to extract this information directly from expectation values beyond the 1D case. Here, we close this gap and propose a pair of nonlocal order parameters that can detect and distinguish all bosonic SPTs in 2D protected by internal discrete, Abelian unitary symmetries. The desired topological invariants are extracted by these quantities by effectively simulating the SPT path integral on topologically non-trivial spacetime manifolds. Our order parameters are defined in terms of expectation values of partial symmetry and permutation operations acting on fixed numbers of replicas of the system in finite spatial regions. These expectation values correspond to symmetry-twisted versions of multipartite entanglement quantities known as multi-entropies. We show explicitly that our two order parameters detect symmetry-protected four-party and six-party entanglement, respectively, and we constrain possible "spurious" contributions. We analytically test our proposal in fixed-point lattice models. Our results suggest multipartite entanglement to be a defining feature of SPTs; indeed, we expect our methods to generalize to fermionic and higher-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [87] [Mapping vortices to anyons in toric code phases of generalized Kitaev models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12027)
*Li Ern Chern,Roderich Moessner,Claudio Castelnovo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套将通量激发（涡旋）映射为电、磁粒子的理论，适用于二维Kitaev蜂窝模型推广的环面码（toric code）相。该方法基于马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermion）表示、阿贝尔任意子（Abelian anyon）融合规则和费米子奇偶性约束，证明了在费米子能隙不闭合的条件下任意子映射保持不变，并揭示了同一平凡陈数（Chern number）相内不同映射区域的分界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Kitaev蜂窝模型的推广中，通量激发（涡旋）与电/磁粒子之间的映射关系尚缺乏统一、系统的理论描述，尤其是在一般模型参数下（包括微扰极限）如何建立该映射、以及任意子种类在参数演化下是否保持不变等问题尚未解决。

Method: 采用马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermion）表示，利用阿贝尔任意子（Abelian anyon）的融合规则以及费米子奇偶性（fermion parity）的物理约束，构建了一套通用的映射理论。该方法适用于任意模型参数，包括二聚体极限（dimer limit）等微扰情形。

Result: 成功复现了二聚体极限下已知的映射方案；推导出单个涡旋的任意子种类不变性条件；证明在无涡旋和双涡旋扇区的费米子能隙不闭合的条件下，任意子映射在模型参数的连续演化下保持不变；从而能够在同一具有平凡陈数（trivial Chern number）的相内精确划分多个与不同映射相关的区域。通过方八边形晶格（square-octagon lattice）和具有Kekulé结构的蜂窝晶格上的大量计算进行了验证；展示了不同的任意子映射可以表现出相同的弱对称性破缺（weak symmetry breaking），并论证其属于相同的对称性 enriched 拓扑序（symmetry-enriched topological order）。

Conclusion: 该理论为Kitaev模型推广中的涡旋-粒子映射提供了统一的框架，明确了任意子映射在参数变化下的稳定性条件，并揭示了同一拓扑相内部可存在多种不同的任意子映射分区，且这些分区可共享相同的对称性 enriched 拓扑序（symmetry-enriched topological order）。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive theory of mapping flux excitations, or vortices, to electric and magnetic particles in the toric code phases of generalizations of the Kitaev honeycomb model in two spatial dimensions. Our method, which is formulated with the Majorana fermion representation, utilizes the fusion rule of the Abelian anyons and the physical constraint on the fermion parity, and applies to generic model parameters including any perturbative limit. Not only are we able to reproduce the known mapping scheme in the dimer limit, we also derive the conditions for the invariance of anyon species of individual vortices. We prove that the mapping of anyons is left unchanged by any continuous evolution of model parameters that does not close the fermion gap in both the vortex-free and two-vortex sectors, which enables precise demarcations between multiple regimes associated with different maps within a single phase characterized by a trivial Chern number. We illustrate our theory via extensive computations for a number of selected models, in particular those defined on the square-octagon lattice and the honeycomb lattice with a Kekulé structure. We also demonstrate that distinct mappings of anyons can nevertheless exhibit the same weak symmetry breaking, and further argue that they belong to the same symmetry-enriched topological order.

Conclusion: 该研究首次系统建立了上临界维度下边界有限尺寸标度的对数修正理论，蒙特卡洛数据定量支持了理论预测，填补了边界临界性中对数修正效应的研究空白。

Abstract: At the bulk upper critical dimension, marginally irrelevant interactions generate multiplicative logarithmic corrections to mean-field scaling. While these corrections are well understood for bulk observables, their consequences for boundary criticality, particularly for finite-size scaling, remain much less explored. Here we combine large-scale quantum Monte Carlo simulations with boundary renormalization-group analysis to study a (3 + 1)D O(3) quantum critical point. After verifying the known logarithmically modified bulk finite-size scaling, including the correlation-length scaling governed by the logarithmic finite-size exponent \hat{\coppa}, we tune the surface coupling to identify ordinary, special, and extraordinary boundary regimes. For the ordinary and special transitions, we derive logarithmic correction exponents and \hat{\coppa}-dependent finite-size scaling forms for boundary correlations, including results that have not been systematically established before. These predictions are quantitatively supported by Monte Carlo data. In the extraordinary regime, we find long-range surface magnetic order and a logarithmically enhanced surface-bulk correlation.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在先前的透射电子显微镜（TEM）和角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）研究中，LaTe2及其元素替代相LaTe2-xSbx中观测到的复杂衍射特征尚未得到合理解释，亟需进一步的微观表征来阐明这些未解特征。

Method: 本研究采用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM），在9 K低温下对LaTe1.6Sb0.4晶体表面进行实空间成像，以直接观测电荷密度波（CDW）调制结构。

Result: 观测到三种交织的电荷密度波（CDW）波矢：q1=8/11a*、q2=5/11a* 和 q3=3/11a*，它们由未占据态中的空穴掺杂（hole doping）诱导产生。其中q1和q3被理论验证为连接px和py能带的嵌套矢量（nesting vectors）。此外，还检测到对应于11a超晶格（11-a-superlattice）的、围绕主布拉格点（Bragg spots）p的卫星斑点。

Conclusion: 这些发现为进一步探索空穴/电子掺杂材料中交织电荷密度波（CDW）的起源提供了关键的实验依据和理论见解。

Abstract: Multiple CDW-ordered layered rare-earth tellurides have increasingly emerged as a research hotspot, owing to their unconventional CDW formation, high transition temperature, and confirmed existence of axial Higgs modes. Recently, interweaved CDW in LaTe2 and its element-substituted phase LaTe2-xSbx have been investigated through TEM and ARPES measurements, revealing their distinct origins. Nevertheless, several complex diffraction features observed in TEM patterns remain unelucidated. In this work, we carried out scanning tunneling microscopy (STM) on LaTe1.6Sb0.4 crystals at 9 K. Three interweaved CDW wave vectors, q1=8/11a*, q2=5/11a* and q3=3/11a* were observed, which are induced by hole doping in unoccupied states. The q1 and q3 are theoretically verified to be nesting vectors connecting px- and py- bands. Furthermore, the satellite spots relative to the main Bragg spots p corresponding to a 11-a-superlattice have also been detected. Our findings provide critical insights for further exploring the origin of the interweaved CDW in hole/electron doping materials.

### [90] [Giant magnetocaloric effect at low fields in triangular-lattice NdMgAl$_{11}$O$_{19}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12262)
*Yantao Cao,He Sun,Zhendong Fu,Zhaoming Tian,Huiqian Luo,Junsen Xiang,Peijie Sun,Jinkui Zhao,Hanjie Guo*

TL;DR: 本文研究了六铝酸盐NdMgAl$_{11}$O$_{19}$，发现其Nd$^{3+}$离子形成的三角晶格体系在50~mK以下仍保持量子自旋液体（QSL）态，并展现出优异的磁制冷性能：仅需2~T磁场变化即可从1.9~K降温至113~mK。其卓越的制冷性能归因于类QSL基态持续的自旋涨落、大有效g因子以及沿易轴方向的小交换相互作用。

Method: 对六铝酸盐NdMgAl$_{11}$O$_{19}$进行磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）和比热（specific heat）测量以表征其基态；采用准绝热退磁（quasi-adiabatic demagnetization）测量评估其制冷性能。

Result: 磁化率和比热测量表明样品在50~mK以下保持磁动力学态（magnetically dynamic state），与QSL态一致；比热测量进一步揭示50~mK以下仍保留大量磁熵。准绝热退磁测试显示仅需2~T的磁场变化即可从1.9~K降温至113~mK，表现出优异的制冷性能。

Conclusion: NdMgAl$_{11}$O$_{19}$的出色制冷性能归因于类QSL基态中的持续自旋涨落（persistent spin fluctuations）、大有效g因子以及沿易轴方向的小交换相互作用。该研究证明，在稀土磁体中结合阻挫（frustration）、强自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和晶格电场效应（crystal-electric-field effect），可为下一代低温磁制冷工质提供可行的设计原理。

Abstract: Magnetic refrigeration in the sub-Kelvin regime requires refrigerant materials to retain a large magnetic entropy at low temperatures by suppressing magnetic ordering. Quantum spin liquids (QSLs), which evade long-range magnetic ordering while retaining strong quantum fluctuations to the lowest temperatures, therefore provide a promising platform for realizing high-performance magnetic refrigerants. Here, we investigate the magnetic ground state and the magnetocaloric effect of the hexaaluminate, NdMgAl$_{11}$O$_{19}$, in which the Nd$^{3+}$ ions form a network of triangular lattices. Magnetic susceptibility and specific heat measurements indicate a magnetically dynamic state down to 50~mK, consistent with a QSL state. Specific heat measurements further reveal substantial magnetic entropy retained below 50~mK. Quasi-adiabatic demagnetization measurements demonstrate a superior cooling performance of NdMgAl$_{11}$O$_{19}$, which can be cooled to 113~mK from 1.9~K by only a small magnetic field change of 2~T. The outstanding refrigeration performance is attributed to the persistent spin fluctuations associated with the QSL-like ground state, together with a large effective \textit{g} factor and the smallness of the exchange interactions along the easy-axis direction. This study demonstrates that frustration, combined with strong spin-orbit coupling and crystal-electric-field effect in the rare earth magnets provides a promising design principle for next-generation cryogenic magnetic refrigerants.

### [91] [Zero-Field Long Range Order at $T \sim 40$ mK in the Proximate Quantum Spin Ice Ce$_2$Sn$_2$O$_7$ and Phase Diagram for Magnetic Fields Along [1,1,0]](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12274)
*E. M. Smith,M. S. Powell,R. Schäfer,A. P. Dioguardi,J. W. Kolis,R. Movshovich,B. D. Gaulin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过极低温热容测量，发现Ce₂Sn₂O₇单晶在零场下存在约0.04 K的一级相变进入长程有序态，证明其并非量子自旋冰（quantum spin ice, QSI）基态；但磁场调控实验表明自旋冰物理仍然邻近且相关。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清Ce₂Sn₂O₇是否具有量子自旋冰（quantum spin ice, QSI）基态的争议。此前该材料因其偶极-八极（dipole-octupole）特征和XYZ近邻模型哈密顿量而被认为是QSI的有力候选者。

Method: 采用水热法（hydrothermal techniques）生长高质量Ce₂Sn₂O₇单晶，并进行极低温热容测量；在零场和沿[1,1,0]方向施加不同强度磁场的条件下观测比热行为。

Result: 零场下在约0.04 K观察到清晰的一级相变（first order transition）进入长程有序，该温度远低于Ce基烧绿石中常见的肖特基型（Schottky-like）宽峰下降位置；沿[1,1,0]施加磁场后，该峰演化为高温处的弱连续平均场（mean field）相变异常，更高场下肖特基型异常分裂为类似经典自旋冰中独立极化α和正交β链的行为。

Conclusion: Ce₂Sn₂O₇在零场下并非QSI基态，但磁场调控显示自旋冰物理邻近且对该材料仍具相关性；Ce基烧绿石的相图比先前认识更为丰富。

Abstract: The Ce$^{3+}$ pseudospin-1/2 degrees of freedom in the pyrochlore magnets Ce$_2$X$_2$O$_7$, with $X$ = Zr, Hf, or Sn, possess dipole-octupole character. The XYZ nearest-neighbor model Hamiltonians which have successfully described their properties make them attractive candidates for quantum spin ice ground states. We report new heat capacity measurements to very low temperatures on a high-quality single crystal of Ce$_2$Sn$_2$O$_7$ grown by hydrothermal techniques. Our zero-field measurements uncover a clear first order transition to long-ranged order at $T \sim 0.04$ K, well below the downturn in the broader Schottky-like anomaly that is a common feature in the zero-field heat capacity for cerium pyrochlores. This observation settles the debate as to whether Ce$_2$Sn$_2$O$_7$ possesses a QSI ground state in zero field - it does not. However, we also find compelling evidence suggesting that spin ice physics is nearby, and remains relevant to Ce$_2$Sn$_2$O$_7$. Application of a magnetic field along the $[1,1,0]$ direction leads to an evolution of this peak to a weak anomaly at higher temperature more characteristic of a continuous, mean field transition. At higher fields along $[1,1,0]$, the Schottky-like anomaly bifurcates similar to expectations for independent polarized $α$ and orthogonal $β$ chains in classical spin ice. These new experimental results demonstrate richness to the phase diagram for Ce-based pyrochlores.

### [92] [Measurement-induced phase transition in space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12386)
*Jia-Qiang Li,Liang-Jun Zhai,Shuo Liu,Shuai Yin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过在一个受监测的克利福德链（Clifford chain）上施加确定性测量梯度，实现了测量诱导相变（measurement-induced phase transition, MIPT）的空间实现。单一稳态中同时存在体积律、临界和面积律区域，空间协议避免了Kibble-Zurek动力学，并可直接提取关联长度指数ν。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的测量诱导相变（MIPT）研究通常依赖于在不同的均匀测量概率下制备稳态，缺乏在单一稳态中直接观测临界行为的空间实现方案。本文旨在引入一种空间非均匀测量梯度来构造并探测MIPT。

Method: 在单个受监测的克利福德链（Clifford chain）上施加确定性的测量概率梯度，使得测量概率在空间中线性变化。通过扫描该空间中不同位置的纠缠可观测量（entanglement observables），分析其空间标度行为。

Result: 所得稳态中同时存在体积律（volume-law）、临界（critical）和面积律（area-law）区域，其中测量概率p(x) = p_c的点充当空间临界切口（spatial critical cut）。该结构受空间标度形式（spatial scaling form）支配，其物理边界0≤p≤1施加了一个有限线性窗口，产生截断控制（cutoff-controlled）的渐近区域，拟合指数可直接获得关联长度指数ν（correlation-length exponent）。

Conclusion: 空间非均匀测量为在单一稳态中工程化和探测测量诱导临界性（measurement-induced criticality）提供了一种可控途径。该空间协议没有Kibble-Zurek动力学，且与时间驱动MIPT的有限时间标度（finite-time scaling）在结构上类似但机制不同。

Abstract: Measurement-induced phase transitions (MIPTs) in monitored quantum circuits are usually characterized by preparing steady states at different uniform measurement probabilities. Here we introduce a spatial realization of the MIPT by imposing a deterministic measurement gradient in a single monitored Clifford chain. The resulting steady state contains coexisting volume-law, critical, and area-law regions, with the point $p(x)=p_c$ acting as a spatial critical cut. By scanning entanglement observables across this profile, we show that the transition is organized by a spatial scaling form. Although this structure is analogous to finite-time scaling in temporally driven MIPT, the spatial protocol has no Kibble-Zurek dynamics. Instead, the physical bounds $0\le p\le 1$ impose a finite linear window, producing cutoff-controlled asymptotic regimes whose fitted exponents provide direct access to the correlation-length exponent $ν$. Our results establish spatially inhomogeneous measurements as a controlled route to engineer and probe measurement-induced criticality within a single steady state.

### [93] [Fractionalized Fermi liquids with the ghost-Gutzwiller Ansatz](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12410)
*Ivan Pasqua,Carlos Mejuto-Zaera,Michele Fabrizio*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过一个简单的 ghost-Gutzwiller 尝试波函数（ghost-Gutzwiller Ansatz）在单带 t-J 模型中展示了分数化费米液体（FL*）相的出现，并在平均场计算成本下进行了优化。所得的温度-掺杂相图包含低掺杂的 FL*、d波超导穹顶和过掺杂的常规费米液体，再现了铜氧化物现象学的关键定性特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数化费米液体（fractionalized Fermi liquids, FL*）是一种难以捉摸的金属态，其特点是存在分数化准粒子（fractionalized quasiparticles）与常规准粒子共存，并且违背了 Luttinger 定理。这类相被认为是欠掺杂铜氧化物（underdoped cuprates）赝能隙区（pseudogap regime）的主要候选者。本研究旨在从微观模型出发展示 FL* 相的出现及其与铜氧化物相图的关系。

Method: 采用简单的 ghost-Gutzwiller 尝试波函数（ghost-Gutzwiller Ansatz），并在平均场（mean-field）计算成本下进行优化，在单带 t-J 模型（single-band $t$-$J$ model）中研究 FL* 相的出现。

Result: 得到的温度-掺杂（temperature-doping）相图包含三个主要区域：低掺杂的 FL* 相、d波超导穹顶（$d$-wave superconducting dome）以及过掺杂的常规费米液体（conventional Fermi liquid）。该相图再现了铜氧化物（cuprate）现象学的关键定性特征。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，FL* 相可以作为单带 t-J 模型中的一种可实现相出现，并且其与 d波超导和常规费米液体共同构成的相图与铜氧化物的实验现象在定性上一致，为理解欠掺杂铜氧化物的赝能隙行为提供了理论支持。

Abstract: Fractionalized Fermi liquids ($\mathrm{FL}^{\!*}$), elusive metallic states characterized by fractionalized quasiparticles alongside conventional ones and defying Luttinger's theorem, are prime candidates for the pseudogap regime of underdoped cuprates. We show that a $\mathrm{FL}^{\!*}$ phase emerges in the single-band $t$-$J$ model through a simple ghost-Gutzwiller Ansatz, optimized at the cost of a mean-field calculation. The resulting temperature-doping phase diagram encompasses a low-doping $\mathrm{FL}^{\!*}$, a $d$-wave superconducting dome, and an overdoped conventional Fermi liquid, thereby reproducing key qualitative features of cuprate phenomenology.

### [94] [Research on topological materials using ultrafast spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12536)
*Hao Liu,Jian-Qiao Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文综述了超快泵浦-探测光谱技术（ultrafast pump-probe spectroscopy）在拓扑绝缘体、拓扑半金属和磁性拓扑材料等拓扑材料（topological materials）非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium dynamics）研究中的进展，涵盖光激发弛豫路径、自旋极化动力学、光致拓扑相变（photoinduced topological phase transitions）等关键机制，并展望了多维超快光谱与理论建模相结合的未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑材料以其对称性保护的非平庸能带结构（如狄拉克锥和韦尔节点）展现出丰富的量子现象，在量子输运、自旋电子学和非线性光学中具有应用潜力。超快泵浦-探测光谱因其飞秒时间分辨率，能够追踪电荷、自旋、轨道和晶格相互作用在固有时间尺度上的演化，从而揭示拓扑相中的关键耦合机制，这构成了综述的核心动机。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，系统梳理了超快光谱学在拓扑绝缘体、拓扑半金属和磁性拓扑材料中的研究成果。具体讨论了光激发表面和体态电子态的弛豫路径（包括电子-声子散射、表面-体态电荷转移和超快自旋转换）、狄拉克和韦尔半金属中的粒子数反转、倾斜韦尔能带相关的自旋极化动力学，以及磁有序对拓扑态的影响（如相干声子和磁子激发、磁驱动的拓扑转变和太赫兹发射）。还综述了光致拓扑相变，涵盖电子关联、晶格畸变和磁有序在强光激发下的驱动机制。

Result: 综述指出，超快泵浦-探测光谱已在拓扑材料中识别出多种非平衡过程，包括电子-声子散射驱动的弛豫、表面-体态电荷转移、超快自旋转换、狄拉克和韦尔半金属中的粒子数反转、倾斜韦尔能带引起的自旋极化动力学，以及磁有序诱导的拓扑转变和太赫兹发射。此外，在强光激发下，电子关联、晶格畸变和磁有序均可驱动光致拓扑相变，为实现量子相的非热控（nonthermal control）提供了路径。

Conclusion: 本文总结了超快光谱在拓扑量子材料非平衡态研究中的现状，并指出未来发展方向：结合具有时间、能量、动量和自旋分辨率的多维超快光谱（multidimensional ultrafast spectroscopy）与先进理论建模，建立非平衡拓扑态的统一图景。该综述旨在为拓扑量子材料的超快研究提供参考，并推动其在高速低功耗信息处理、自旋电子学和量子技术中的应用。

Abstract: Topological materials, characterized by symmetry-protected nontrivial band structures such as Dirac cones and Weyl nodes, host diverse quantum phenomena, with potential applications in quantum transport, spintronics, and nonlinear optics. Ultrafast pump-probe spectroscopy has emerged as a powerful tool for exploring nonequilibrium dynamics in these systems. Its femtosecond resolution allows charge, spin, orbital, and lattice interactions to be tracked on their intrinsic timescales, thereby revealing key coupling mechanisms in topological phases. This review summarizes progress in ultrafast spectroscopic studies of topological insulators, topological semimetals, and magnetic topological materials. We first discuss the relaxation pathways of photoexcited surface and bulk electronic states, emphasizing electron-phonon scattering, surface-bulk charge transfer, and ultrafast spin conversion. We then examine population inversion in Dirac and Weyl semimetals, spin-polarization dynamics associated with tilted Weyl bands, and the effects of magnetic order on topological states, including coherent phonon and magnon excitations, magnetically driven topological transitions, and terahertz emission. We further review photoinduced topological phase transitions driven by electronic correlations, lattice distortions, and magnetic order under intense optical excitation, highlighting routes toward nonthermal control of quantum phases. Finally, we outline future directions that combine multidimensional ultrafast spectroscopy with temporal, energy, momentum, and spin resolution and advanced theoretical modeling to establish a unified picture of nonequilibrium topological states. This review aims to provide a useful reference for ultrafast studies of topological quantum materials and to advance their applications in high-speed, low-power information processing, spintronics, and quantum technologies.

### [95] [Halogen control of magnetic competition in Kitaev candidate Ru$X_3$ ($X =$ Cl, Br)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12595)
*Ryuta Iwazaki,Shinnosuke Koyama,Takashi Koretsune,Shintaro Hoshino,Joji Nasu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从第一性原理（first-principles）计算出发，构建多轨道哈伯德模型，进而推导出有效的赝自旋模型，用于研究RuCl₃和RuBr₃的磁态。

Result: RuBr₃相比RuCl₃具有更扩展的瓦尼尔轨道和更强的层间交换相互作用（interlayer exchange interaction），这些相互作用增强了三维关联性（three-dimensional correlation），与实验推断的RuBr₃更强的反铁磁性（antiferromagnetic tendency）一致。此外，轨道依赖的库仑各向异性进一步降低了铁磁态（ferromagnetic state）与锯齿形态（zigzag state）之间的能量差。

Conclusion: 卤素取代通过层间交换相互作用和轨道依赖的库仑相互作用效应，调控RuX₃中的磁竞争。该工作为理解RuX₃家族中磁性质的化学调控提供了微观理论依据。

Abstract: The spin-orbital Mott insulators Ru$X_3$ ($X =$ Cl, Br) have attracted considerable attention as promising candidate materials for realizing a Kitaev spin liquid. In this study, we construct effective pseudospin models from multiorbital Hubbard models derived from first-principles calculations and investigate the magnetic states of RuCl$_3$ and RuBr$_3$. From the constructed effective models, we find that RuBr$_3$ has more extended Wannier orbitals and stronger interlayer exchange interactions than RuCl$_3$. These interactions enhance three-dimensional correlations, consistent with the stronger antiferromagnetic tendency experimentally inferred for RuBr$_3$. Orbital-dependent Coulomb anisotropy further reduces the energy difference between ferromagnetic and zigzag states. Our results clarify how halogen substitution controls magnetic competition in Ru$X_3$ through interlayer exchange interactions and effects of orbital-dependent Coulomb interactions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过等价位点替代（isovalent substitution）在Ca₃(Ru₁₋ₓTiₓ)₂O₇中实现带宽控制的Mott绝缘体相；利用仅1%的Ti掺杂使体系自由能景观（free energy landscape）异常平坦，磁学和输运性质对外部扰动高度敏感，从而为系统研究磁场诱导的相变提供了理想平台。

Method: 对Ca₃(Ru₀.₉₉Ti₀.₀₁)₂O₇单晶进行系统的磁化与电阻测量，沿易轴b轴和a轴分别施加磁场，构建磁场的H-T相图，观测自旋翻转转变和强迫铁磁金属相的出现条件。

Result: 沿b轴施加磁场时，在约6 T处发生一级自旋翻转（first-order spin-flop）转变，电阻下降但仍保持绝缘；在10.5 T以上所有Ru磁矩与b轴对齐，进入强迫铁磁金属相（forced ferromagnetic metallic phase）。沿a轴施加时，直至14 T均未观测到上述两种相变。

Conclusion: 尽管电子动能和电子-晶格耦合对自由能平衡有贡献，Ca₃(Ru₀.₉₉Ti₀.₀₁)₂O₇的H-T相图意外地简单，与经典各向异性反铁磁体（canonical anisotropic antiferromagnet）的相图高度相似，但临界场（critical fields）发生了显著的重整化。

Abstract: A bandwidth-controlled antiferromagnetic Mott-insulating phase in Ca$_3$(Ru$_{1-x}$Ti$_x$)$_2$O$_7$ is realized through isovalent substitution at the Ru site. For a dilute substitution with only 1% Ti, the Mott insulator ground state remains nearly degenerate with the ground state of pristine Ca$_3$Ru$_2$O$_7$, where the Ru moments are ferromagnetically aligned within the metallic RuO$_2$ bilayers stacked in an antiferromagnetic fashion. The exceptionally shallow free energy landscape of this doped compound arises from intertwined electron-electron and electron-lattice interactions. This makes its magnetic and transport properties highly sensitive to external perturbations. We systematically investigated magnetic-field-induced phase switching in Ca$_3$(Ru$_{0.99}$Ti$_{0.01}$)$_2$O$_7$ to explore its magnetic $H$-$T$ phase diagram. With the field applied along the easy $b$-axis, parallel to the antiferromagnetic moments, the magnetization exhibits a first-order spin-flop transition at $\approx $ 6 T, indicating reorientation of the Ru moments perpendicular to the field. The transition is accompanied by a decrease in the electrical resistance, but the spin-flop phase remains insulating. Above 10.5 T, all Ru moments align with the $b$-axis, resulting in a forced ferromagnetic metallic phase. In contrast, neither spin-flop nor forced-ferromagnetic phases are observed up to 14 T, when the field is applied along the $a$-axis. While the electronic kinetic energy and the electron-lattice coupling contribute to the free-energy balance of this system, the resulting $H$-$T$ phase diagram is remarkably simple and closely resembles that of a canonical anisotropic antiferromagnet, albeit with substantially renormalized critical fields.

</details>


### [97] [Emergent $s+id$ Superconductivity from the Interplay between Electronic Correlations and Electron-Phonon Coupling in $\mathrm{R}_{1-x}\mathrm{Sr}_x\mathrm{NiO}_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12773)
*Zi Yuan,Jun Zhan,Xianxin Wu,Shaozhi Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算与涨落交换-Migdal-Eliashberg理论（fluctuation-exchange-Migdal-Eliashberg theory）相结合，研究发现无限层镍酸盐中自旋涨落（spin fluctuations）和电子-声子相互作用（electron-phonon interactions）的竞争导致了空间不均匀的s+id超导态，为实验观察到的空间变化超导对称性提供了解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期无限层镍酸盐的隧道测量实验揭示了空间变化的超导对称性（spatially varying superconducting symmetries），但其微观起源尚不清楚，这构成了本研究的核心动机。

Method: 将第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与涨落交换-Migdal-Eliashberg理论（fluctuation-exchange-Migdal-Eliashberg theory）相结合，研究电子关联（electron correlations）与电子-声子相互作用在无限层镍酸盐中的耦合效应。

Result: 自旋涨落在Ni d_{x^2-y^2}轨道上诱导稳健的d波超导（d-wave superconductivity），而电子-声子耦合在间隙轨道（interstitial orbital）上诱导s波配对（s-wave pairing），形成s+id超导态。该s+id态具有强载流子密度依赖性：当电子-声子耦合强度λ=0.4时，在n=0.9下稳定存在，在n=0.8下则不稳定。

Conclusion: 局部氧缺陷（local oxygen defects）调节局域电子密度并形成具有不同配对对称性的有限尺寸区域（finite-size domains），为实验中观察到的空间不均匀超导对称性提供了有说服力的解释。

Abstract: Recent tunneling measurements on infinite-layer nickelates have revealed spatially varying superconducting symmetries, whose microscopic origin remains unclear. Motivated by this observation, we investigate the interplay between electron correlations and electron-phonon interactions in infinite-layer nickelates by combining first-principles calculations with the fluctuation-exchange-Migdal-Eliashberg theory. Our calculations show that spin fluctuations yield robust $d$-wave superconductivity on the Ni $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital, whereas electron-phonon coupling induces $s$-wave pairing on an interstitial orbital, leading to an $s+id$ superconducting state. The emergence of the $s$-wave component is strongly carrier-density dependent: an intermediate electron-phonon coupling of $λ=0.4$ stabilizes the $s+id$ state at $n=0.9$ but not at $n=0.8$. These results imply that local oxygen defects tune the local electron density and form finite-size domains with distinct pairing symmetries, offering a compelling explanation for the spatially inhomogeneous superconducting symmetries observed in experiments.

</details>


### [98] [Phase-shifted multicomponent spin-charge nematicity in an altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12824)
*Christopher Candelora,Siyu Cheng,Muxian Xu,Keyu Zeng,Hengxin Tan,Younghun Hwang,Binghai Yan,Federico Mazzola,Ziqiang Wang,Ilija Zeljkovic*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文报告在Co0.25NbSe2中发现交变磁向列性（altermagnetic nematicity），这是一种多组分电子液晶（electronic liquid-crystal）序的新形式。通过STM和自旋极化STM实验发现，零场下三个名义上C3对称的方向在电荷和自旋通道中都失去了旋转等价性，且自旋敏感分量相对于电荷敏感分量发生了相位移动。唯象理论表明，交变磁序（altermagnetic order）倾向于在电荷与自旋向列性分量之间产生有限相对相位，而C3晶格钉扎（C3 lattice pinning）阻止了这一偏移并选择了观察到的相位锁定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）具有自旋劈裂费米面（spin-split Fermi surfaces）但不产生净磁化，这种固有地多组分电子环境促使研究者探索其能否催生具有非常规自旋-电荷结构的关联电子相（correlated electron phases）。

Method: 采用光谱成像扫描隧穿显微镜（spectroscopic-imaging scanning tunneling microscopy, SI-STM）和自旋极化扫描隧穿显微镜（spin-polarized scanning tunneling microscopy, SP-STM）对Co0.25NbSe2进行实验测量。结合唯象理论（phenomenological theory）分析交变磁序对电荷和自旋向列性分量的耦合作用。

Result: 实验发现，在零场状态下，三个名义上C3相关的方向在电荷敏感和自旋敏感隧穿通道中都失去了旋转等价性。自旋敏感的主导分量相对于电荷敏感的主导分量发生了整体偏移，偏移量为一个C3扇区（one C3 sector），揭示了相位移动的自旋-电荷向列响应（phase-shifted spin-charge nematic response）。

Conclusion: 交变磁向列性是一种新的多组分电子液晶序形式。交变磁体为将传统关联电子相转变为受对称性调控的自旋-电荷序（symmetry-engineered spin-charge orders）提供了潜在的通路。

Abstract: Altermagnets host spin-split Fermi surfaces without net magnetization. This intrinsically multicomponent electronic setting raises the possibility that familiar correlated electron phases acquire unconventional spin-charge structure. Here we report the discovery of altermagnetic nematicity in Co0.25NbSe2. Using spectroscopic-imaging scanning tunneling microscopy and spin-polarized scanning tunneling microscopy, we find that the three nominally C3-related directions lose rotational equivalence in the zero-field state, in both charge and spin-sensitive tunneling channels. Strikingly, the dominant spin-sensitive component is shifted by one C3 sector relative to the dominant charge component, revealing a phase-shifted spin-charge nematic response. A phenomenological theory shows that altermagnetic order favors a finite relative phase between the charge and spin-sensitive nematic components -- C3 lattice pinning frustrates this preferred offset and selects the observed phase locking. These results establish altermagnetic nematicity as a new form of multicomponent electronic liquid-crystal order and point to a potentially generic route by which altermagnets can transform conventional correlated phases into symmetry-engineered spin-charge orders.

</details>


### [99] [Microscopic Spin-1 Parent Hamiltonians for Emergent Valence-Bond Loop Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12925)
*Hari Borutta,Yasir Iqbal,Kirill Shtengel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文构造了棋盘和烧绿石晶格上自旋-1的精确父哈密顿量，其基态为完全填充的单态环流形，为约束价键物理提供了微观自旋模型起点，并揭示了低能下烧绿石情形可映射为金刚石晶格上的自旋-1/2 XY模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通常环或二聚体约束是作为Rokhsar–Kivelson有效描述引入的，缺乏微观自旋哈密顿量的严格基础。本文旨在构建自旋-1的精确父哈密顿量，使其基态流形自然产生约束价键环态，从而建立从微观磁体到环/二聚体/规范理论描述的严格联系。

Method: 哈密顿量由作用于三角面上的正半定投影子（positive-semidefinite projectors）构成，每个投影子仅移除一个三角形的最大极化态，因此模型无挫折（frustration-free）。通过类似AKLT的构造，将每个自旋-1分解为两个虚拟自旋-1/2自由度，在交叉的方格或四面体内形成单态，再通过投影恢复物理自旋-1希尔伯特空间。

Result: 基态为角共享晶格上的完全填充单态环态（fully packed singlet-loop states），自旋关联由环连通性决定。棋盘与烧绿石情形差异显著：烧绿石晶格上四面体对称性消除了局域偏置项，主导的次近邻海森堡微扰在四面体中心构成的金刚石晶格上产生自旋-1/2 XY模型。

Conclusion: 该工作为二维和三维约束价键物理提供了精确的自旋-1微观起点，展示了如何从小自旋、SU(2)不变的阻挫磁体出发趋近环、二聚体和规范理论描述。

Abstract: We construct an exact spin-$1$ parent Hamiltonian for constrained valence-bond loop manifolds on the checkerboard and pyrochlore lattices. The Hamiltonian is local, SU(2)- and time-reversal-invariant, and built from positive-semidefinite projectors acting on triangular faces. Each projector removes only the maximally polarized state of a triangle, so the model is frustration-free. Its zero-energy states are generated by an AKLT-like construction in which each spin-$1$ moment is resolved into two virtual spin-$\tfrac12$ degrees of freedom, singlets are formed inside every crossed plaquette or tetrahedron, and the physical spin-$1$ Hilbert space is recovered by projection. The resulting ground states are fully packed singlet-loop states on the corner-sharing lattice. Thus, a loop or dimer constraint, usually introduced as part of an effective Rokhsar--Kivelson description, appears here as the exact zero-energy manifold of a microscopic spin Hamiltonian. We analyze spin correlations within this manifold and show that, for a fixed loop covering, they are determined by loop connectivity. We also project symmetry-allowed perturbations into the ground-state manifold and derive the resulting low-energy pseudospin dynamics. The checkerboard and pyrochlore cases differ sharply. On the pyrochlore lattice, tetrahedral symmetry removes simple local bias terms, and the leading nontrivial next-nearest-neighbour Heisenberg perturbation gives an emergent spin-$\tfrac12$ XY model on the diamond lattice of tetrahedron centers. These results give an exact spin-$1$ microscopic starting point for constrained valence-bond physics in two and three dimensions, and show how loop, dimer, and gauge-theoretic descriptions can be approached from a small-spin, SU(2)-invariant frustrated magnet.

</details>

### [100] [Density evolution at fluid-fluid interfaces: A generalized Gibbs-Duhem theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11988)
*Fei Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了一个包含动力学贡献的广义吉布斯-杜亥姆框架（generalized Gibbs-Duhem framework），从而在经典热力学与牛顿力学之间建立了统一联系；基于该框架，进一步提出了控制流-流界面处密度动力学的替代演化方程，该方程在适当极限下能自然还原声速定义、伯努利定律（Bernoulli's law）和范德瓦尔斯状态方程（van der Waals equation of state）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典吉布斯-杜亥姆关系（Gibbs-Duhem relation）仅适用于准静态过程（quasi-static processes），忽略了动力学效应，导致吉布斯热力学（Gibbs thermodynamics）与牛顿力学（Newtonian mechanics）之间存在根本性鸿沟。本文旨在弥补这一空白。

Method: 推导了一个广义的吉布斯-杜亥姆框架，将动力学贡献纳入其中；随后基于该框架提出一个替代的演化方程，用于描述流-流界面处的密度动力学。

Result: 在适当的极限条件下，所提出的密度演化方程能够自然恢复声速的定义、伯努利定律以及范德瓦尔斯状态方程。

Conclusion: 广义吉布斯-杜亥姆框架统一了经典热力学与牛顿力学，填补了准静态假设下热力学关系与动力学描述之间的理论空隙。

Abstract: The classical Gibbs-Duhem relation applies to quasi-static processes and neglects kinetic effects, leaving a fundamental gap between Gibbs thermodynamics and Newtonian mechanics. Here, we derive a generalized Gibbs-Duhem framework that incorporates kinetic contributions, thereby establishing a unified connection between classical thermodynamics and Newtonian mechanics. Based on this framework, we propose an alternative evolution equation governing density dynamics at fluid-fluid interfaces. In appropriate limiting cases, the resulting density evolution equation naturally recovers the definition of the speed of sound, Bernoulli's law, and the van der Waals equation of state (EOS).

### [101] [Bulk and microphase separation in chiral active systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12045)
*Sumeja Bureković,S. J. Kole,Ananyo Maitra,Cesare Nardini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过粒子和连续模型揭示了手性（chirality）在活性粒子群体感应相分离中的作用，发现手性可诱导体相分离或微相分离，并形成由蒸汽泡组成的手性相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性粒子常因群体感应（quorum-sensing）相互作用而发生相分离，其自推进机制往往破坏手性对称性（chiral symmetry），但手性对相分离行为的具体影响尚不清楚。

Method: 采用粒子模型与连续模型相结合的方法，并基于多重尺度分析（multiple-scale analysis）的粗粒化（coarse-graining）技术进行理论预测；同时引入最小活性场论（minimal active field theory）。

Result: 手性在体相分离区域不改变扩散型 $t^{1/3}$ 粗化律（coarsening law）及与毛细波（capillary waves）相关的动力学指数，但会在界面处诱导行波（traveling waves）；此外，即使无流体流动，手性也可导致细长液滴的断裂。

Conclusion: 手性在活性物质相分离中扮演重要角色，既可调控体相分离与微相分离的形态，又能产生与实验观察相似的液滴断裂现象。

Abstract: Many active particles phase-separate due to quorum-sensing interactions, and their self-propulsion mechanisms often break chiral symmetry. Using particle and continuum models, we uncover the role of chirality in inducing bulk or microphase separation, including a chiral phase formed of vapor bubbles. Analytical predictions for the emergence of these phases require a coarse-graining technique based on multiple-scale analysis. Further, introducing a minimal active field theory, we show that, in the bulk phase separation regime, chirality does not alter the diffusive $t^{1/3}$ coarsening law nor the dynamical exponent associated with capillary waves, but induces traveling waves at the interface. We finally demonstrate that, even in the absence of fluid flows, chirality can cause the breakup of elongated droplets, resembling phenomena previously observed experimentally.

### [102] [Harvesting Reshapes Dynamical Populations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12093)
*R. K. Singh,Michael Assaf,Jason R. Green,Erez Aghion*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过周期性地移除阈值上方或下方的个体（harvesting），可以在不改变随机过程动力学的前提下重塑异质性种群的概率密度演化。研究涵盖正常/反常随机过程与捕食者-猎物模型，发现移除上方部分会使系统进入仅依赖于阈值和频率的准稳态，而移除下方部分则会固定密度形状并产生稳定有效漂移，暗示可通过外部选择干预操纵随机种群动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究周期性阈值收割（harvesting）事件如何在不改变底层随机动力学的情况下，重塑异质性种群概率密度的演化行为。

Method: 研究覆盖了兼具正常动力学（normal dynamics）与反常动力学（anomalous dynamics）的多类随机过程（stochastic processes），以及一个经典的捕食者-猎物模型（predator-prey model），通过周期性移除阈值上方或下方的个体来考察密度演化的响应。

Result: 移除密度上方部分后，系统在“收割时钟”（harvesting clock）观测下进入准稳态（quasi-steady state），该状态仅取决于收割阈值和频率而与初始条件无关；移除密度下方部分则会固定概率密度的形状，并产生一个超过未收割均值（unharvested mean）的恒定有效漂移（effective drift）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，通过外部选择干预（external selection interventions）手段，有可能实现对随机种群动力学的主动操控。

Abstract: Harvesting -- the periodic removal of individuals above or below a threshold trait value -- reshapes heterogeneous populations without altering their underlying stochastic dynamics. We study how repeated harvesting events steer the evolution of probability densities for classes of stochastic processes exhibiting both normal and anomalous dynamics, as well as a prototypical predator-prey model. Removal of the upper portion of the density drives the system to a quasi-steady state when viewed at the ``harvesting clock''. This state depends only on the harvesting threshold and frequency but not on the initial conditions. Removal of the lower portion of the density fixes its shape while generating a constant effective drift that exceeds that of the unharvested mean. Our results suggest the possibility of manipulating the dynamics of stochastic populations through external selection interventions.

### [103] [Topological building blocks of nonequilibrium response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12096)
*Sean Fancher,Jordan Horowitz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对非平衡系统对外部刺激的响应行为，提出了一种系统化的几何表征方法。通过识别由状态空间拓扑决定的最优敏感模型，并推测所有响应可表示为这些最优模型的凸组合，从而结构化整个响应空间。该几何视角被用于分析非单调生化输入-输出函数的灵敏度极限，并识别了分子在三位置间无序结合的所有最优动力学方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论（如涨落-响应关系以及限制系统行为的边界与约束）虽然捕捉了非平衡放大（nonequilibrium amplification）的不同侧面，但缺乏对完整响应行为范围的系统性刻画。本工作旨在填补这一空白，从更广泛的视角对可能的响应行为进行系统化表征。

Method: 针对一大类非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium dynamics），识别出一组由状态空间拓扑（topology of state space）决定的最优敏感模型。进一步推测，所有可能的响应均可表示为这些最优模型的凸组合（convex combination），从而利用几何视角结构化整个响应空间。

Result: 利用该几何视角，分析了非单调（nonmonotonic）生化输入-输出函数的灵敏度极限，并识别了分子在三位置间无序结合（unordered binding）的所有最优动力学方案（optimal kinetic schemes）。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解非平衡系统响应行为的完整范围提供了系统化的几何框架，有助于揭示非平衡放大的基本限制，并为工程装置与生物体中功能设计提供理论指导。

Abstract: Nonequilibrium systems can exploit energy to amplify their sensitivity to external stimuli, allowing them to be harnessed for a variety of functions in both engineered devices and living organisms. An assortment of theoretical results capture different facets of this nonequilibrium amplification, including fluctuation-response relations as well as bounds and constraints that limit the potential behavior. Here, we take a broader perspective, aiming for a systematic characterization of the full range of possible response behaviors. For a wide class of nonequilibrium dynamics, we identify a collection of optimally sensitive models whose behavior is determined by the topology of the state space. We further conjecture that every response can be written as a convex combination of these optimal models, thereby structuring the entire space of responses. We use this geometric perspective to put sensitivity limits on nonmonotonic biochemical input-output functions, and identify all optimal kinetic schemes for the unordered binding of molecules among three sites.

</details>


### [104] [From stable periodic orbits to many-body chaos: doubly tunable prethermalization via engineering of an emergent band structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12355)

TL;DR: 本文在远离高频极限的周期性驱动（Floquet）自旋系统中发现了一族多体周期轨道。通过线性稳定性分析与热力学预期的张力，作者揭示了扰动围绕稳定周期轨道呈现类似准粒子能带结构的描述，并展示了通过能带工程可实现预热寿命的"双可调"参数依赖关系，从而在驱动多体系统中稳定非平衡物质相，并在低维非线性系统与多体混沌之间建立了概念桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在远离高频极限的周期性驱动（Floquet）自旋系统中，线性稳定性分析预测扰动后的多体轨迹仍接近稳定周期轨道，但热力学原理表明Floquet加热最终必然发生。本文旨在解决这两种预期之间的张力。

Method: 通过分析稳定周期轨道附近的扰动，揭示其具有类似准粒子能带结构（quasiparticle band structure）的描述；当围绕无能隙点（gapless point）的模式被缓慢填充时，出现长寿命的预热（prethermal） regime；利用能带工程（band engineering）调控预热寿命。

Result: 预热寿命具有"双可调"（doubly tunable）的参量依赖关系 $R^{-W}$，其中 $R$ 为准粒子分布在动量空间中的宽度，$W$ 为无能隙点附近色散关系的指数。

Conclusion: 本文不仅为在驱动多体系统中稳定非平衡物质相（non-equilibrium phases of matter）建立了有效途径，还在低维非线性系统中的周期轨道与多体混沌（many-body chaos）之间建立了概念上的桥梁。

Abstract: We uncover a family of many-body periodic orbits in a periodically driven (Floquet) spin system away from the high-frequency limit. While linear stability analysis predicts that perturbed many-body trajectories remain close to stable periodic orbits, thermodynamic principles dictate that Floquet heating will ultimately set in. Our work aims to resolve the tension between these two expectations. In particular, we show that perturbations away from the stable periodic orbits feature a description akin to a quasiparticle band structure. A long-lived prethermal regime appears when modes around the gapless point are slowly populated. The dispersion determines the prethermal lifetime, and we show how band engineering leads to a "doubly tunable" parametric dependence of the prethermal lifetime $R^{-W}$, with $R$ the width in momentum space of the quasiparticle distribution and $W$ the exponent of the dispersion around the gapless point. Our results not only establish a powerful route toward stabilizing non-equilibrium phases of matter in driven many-body systems but also establish a conceptual bridge between periodic orbits in 'low-dimensional' nonlinear systems and many-body chaos.

</details>


### [105] [A Gaussian-Remainder Hierarchy for Sums of Random Variables with Big-Jump Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12357)
*Stanislav Burov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种精确的高斯余项层次结构（Gaussian-remainder hierarchy），用于描述独立同分布随机变量之和的概率密度，该层次结构将高斯固定点贡献与保留原始单加数密度的剩余扇区分离开来，并在一阶截断下给出了一个同时捕捉高斯中心、交叉区域和大跳尾部的有限N近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于具有有限方差但分布宽泛（broad, finite-variance distribution）的独立同分布随机变量之和，标准中心极限定理（central limit theorem）在有限N情况下对尾部行为的描述不够精确，尤其是当单加数密度为次指数（subexponential）分布时，大偏差（large deviation）区域需要更细致的理论框架。

Method: 通过构造一个精确的高斯余项层次结构，将和变量的概率密度分解为高斯固定点（Gaussian fixed-point）贡献和保留原始单加数密度的剩余扇区（residual sectors）。对于次指数密度，一阶（first nontrivial）截断得到一个简单有限N近似：一次与高斯背景的卷积（convolution），再减去一个修正项以消除高斯过计数（overcounting）。

Result: 数值实验在 stretched-exponential 和有限方差幂律（finite-variance power-law）示例中验证了该近似能同时描述高斯中心、交叉区域（crossover region）和大跳尾部（big-jump tail）。该一阶近似复现了 stretched-exponential 随机变量之和的已知渐近反常速率函数（asymptotic anomalous rate function），并对相应的有限N速率函数提供了准确近似。

Conclusion: 所提出的高斯余项层次结构为大偏差理论提供了统一且可计算的分析工具，特别适用于有限N情况下次指数分布的求和问题，能够用一个表达式同时涵盖高斯区域和尾部大跳行为。

Abstract: We develop an exact Gaussian-remainder hierarchy for the probability density of the sum of $N$ independent, identically distributed random variables with broad, finite-variance distribution for the summands. The hierarchy separates the Gaussian fixed-point contribution from residual sectors that retain the original single-summand density. For subexponential densities, the first nontrivial truncation yields a simple finite-$N$ approximation that involves one convolution with a Gaussian background and a subtraction that removes Gaussian overcounting. This approximation captures the Gaussian center, the crossover region, and the big-jump tail within a single expression, as demonstrated numerically for stretched-exponential and finite-variance power-law examples. The same first-order approximation reproduces the known asymptotic anomalous rate function for sums of stretched-exponential random variables and also provides an accurate approximation to the corresponding finite-$N$ rate function.

</details>


### [106] [From phase space to Krylov space, one shell at a time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12585)
*Nicolas De Ro,Adrián Sánchez-Garrido,Julian Sonner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发展了基于相空间辛结构（symplectic structure）的经典Lanczos算法，定义了经典Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity），并证明了其在$\hbar \to 0$极限下平滑过渡为量子力学对应量。通过引入Krylov-Ehrenfest时间和微正则Krylov复杂度，应用于LMG和FP模型，揭示了混沌动力学与鞍点主导的早期不稳定性行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将量子Krylov复杂度扩展至经典力学体系，建立经典与量子Krylov复杂度之间的平滑对应关系，并利用该框架研究经典混沌动力学与量子混沌的早期行为和偏离尺度。

Method: 利用相空间的辛结构（symplectic structure）和泊松括号（Poisson brackets）取代量子对易子，相空间积分提供内积，构造经典Lanczos算法；通过相空间量子力学的一般方法证明$\hbar \to 0$极限下量子Krylov框架平滑过渡到经典框架；定义Krylov-Ehrenfest时间和微正则Krylov复杂度（microcanonical Krylov complexity）。

Result: 经典Krylov复杂度在早期时间能准确近似量子复杂度；经典与量子复杂度发散的时间尺度对应Krylov链特征深度$n\sim n_*(\hbar)$，在时域对应混沌系统的普适尺度$t_*\sim λ_K^{-1}\log(1/\hbar)$。在FP模型中观察到谱混沌（spectral chaos），而LMG模型中微正则Krylov复杂度揭示了鞍点主导的早期不稳定性行为，该不稳定性被与哈密顿量可积结构相关的谱窗口所控制。

Conclusion: 经典Krylov复杂度是早期混沌动力学的有效刻画工具，微正则Krylov复杂度提供了逐能量壳的精细分析方法，尤其适用于存在鞍点不稳定性的系统。

Abstract: In this work, we develop and study the classical Lanczos algorithm allowing us to define Krylov complexity using the symplectic structure of phase space: Poisson brackets take on the role of the quantum commutators and phase-space integrals furnish the inner product needed to define the Lanczos recursion. We show, using general methods of quantum mechanics in phase space, that the $\hbar \to 0$ limit of the usual quantum mechanical Krylov framework smoothly goes over into the classical one. In theories with well-defined semiclassical limits, we show that classical Krylov complexity accurately approximates quantum complexity at early enough times, and thus is a useful characteristic of early-time chaotic dynamics. We define a Krylov-Ehrenfest time, which quantifies the eventual divergence of classical and quantum complexities, corresponding to a characteristic depth of the Krylov chain, $n\sim n_*(\hbar)$, which in the time domain translates to the well-known scale, $t_*\simλ_K^{-1}\log(1/\hbar)$, in generic chaotic systems. We additionally define microcanonical Krylov complexities, both in the classical and quantum setting, which allows one a fine-grained study of complexity, energy shell by energy shell. We apply this framework to the Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick (LMG) and Feingold-Peres (FP) models, which are collective spin systems known to classicalize in the thermodynamic limit. In particular, while the FP model features spectral chaos for some range of coupling values, the LMG model is known to exhibit early-time saddle-dominated scrambling. Our analysis shows that the instability in LMG is resolved by the microcanonical Krylov complexity, which is controlled by the integrable structure of the Hamiltonian in spectral windows away from the instability, both at early and late times.

</details>


### [107] [Emergence of drifted diffusion in quantum walks with subspace restart](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12727)
*Liwei Qiao,Ruoyu Yin,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出子空间重启（subspace restart）协议——仅重置系统的内部自由度（internal degrees of freedom）而保留空间分布——作为控制量子-经典交叉（quantum-to-classical crossover）的可调旋钮。以离散时间量子行走（discrete-time quantum walk）为例，该选择性重置驱动行走者进入工程化的漂移-扩散（drifted-diffusion） regime，可通过惠更斯-菲涅尔机制（Huygens-Fresnel mechanism）理解，其中残余量子干涉仅作为短程修正存在于有效光锥（light cones）内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子过程重启模型采用全局重新初始化（global reinitialization），会擦除系统的全部历史。本文意在引入一种更精细的控制协议，仅重置内部自由度而不影响空间分布，从而实现对量子-经典交叉的可调控操作。

Method: 提出子空间重启协议：周期性地仅重置离散时间量子行走中行走者（walker）的内部自由度（初始硬币态），同时保持其空间概率分布不变。通过分析该选择性重置对行走者动力学的影响，揭示其驱动的漂移-扩散行为。

Result: 子空间重启将波函数碎片化为一组独立的次级源（secondary sources），屏蔽长程关联（long-range correlations），分离出稳健的经典骨架（classical backbone），其漂移率与扩散系数由初始硬币的几何取向和重启周期决定。残余量子干涉被限制在有效光锥内，仅作为短程修正出现，重整化（renormalize）上述系数并在累积量（cumulants）上留下周期性调制。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了子空间重启作为在合成晶格（synthetic lattices）中控制量子-经典交叉的有效途径，为量子动力学中经典行为的工程化调控提供了新工具。

Abstract: Restart of a quantum process is typically modeled as a global reinitialization that erases the system's entire history. Here we introduce subspace restart, a protocol that periodically resets only the internal degrees of freedom while preserving the spatial distribution, as a tunable knob for the quantum-to-classical crossover. Using the discrete-time quantum walk as an example, we show that this selective reset drives the walker into an engineered drifted-diffusion regime. This phenomenon can be understood by a Huygens-Fresnel mechanism, where each restart fragments the wave function into a set of independent secondary sources to screen long-range correlations and isolate a robust classical backbone, whose drift and diffusivity are set by the geometric orientation of the initial coin and the restart period. Residual quantum interference, confined to effective light cones, survives only as a short-range correction that renormalizes these coefficients and imprints periodic modulations on the cumulants. Our results establish subspace restart as a route to controlling the quantum-to-classical crossover in synthetic lattices.

### [108] [Coherent Bose-Einstein condensation with fluctuating density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12926)
*L. Salasnich,A. Crisanti,A. Sarracino,M. Zannetti*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在巨正则系综（grand canonical ensemble）框架下，基于凝聚体模算符的相位-密度分解，研究了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation, BEC）中宏观凝聚体数涨落对关联函数和异常平均值的影响，并提出了实验可检验的理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在巨正则系综中，凝聚体存在宏观的粒子数涨落，这给玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚的理论表述带来了非平凡的影响，需要一种能够同时处理相位和密度涨落的统一框架。

Method: 采用凝聚体模算符 $\hatψ_{\bf 0}$ 的相位-密度分解（phase-density decomposition），在假设相位定义良好而凝聚体密度存在涨落的条件下，将关联函数层级结构完全由密度的统计量决定。

Result: 对于理想玻色气体，在巨正则统计下，异常平均值（anomalous average）的模平方 $|\langle {\hat ψ}_{\bf 0}\rangle|^2 = (\pi/4) ρ_{\bf 0}$，仅为整个凝聚体密度 $ρ_{\bf 0}$ 的一部分；剩余部分由 $\hatψ_{\bf 0}$ 的宏观涨落补充，这是该设定下BEC的一个显著特征。

Conclusion: 该框架为染料填充微腔光子实验中观测到的具有良好相位但大数涨落的光子凝聚体提供了清晰的物理解释，并提出了测量异常平均值模平方以检验理论预测的实验方案。

Abstract: Bose-Einstein condensation in the grand canonical ensemble admits a formulation in terms of a phase-density decomposition of the condensate mode operator $\hatψ_{\bf 0}$. In the presence of macroscopic condensate number fluctuations this representation presents nontrivial implications. In particular, we show that, for the ideal gas, under the assumption of a well-defined phase and a fluctuating condensate density, the full hierarchy of correlation functions is determined by the statistics of the density. Within this framework, the modulus squared of the anomalous average $\langle \hatψ_{\bf 0}\rangle$ can provide only a fraction of the whole condensate density $ρ_{\bf 0}$ and for the grand canonical statistics of the ideal Bose gas one obtains the value $|\langle {\hat ψ}_{\bf 0}\rangle|^2 =(π/4) ρ_{\bf 0}$. The remaining part is supplemented by the (macroscopic) fluctuations of $\hatψ_{\bf 0}$, which become a distinctive feature of the BEC in this setting. This provides a transparent physical picture of a condensate of photons with a well-defined phase but large number fluctuations, as observed in dye-filled microcavity photon experiments. We also propose a way to access the square modulus of the anomalous average to test theoretical predictions.

</details>


### [109] [Optimal preparation and reachable-state constraints in the Mpemba effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12955)
*C. Ríos-Monje,A. Patrón-Castro,C. A. Plata,B. Sánchez-Rey,A. Prados*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过将老化协议（aging protocol）明确纳入分析框架，重新审视了姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect）。以均匀加热的颗粒流体（granular fluids）为研究对象，将状态制备阶段表述为一个最优控制问题（optimal-control problem），利用庞特里亚金最大值原理（Pontryagin's maximum principle）证明最优协议为单脉冲协议（one-bang protocol），并发现随机热浴（stochastic thermostat）对可达状态施加了非平凡约束，限制了松弛速率不对称性及最大可实现的姆潘巴效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有对姆潘巴效应的动力学分析通常预设非平稳初始条件（non-stationary initial conditions），而未充分考虑这些状态的实际制备过程。本文旨在通过显式引入老化协议来修正这一视角，探索初始条件的制备方式对后续弛豫速率及姆潘巴效应强度的影响。

Method: 以均匀加热的颗粒流体为模型系统，将初始状态的制备阶段构建为一个最优控制问题：通过调节能量注入（energy injection）来生成使后续弛豫速率最大化或最小化的初始条件。在第一松奈近似（first Sonine approximation）下，该优化问题等价于对速度分布函数（velocity distribution function）的超额峰度（excess kurtosis）取极值，并应用庞特里亚金最大值原理求解最优制备协议。

Result: 最优制备协议始终为单脉冲协议；随机热浴施加的可达状态约束使得可达到的非高斯性（non-Gaussianities）被同质冷却态（homogeneous cooling state）的对应值所界定，从而限制了松弛速率的不对称性及姆潘巴效应的最大可实现强度。

Conclusion: 动力学姆潘巴效应（kinetic Mpemba effect）的强度无法与底层非平衡态（non-equilibrium states）的可达性脱钩。本文在非平衡系统中的反常弛豫（anomalous relaxation）、最优控制（optimal control）与状态可达性（state accessibility）之间建立了联系。

Abstract: The Mpemba effect, whereby an initially hotter system relaxes faster than a colder one towards a common final state, is often analysed within the kinetic framework by assuming non-stationary initial conditions that are selected a priori. Here, we revisit this viewpoint by explicitly incorporating the aging protocol used to prepare those states. Focusing on uniformly heated granular fluids, we formulate the preparation stage as an optimal-control problem in which the energy injection is tuned to generate the initial conditions that maximise or minimise the subsequent relaxation rate. Within the first Sonine approximation, this optimisation reduces to extremising the excess kurtosis of the velocity distribution function, the quantity controlling the cooling rate at fixed temperature. Applying Pontryagin's maximum principle, we show that the optimal preparation protocol is always a one-bang protocol and determine the corresponding extremal values of the excess kurtosis. Most importantly, we find that the stochastic thermostat imposes non-trivial reachable-state constraints: the accessible non-Gaussianities are bounded by those of the homogeneous cooling state, thereby limiting the relaxation-rate asymmetry and the maximum attainable Mpemba effect. These results demonstrate that the strength of the kinetic Mpemba effect cannot be disentangled from the accessibility of the underlying non-equilibrium states. More generally, our work establishes a connection between anomalous relaxation, optimal control, and state accessibility in non-equilibrium systems.

</details>

Despite recent progress in modelling core transport, a dedicated analysis regarding the thermal conductivity of a specific \(npΛ\) mixture remains absent from the existing literature. In this work, we investigate the thermal conductivity of dense, \(β\)-equilibrated \(npΛ\) matter within the framework of the variational linearized Boltzmann kinetic approach, employing the density-dependent DDME2 equation of state across a baryon density range of \((0.5\text{--}4.5)\,n_0\). We find that neutrons still dominate thermal transport, while the onset of \(Λ\) hyperons induces only a remarkably small reduction in neutron conductivity compared to pure nucleonic matter. ### [111] [Semi-open boundary for random walking shocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12795)
*Márton Balázs*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文发现半开放边界条件下非对称排斥过程（asymmetric exclusion）与指数砌砖模型（exponential bricklayers model）中隐藏的随机游走结构得以保留，并刻画了特殊的双物种不可逆平稳分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相互作用粒子系统的非平稳时间演化通常难以处理，但存在一些例外模型（如非对称排斥与指数砌砖模型）因隐藏的有限个相互作用随机游走（random walks）过程而使描述变得可行；此前这些分布结构仅在无限体积下被证明。本文旨在寻找边界机制，使得有限体积下该结构仍然成立。

Method: 通过在半开放边界（semi-open boundaries）条件下设置特殊的边界速率，允许普通粒子通过但不允许激波（shocks）通过，从而在有限体积模型中保留隐藏的随机游走结构。

Conclusion: 半开放边界条件能将原本仅在无限体积下成立的隐藏随机游走结构推广至有限体积；这一发现为理解有限系统中双物种非可逆平稳分布提供了新的途径。

Abstract: Non-stationary time evolution of interacting particle systems is in general a rather difficult topic however, exceptional examples are known where hidden processes within the model make the description manageable. These hidden processes often take the form of a finite number of interacting random walks and in some cases, rather than being hidden, were very explicitly revealed as second class particles associated with the model. The examples of asymmetric exclusion and exponential bricklayers model are known in this context, where such distributional structure was demonstrated in infinite volume. Here we find boundary mechanisms that save this remarkable structure in finite volume of the model with semi-open boundaries that let ordinary particles, but not the shocks, through. This finding also allows to characterise nontrivial two-species, non-reversible stationary distributions subject to our special boundary rates.

### [112] [Obstructions to Deformation Quantization of Bundles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12910)
*Vladimir Baranovsky,Greg Huey*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了光滑代数簇或复流形上向量丛的形变量子化（deformation quantization）的拓展问题。在已有 $\hbar^k$ 阶形变量子化的前提下，分析了将其拓展至 $\hbar^\ell$ 阶（$\ell > k$）的必要条件与充分条件，证明了障碍类（obstruction class）的平凡性是拓展存在的必要条件，并在 $\ell \le 2k+1$ 时证明了该条件也是充分的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在代数簇或复流形上，给定辛形式（symplectic form）$\omega$ 与结构层 $\mathcal{O}_M$ 的形变量子化 $\mathcal{O}_{\hbar}$ 后，向量丛 $E$ 的形变量子化能否从低阶拓展到高阶是一个基本且核心的问题。该问题关系到量子化理论的完备性与可构造性，但目前缺乏系统的充要条件刻画。

Method: 论文采用障碍理论（obstruction theory）的方法，将向量丛形变量子化的高阶拓展问题形式化为障碍类的平凡性判定。通过分析形变参数 $\hbar$ 的幂次关系，在 $\ell \le 2k+1$ 的范围内建立了必要性与充分性的严格证明。

Result: 首先，证明了障碍类的平凡性是向量丛形变量子化从 $\hbar^k$ 阶拓展到 $\hbar^\ell$ 阶（$\ell > k$）的必要条件。其次，当 $\ell \le 2k+1$ 时，证明了该条件也是充分的，即障碍类平凡足以保证拓展的存在性。

Conclusion: 该工作为辛簇（symplectic manifold）上向量丛的形变量子化拓展问题提供了清晰的充要条件刻画，特别是给出了一个实用的充分性范围 $\ell \le 2k+1$，有助于进一步理解形变量子化结构的可延拓性。

Abstract: Let $\left(M, \mathcal{O}_M \right)$ be a smooth algebraic variety over field $κ$ of characteristic $0$ with an algebraic symplectic form $ω$, or a complex manifold with a holomorphic form $ω$. Furthermore, let $E$ be a vector bundle over $\left(M, \mathcal{O}_M \right)$ and $\mathcal{O}_{\hbar}$ a deformation quantization of $\mathcal{O}_M$ compatible with $ω$.
  Assuming that $E$ possesses a deformation quantization to order $\hbar^k$ we consider the problem of extending it to order $\hbar^\ell$ for $\ell > k$, and establish triviality of an obstruction class as a necessary condition for this extension to exist. Furthermore, in the case $\ell \le 2k+1$, we prove that this condition is also sufficient.

</details>

Method: 作者通过生成并分析大量的枚举数据（enumeration data），从中推测出 $k$-凸多联骨牌按半周长计数的生成函数形式，并提出该函数为猜想解（conjectured solution）。

Abstract: We give the conjectured solution for the generating function of $k$-convex polyominoes, enumerated by semi-perimeter. The solution was obtained from the analysis of enumeration data that we generated.

### [114] [Beyond ΛCDM with the SKA Observatory -- I: Probing Gravity on Cosmological Scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11917)
*S. Camera,C. Addis,S. L. Guedezounme,F. Montano,T. Montandon,M. Novara,S. J. Rossiter,J. Asorey,S. Castello,C. Clarkson,J. Fonseca,N. Frusciante,C. Gomes,N. Grimm,A. Nasirudin,L. G. T. Oliveira,F. Pace,Z. Sakr,M. Berti,C. Bonvin,P. Bull,E. Di Dio,C. Cress,C. Heneka,H. -R. Kloeckner,R. Maartens,C. J. A. P. Martins,D. Parkinson,C. S. Saraf*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文聚焦于广义相对论（GR）在宇宙学尺度上的检验问题。尽管GR在强场区域已被高精度验证，但在宇宙大尺度上，引力极弱且时空曲率几乎可忽略，暗物质与暗能量的存在暗示GR可能并非终极引力理论。SKA天文台凭借其巨大的探测规模和多样化的宇宙学观测量，被视为检验GR在宇宙学尺度上有效性的理想工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论是目前描述引力的最佳理论，但它在量子层面存在根本性缺失。宇宙大尺度上暗物质和暗能量的存在，提出了一个关键问题：这些奇异组分是真实存在，还是我们对引力理解不完备的产物？因此，亟需在宇宙学尺度上检验GR的适用性。

Method: 利用SKA天文台的观测能力——包括其巨大的探测体积以及多样且互补的宇宙观测量（cosmological observables）——来检验广义相对论在宇宙学尺度上的有效性。

Result: 论文提到广义相对论在强场区域已被高精度验证，而在宇宙大尺度上引力极弱、时空曲率几乎可忽略。SKA天文台因其独特优势，被认为是进行这一检验的特别合适的观测平台。

Conclusion: 在宇宙学尺度上检验GR至关重要，无论是进一步确证其稳健性，还是探测到可能存在的偏差，后者有望引导我们走向更一般、更完备的引力理论。SKA天文台为实现这一目标提供了前所未有的机遇。

Abstract: General relativity (GR) is currently the best description of the gravitational interaction at our disposal and is one of the foundations of the concordance cosmological model. For as much as we know that GR is not the final theory of gravitation - we still lack an understanding of its fundamental, quantum nature - it has demonstrated a remarkable success in describing observed phenomena and predicting effects that have later been confirmed by laboratory experiments or astronomical observations. Since gravity is extremely weak compared to the other three fundamental interactions, it has so far been tested with exquisite precision only in the strong-field regime. On the immense scales of the cosmos, on the other hand, the gravitational field is extremely weak and spacetime curvature is almost negligible. But crucially, it is on these scales that we see hints at the need for exotic components, such as dark matter and dark energy. The question of whether they really exist or their presence is but an artefact of the incompleteness of our understanding of gravity on cosmological scales then naturally arises. It is therefore paramount to test the validity of GR on these scales, either to further confirm its robustness or to detect deviations that could lead us to the formulation of a more general and conclusive theory of gravitation. To this purpose, the SKA Observatory is especially suited, thanks both to the enormous volumes it will probe, and to the variety and complementarity of cosmological observables that its surveys will make available to us.
