### [115] [Optical and thermodynamic properties of Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11979)
*Hassan Hassanabadi,Michael R. R. Good,Soroush Zare,Orlando Luongo,Fariba Kafikang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了嵌入Bertotti-Robinson电磁背景的Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson黑洞的热力学与光学性质，包括热力学量、极端残骸构型、等效AdS热力学解释、Komar守恒量以及阴影边界与磁阴影磁化率等观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在外部Bertotti-Robinson电磁背景下旋转黑洞（Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson黑洞）的热力学与光学性质，并揭示电磁背景对黑洞热力学和阴影观测特征的修正效应。

Method: 在固定角动量（fixed-a）系综中推导热力学量；使用Komar积分定义有限半径处的质量与电荷；采用Hamilton-Jacobi（Hamilton–Jacobi）形式分离零测地线势，计算球面光子轨道冲击参数和有限距离观测者的阴影边界。

Result: 弱场下热力学修正首现于B²阶，极端半径在同一阶发生偏移，而残骸质量首次修正出现在B⁴阶；Bertotti-Robinson背景使平均能层厚度（ergosphere thickness）和阴影面积减小，光子-能层间隙（photon–ergosphere gap）增大，并产生由旋转增强的负磁阴影磁化率（shadow susceptibility）。

Conclusion: Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson黑洞的热力学量在B→0时平滑退化为Kerr黑洞；Bertotti-Robinson尺度可形式化地类比AdS热力学解释；电磁背景显著改变黑洞的阴影和能层等可观测特征。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic and optical properties of Kerr--Bertotti--Robinson black holes, namely rotating black holes immersed in an external Bertotti--Robinson electromagnetic background. In the fixed-$a$ ensemble, we derive the horizon mass relation, the Hawking temperature, the entropy, the Helmholtz-type free energy, the heat capacity, and the extremal remnant configuration. These quantities reduce smoothly to their Kerr counterparts as $B\to0$. In the weak-field regime, the leading thermodynamic corrections arise at order $B^2$; the extremal radius is shifted at this order, whereas the remnant mass receives its first correction only at order $B^4$. We also introduce a formal AdS-like thermodynamic interpretation of the Bertotti--Robinson scale, treating the associated pressure as an effective response variable rather than a genuine cosmological pressure. Because the spacetime is not asymptotically flat, we further compute the finite-radius Komar mass and the Komar charge associated with the horizon generator. Using the Hamilton--Jacobi formalism, we derive the separated null-geodesic potentials, the impact parameters of spherical photon orbits, and the celestial coordinates of the shadow boundary for a finite-distance observer. We then characterize the photon-region boundaries, ergosphere thickness, photon--ergosphere gap, shadow area, and magnetic shadow susceptibility. Within the perturbative regime considered, the Bertotti--Robinson background decreases the averaged ergosphere thickness and shadow area, increases the photon--ergosphere gap, and produces a negative shadow susceptibility whose magnitude is enhanced by rotation.

</details>


### [116] [Geometric effects of torsion on black hole ringdown and shadows in Poincaré gauge gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11989)
*Terkaa Victor Targema,Kazuharu Bamba,Riasat Ali,Usman Zafar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在庞加莱规范引力（Poincaré gauge gravity）中研究了一类由时空挠率（spacetime torsion）产生有效电荷的类Reissner-Nordström黑洞，发现其具有单视界结构，并通过WKB方法、连分式方法和eikonal对应研究了标量与自旋-2场的扰动，表明增大挠率会降低振荡频率和阻尼率、延长铃宕（ringdown）信号寿命；结合EHT与LVK观测数据，通过profile-χ²分析和蒙特卡洛采样给出了挠率参数约束，确认其与Schwarzschild极限在当前精度下一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时空挠率是广义相对论的自然推广，可能产生与爱因斯坦理论显著不同的黑洞解；本研究旨在探讨庞加莱规范引力中完全由挠率生成有效电荷的Reissner-Nordström型黑洞的视界结构、扰动行为及其可观测特征。

Method: 采用六阶Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin (WKB)近似、Leaver连分式法（continued-fraction method）以及似正规模（quasinormal modes）与不稳定零测地线（null geodesics）之间的eikonal对应，研究标量场与自旋-2测试场在挠率修正背景上的扰动。利用Event Horizon Telescope对Sgr A*和M87*的观测数据及LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK)铃宕尺度，通过profile-χ²分析和蒙特卡洛抽样约束挠率参数。

Result: 在相关挠率扇区，黑洞呈现单视界结构，无内视界（inner horizons）和极端态（extremal states）。增大挠率会同时降低振荡频率和阻尼率，使铃宕信号寿命延长。观测约束结果在现有不确定度内与Schwarzschild极限一致。

Conclusion: 时空挠率会在黑洞阴影（black hole shadows）和铃宕可观测量上留下关联性印记（correlated imprints），尽管当前观测精度尚不足以区分挠率效应与Schwarzschild情形。

Abstract: Spacetime torsion provides a natural extension of general relativity and may lead to black hole solutions that differ significantly from their Einsteinian counterparts. We investigate a class of Reissner-Nordström-like black holes in Poincaré gauge gravity, where the effective charge is generated entirely by spacetime torsion instead of an electromagnetic field. Within the physically relevant torsion sector, the spacetime exhibits a single-horizon structure, free from the inner horizons and extremal states characteristic of charged black holes. Using the sixth-order Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin (WKB) approximation, Leaver's continued-fraction method, and the eikonal correspondence between quasinormal modes and unstable null geodesics, we study scalar perturbations and spin-2 test fields on the torsion-modified background. We find that increasing torsion decreases both the oscillation frequencies and damping rates, leading to longer-lived ringdown signals. We further compare the model predictions with Event Horizon Telescope observations of Sgr A* and M87*, along with representative LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) ringdown scales, to derive constraints on the torsion parameter via a profile-$χ^{2}$ analysis supplemented by Monte Carlo sampling. Although the resulting bounds remain consistent with the Schwarzschild limit within current observational uncertainties, our results show that spacetime torsion leaves correlated imprints on both black hole shadows and ringdown observables.

</details>


### [117] [A new non-commutative correction to the thermodynamics and evaporation of the Schwarzschild black hole in non-commutative gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11991)
*Slimane Zaim,Fatma Zohra Bara*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过Seiberg-Witten映射引入的非对易修正，研究了变形史瓦西黑洞的热力学性质，发现热容呈现“不稳定大黑洞—稳定中间相—不稳定小黑洞”的三相结构，且非对易几何中的黑洞寿命比经典情形更长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非对易几何（noncommutative geometry）框架下修正史瓦西黑洞的tetrad场，以探索非对易性对黑洞热力学性质及蒸发过程的影响。

Method: 基于Seiberg-Witten映射（Seiberg-Witten map）得到tetrad场的非对易修正，推导修正后的黑洞视界半径（event horizon radius），进而计算霍金温度（Hawking temperature）、熵（entropy）、热容（heat capacity）、亥姆霍兹自由能（Helmholtz free energy）和压强（pressure）等热力学量。

Result: 热容行为揭示出三相结构：两个负热容的不稳定相（分别为大黑洞和小黑洞），被一个正热容的稳定中间相分隔。非对易修正使黑洞质量获得有效贡献，导致黑洞的有限寿命超过经典史瓦西黑洞。非对易性自然引入一个普朗克长度量级的基本长度标度 Θ=1.6×10⁻³⁵ m。

Conclusion: 非对易修正不仅改变了史瓦西黑洞的热力学相结构，还延长了黑洞的蒸发寿命，表明非对易几何在黑洞物理中具有重要的调和作用。

Abstract: We investigate the modified thermodynamic properties of a deformed Schwarzschild black hole arising from new noncommutative corrections to the tetrad fields obtained through the Seiberg-Witten map. By deriving the corrected event horizon radius, we evaluate the corresponding thermodynamic quantities, including the Hawking temperature, entropy, heat capacity, Helmholtz free energy, and pressure. We also examine the evaporation process of the black hole within this noncommutative framework. The behavior of the heat capacity reveals a rich thermodynamic structure consisting of three distinct phases: two unstable phases with negative heat capacity, corresponding to a large black hole and a small black hole, separated by an intermediate stable phase with positive heat capacity. Our analysis also shows that the Schwarzschild black hole in noncommutative geometry possesses a finite lifetime that exceeds that of its classical counterpart, owing to the effective contribution of noncommutativity to the black hole mass. The noncommutative correction naturally introduces a fundamental length scale, Θ=1,6.10^-35 m, which is of the order of the Planck length.

### [118] [Spinning particle dynamics, epicyclic frequencies, and transient QPO signatures in Schwarzschild spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11993)
*Uktamjon Uktamov,Ali Övgün,Reggie C. Pantig,Bobomurat Ahmedov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在 Schwarzschild 时空中，基于 Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon (MPD) 极-偶极近似和 Tulczyjew-Dixon 自旋补充条件，系统推导了自旋测试粒子在赤道面上的线性自旋修正动力学，包括径向势、圆轨道条件、束缚周期轨道、epicyclic 频率、Lyapunov 指数，并将其与周期轨道分类、准周期振荡模型和极端质量比旋近的引力波波形建立解析联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自旋测试粒子在非旋转黑洞背景下的运动，对于理解极端质量比旋近（extreme mass-ratio inspirals, EMRI）中的自旋-曲率耦合效应以及相应的引力波信号至关重要。已有研究主要集中在无自旋粒子上，而自旋效应对动力学和可观测量的影响需要系统分析。

Method: 采用 Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon (MPD) 极-偶极近似（pole-dipole approximation）描述自旋粒子的运动，并施加 Tulczyjew-Dixon 自旋补充条件（spin supplementary condition）。将轨道限制在赤道面上且粒子自旋与轨道角动量对齐，保留到比自旋 s 的线性阶。推导自旋修正的径向势、圆轨道条件、epicyclic 频率和 Lyapunov 指数；运用 Levin-Perez-Giz zoom-whirl 分类法构建束缚周期轨道；利用相对论进动（relativistic precession）和共振（resonance）方案分析准周期振荡；通过局部分离线（separatrix）结构关联 Lyapunov 指数与近同宿 zoom-whirl 运动。

Result: 自旋-曲率耦合使圆轨道的能量和角动量发生偏移；最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）位置修正为 $r_{\rm ISCO}=6M-2\sqrt{2/3}\,s+\mathcal{O}(s^2)$。获得了自旋对束缚周期轨道能量-角动量图的变形效应。得到了坐标时的 azimuthal 和 radial epicyclic 频率，并用于准周期振荡（quasi-periodic oscillations, QPOs）的建模。Lyapunov 指数与局部分离线结构建立了解析关系。进一步计算了来自周期轨道的引力波形。

Conclusion: 本文建立的解析框架在线性自旋阶上统一了 MPD 动力学、周期轨道分类、epicyclic 频率偏移以及强场暂态现象学，可直接应用于涉及绕超大质量黑洞运动的恒星质量致密自旋天体的极端质量比旋近引力波建模。

Abstract: We study the motion of spinning test particles in Schwarzschild spacetime within the Mathisson--Papapetrou--Dixon pole--dipole approximation, imposing the Tulczyjew--Dixon spin supplementary condition. Restricting to equatorial orbits with the particle spin aligned with the orbital angular momentum, and retaining terms through linear order in the specific spin $s$, we derive the spin-corrected radial potential, circular-orbit conditions, bound periodic trajectories, epicyclic frequencies, and Lyapunov exponents of unstable circular orbits. The spin--curvature coupling shifts the circular-orbit energy and angular momentum and moves the innermost stable circular orbit to $r_{\rm ISCO}=6M-2\sqrt{2/3}\,s+\mathcal{O}(s^2)$ in the sign convention adopted here. We construct bound periodic orbits using the Levin--Perez-Giz zoom--whirl taxonomy and show how the particle spin deforms the corresponding energy--angular-momentum map. We then obtain the coordinate-time azimuthal and radial epicyclic frequencies and use them as kinematical inputs for relativistic-precession and resonance prescriptions for quasi-periodic oscillations. Finally, we relate the Lyapunov exponent of unstable circular orbits to the local separatrix structure governing near-homoclinic zoom--whirl motion. The resulting formulation provides a compact analytic connection between linear-in-spin MPD dynamics, periodic-orbit taxonomy, epicyclic-frequency shifts, and transient strong-field phenomenology in a nonrotating black-hole background. Also, we study the gravitational waveforms from the periodic orbits of a massive spinning particle around a black hole, presenting those associated with extreme mass-ratio inspirals involving a stellar-mass compact spinning object orbiting a supermassive black hole.

</details>


### [119] [Thin-shell wormholes in cosmic voids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11995)
*Jonathan A. Rebouças,Edson Otoniel,Francisco S. N. Lobo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过将黑洞嵌入宇宙空洞（cosmic void）的密度分布，构建了一个对称的薄壳虫洞（thin-shell wormhole），并基于Darmois-Israel连接条件推导了表面应力，分析了能量条件、热力学性质和喉部径向动力学，最终通过数值结果研究了在两种Chaplygin气体状态方程下的静态构型稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙空洞作为具有de Sitter-like引力行为的欠密区域，为研究黑洞和虫洞等引力构型提供了新的背景环境。受近期将黑洞解嵌入空洞密度分布的研究启发，本文旨在构造一个对称的薄壳虫洞，并探讨其稳定性与热力学性质。

Method: 通过将黑洞内部正时区（positive-lapse region）的两个副本粘合，构造对称薄壳虫洞；利用Darmois-Israel连接条件（junction conditions）获得表面应力；基于空洞质量函数和密度分布直接表达各能量条件组合；通过有效势（effective potential）描述喉部径向动力学；采用广义宇宙Chaplygin气体（GCCG）和修正宇宙Chaplygin气体（MCCG）两种状态方程进行局部稳定性分析。

Result: Chaplygin参数B由静态连接条件固定，稳定性由空洞几何和状态方程参数决定。数值结果表明，GCCG支持的构型通常不稳定，而MCCG支持的虫洞在状态方程线性项足够大时可以稳定。

Conclusion: 本文建立的框架将宇宙空洞的de Sitter-like结构与标准薄壳虫洞形式联系起来，为识别位于空洞时空中黑洞视界与类宇宙学视界之间的稳定或不稳定虫洞构型提供了起点。

Abstract: Cosmic voids are underdense regions that can provide an effective large-scale environment with a de Sitter-like gravitational behavior. Motivated by recent black-hole solutions embedded in void density profiles, we construct a symmetric thin-shell wormhole by gluing two copies of the positive-lapse region of a black hole inside a cosmic void. The surface stresses are obtained from the Darmois--Israel junction conditions, and the corresponding null, weak, dominant, and strong energy-condition combinations are written directly in terms of the void mass function and density profile.We further develop the thermodynamics of the static shell, deriving a first law that relates the shell entropy to the black-hole and cosmological-like horizon entropies.We then formulate the radial dynamics of the throat through an effective potential and study the local stability of static configurations when the exotic matter on the shell obeys either a generalized cosmic Chaplygin gas or a modified cosmic Chaplygin gas equation of state. In both models the Chaplygin parameter $B$ is fixed by the static junction condition, so that the remaining stability test is governed by the void geometry and by the equation-of-state parameters. Numerical results reveal that GCCG-supported configurations are generically unstable, whereas MCCG-supported wormholes can be stable for a sufficiently large linear term in the equation of state. The resulting framework connects the de Sitter-like structure of cosmic voids with the standard thin-shell wormhole formalism and provides a starting point for identifying stable or unstable wormhole configurations located between the black-hole and cosmological-like horizons of the void spacetime.

</details>


### [120] [No persuasive evidence yet of gravitational-wave tails from perturbers along the line of sight in LVK observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12043)
*Kuba Kopczuk,Ethan Blake,Matthew F. Carney,Jeremy G. Baier,Michael Van Keuren,Adam Khan,Leslie Wade,Madeline Wade,Glenn Starkman,Craig Copi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究基于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作在前三次观测运行中探测到的90例致密双星并合（compact binary coalescences, CBCs）事件，通过贝叶斯模型比较（Bayesian model comparison）搜索了所谓“引力闪烁”（gravitational glints）信号——即由信号与时空扰动体（spacetime perturber）相互作用产生的引力波尾部，理论上呈现为主信号的回声。研究未在信噪比（SNR）不低于12的双黑洞或中等质量黑洞双星事件中找到引力闪烁的可信证据，并给出了闪烁相对振幅的概率上限，用于约束宇宙中扰动体的性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波探测已积累大量致密双星并合事件，但信号与时空扰动体相互作用产生的尾部信号——“引力闪烁”——尚未被系统搜索。该研究旨在检验此类信号是否存在，并利用搜索结果为宇宙中扰动体的性质提供约束。

Method: 对前三次观测运行中信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）不低于12的双黑洞及中等质量黑洞双星事件，采用贝叶斯模型比较（Bayesian model comparison）方法在最强信号附近数据中搜索引力闪烁。

Result: 未发现引力闪烁的可信证据；标准匹配滤波CBC搜索不会因模板库未包含引力闪烁而遗漏包含该信号的探测；给出了闪烁概率随相对振幅变化的上限估计。

Conclusion: 当前数据不支持引力闪烁的存在，但基于估计的上限可约束宇宙中扰动体的性质；随着第四次观测运行灵敏度的提升，预计引力闪烁将有望被探测到。

Abstract: Observations of compact binary coalescences (CBCs) by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA collaboration resulted in 90 events in the first three observing runs. We search the data near the loudest of these detections for so-called "gravitational glints," by performing Bayesian model comparison. Gravitational glints are gravitational-wave tails caused by interactions between a signal and a spacetime perturber and are theorized to present as echoes of the primary signal. We do not find convincing evidence of gravitational glints in binary black hole or intermediate-mass black hole binary events with a signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) of at least 12. We also found that standard matched-filter CBC searches with template banks that do not contain gravitational glints would likely not have missed signals containing a gravitational glint. We therefore estimate upper limits on the probability of a glint as a function of its relative amplitude and use these estimates to constrain the properties of perturbers in the Universe. With increased sensitivity in the fourth observing run, which will increase the number and SNR of detectable events, we remain optimistic that glints will soon be detectable.

### [121] [High-order gravitational late-time tails in Kerr spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12151)
*Marc Casals,Chris Kavanagh,Jakob Neef,Adrian Ottewill*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过计算Kerr时空中Teukolsky方程推迟格林函数的高阶晚期尾项，推导出有限半径、未来事件视界和未来零无穷三个区域上线性场扰动在固定球谐模下的前三阶渐近行为，包括已知的幂律衰减及其高阶对数修正，并给出了引力扰动（s=-2）下的具体尾系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Kerr时空（Kerr spacetime）中线性场扰动的晚期行为对于引力波天文学和黑洞扰动理论具有重要意义，特别是高阶尾项（tails）的精确形式对数值模拟和数据分析至关重要。

Method: 基于频率域中推迟格林函数（retarded Green function）的小频率展开（small-frequency expansion），对固定球谐模（spheroidal harmonic）$\ell$和方位角数（azimuthal number）$m$，在三个区域（有限半径、未来事件视界$\mathscr{H}^+$、未来零无穷$\mathscr{I}^+$）分别取大时间极限展开，得到前三阶渐近表达式。

Result: 得到了一般整数自旋$s$下的尾幂次和引力扰动（$s=-2$）的尾系数：有限半径处首项为$t^{-2\ell-3}$，一阶对数修正为$t^{-2\ell-5}\ln t$；事件视界处首项为$e^{im\Omega_H v}v^{-2\ell-3-b}$（$b$取决于$s$和$m$），一阶修正为$e^{im\Omega_H v}v^{-2\ell-5-b}\ln v$；未来零无穷处首项为$u^{-\ell+s-2}$，修正包括$u^{-\ell+s-3}\ln u$和$u^{-\ell+s-4}\ln^2 u$。

Conclusion: 获得了完整推迟格林函数在晚期时间的高阶展开形式，并提供了两个计算笔记本以支持特定自旋参数下的高阶展开计算。

Abstract: We calculate high-order late-time tails of the retarded Green function of the Teukolsky equation for linear field perturbations of (subextremal) Kerr spacetime. We calculate these tails at a fixed spheroidal harmonic $\ell$ and azimuthal number $m$ up to the first three orders for the field point: at finite radius (away from the event horizon) for large Boyer-Lindquist time $t$; along the future event horizon $\mathscr{H}^+$ for large ingoing Eddington-Finkelstein coordinate $v$; and along future null infinity $\mathscr{I}^+$ for large outgoing Eddington-Finkelstein coordinate $u$. We obtain the tail powers for generic integer field spin $s$ and the tail coefficients specifically for gravitational ($s=-2$) perturbations. Our asymptotics include the known leading power-law (generic) tails, respectively,$t^{-2\ell-3}$, $e^{imΩ_H v}v^{-2\ell-3-b}$ (where $b=1$ for $s>0, m=0$ and $b=0$ otherwise, and where $Ω_H$ is the angular velocity of the event horizon) and $u^{-\ell+s-2}$, as well as their higher-order logarithmic corrections: $t^{-2\ell-5}\ln t$, $e^{imΩ_H v}v^{-2\ell-5-b}\ln v$ and $u^{-\ell+s-3}\ln u$ (as well as $u^{-\ell+s-4}\ln^2 u$). Since we obtain the high-order expansions for modes for generic $\ell$ and $m$, we can readily infer the explicit expansions of the {\it full} retarded Green function for $s=-2$ (and its decay powers for generic integer $s$). We obtain the late-time asymptotics from small-frequency expansions of the Fourier modes of the retarded Green function in the frequency domain. Accordingly, we also provide small-frequency expansions of various quantities of interest in the scattering theory. We also attach two notebooks which provide expansions for specific values of $s$: one notebook provides them to the first three leading orders for generic $\ell$ and the other one to arbitrary order for specific values of $\ell$.

</details>


### [122] [Dynamics of potential-free warm $\mathbf{k}$-inflation with nonminimal derivative coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12280)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有势驱动暖暴胀模型依赖势能形式，本文旨在探索纯由非正则动能驱动的暴胀机制，以拓展暖暴胀理论框架并规避势驱动模型中的某些限制。

Method: 推导了纯动能暴胀情形下的演化方程及相应的慢滚近似；引入非最小导数耦合以增强引力摩擦，并结合热阻尼效应；分析了系统的吸引子行为；计算了密度涨落方程并给出功率谱、谱指数及张标比的解析表达式。

Result: 慢滚解能在宽松条件下逼近严格的指数膨胀吸引子；功率谱、谱指数与张标比均有解析结果；能标在视界穿越（horizon crossing）处低于广义相对论（general relativity）标准暴胀；张标比因热阻尼与非最小导数耦合的联合作用而显著降低；场位移保持在亚普朗克尺度内。

Conclusion: 模型的预言与**Planck 2018**数据高度一致，为暖暴胀（warm inflation）范式提供了一种新颖且成功的扩展。

Abstract: In contrast to potential-driven warm inflation models, this paper presents a new inflationary scenario driven purely by noncanonical kinetic terms. We derive the evolution equations and the associated slow-roll approximations specific to the kinetic case. The model incorporates a nonminimal derivative coupling that enhances gravitational friction; when combined with thermal damping, this leads to a significantly slower evolution of the pure kinetic inflaton. The resulting slow-roll approximations differ fundamentally from those of potential-driven inflation. The attractor behavior of this warm $k$-inflation with nonminimal derivative coupling is explored, confirming that slow-roll solutions can approach a strict exponential expansion attractor under relaxed slow-roll conditions. We further calculate the density fluctuation equations and obtain analytic expressions for the power spectrum, spectral index, and tensor-to-scalar ratio. Compared to standard inflation in general relativity, the energy scale at horizon crossing is lower, and the tensor-to-scalar ratio is significantly reduced due to the combined effects of thermal damping and nonminimal derivative coupling. The field excursion remains comfortably sub-Planckian. The model's predictions are in excellent agreement with the latest Planck 2018 data, offering a novel and successful extension of the warm inflation paradigm.

### [123] [Particle decay and energy conservation in the Kerr-Newman black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12475)
*Bing-Bing Chen,Guo-Ping Li,Ke Wang,Xiao-Xiong Zeng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究Kerr-Newman时空中粒子衰变过程，发现粒子分裂时质量必然减少，质量亏损转化为质心系动能；并揭示了电荷参数增大对各物理量（比角动量、质量、比能量、相对洛伦兹因子、四速度）的影响趋势，这些趋势与Kerr-de Sitter时空中增大宇宙学常数的效果相反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Kerr-Newman时空中粒子衰变行为，尤其是电荷参数对衰变产物动力学性质的影响，并与Kerr-de Sitter时空进行对比。

Method: 采用理论分析（theoretical analysis）与数值模拟（numerical simulation）相结合的方法，研究Kerr-Newman时空中粒子的分裂过程。

Result: 粒子分裂时质量必然减少，质量亏损转化为质心系（center-of-mass frame）动能。随电荷参数Q增大，母粒子O与子粒子B的比角动量减小，两子粒子质量增大，比能量绝对值减小，三者间的相对洛伦兹因子（Lorentz factor）和四速度均减小。

Conclusion: Kerr-Newman时空中电荷参数对粒子衰变的影响趋势与Kerr-de Sitter时空中宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的影响趋势恰好相反。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the decay of a particle in Kerr--Newman spacetime. Both theoretical analysis and numerical simulations show that when a particle splits in Kerr--Newman spacetime, its mass is inevitably reduced, and this mass deficit is transformed into kinetic energy in the center-of-mass frame. We denote the parent particle as $O$ and the daughter particles as $A$ and $B$. We also find that as the charge parameter $Q$ increases, the specific angular momenta of the parent particle $O$ and the daughter particle $B$ become smaller, the masses of the two daughter particles become larger, the absolute values of their specific energies become smaller, the relative Lorentz factors among the three particles become smaller, and their four-velocities also become smaller. These trends are opposite to those observed when increasing the cosmological constant in Kerr--de Sitter spacetime.

### [124] [Role of spin-curvature and magnetic interactions on circular orbits of particles with magnetic monopole around Bardeen black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12486)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索规则黑洞（regular black hole）作为奇异黑洞替代候选体的可观测特征，尤其是非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics）和磁单极子（magnetic monopole）在强引力环境中的动力学信号。

Method: 采用Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon（MPD）方程，辅以Tulczyjew自旋条件，并引入广义洛伦兹力（generalized Lorentz force）以纳入磁相互作用，在赤道面上导出径向运动有效势。

Result: 顺行自旋（prograde spin）与吸引性磁相互作用减小ISCO半径，逆行自旋（retrograde spin）与排斥性相互作用将其外推；类时约束排除了非物理的超光速轨迹；BSW效应在规则黑洞中被显著抑制，碰撞能量被限制在有限值。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of magnetically charged spinning test particles in the spacetime of the Bardeen regular black hole, sourced by nonlinear electrodynamics and featuring a magnetic monopole charge parameter g. Employing the Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon equations supplemented by the Tulczyjew spin condition and extended to include magnetic interactions via the generalized Lorentz force, we derive the effective potential governing the radial motion in the equatorial plane. We analyze the properties of circular orbits, including the location and parameters of the innermost stable circular orbit, and examine how they are modified by the particle's spin s, specific magnetic charge lambda, and the black hole's magnetic charge g. Prograde spin and attractive magnetic interactions reduce the ISCO radius, whereas repulsive interactions and retrograde spin shift it outward. We further impose timelike constraints to exclude unphysical superluminal trajectories, delineating the admissible parameter space. Finally, we explore high-energy particle collisions near the horizon, computing the critical angular momentum and the center-of-mass collision energy. Due to the regular core of the Bardeen spacetime, the Bañados-Silk-West effect is significantly suppressed or capped at finite values, in contrast to singular black hole solutions. These results highlight distinctive phenomenological signatures of regular black holes and offer potential observational probes of nonlinearity in electrodynamics and of magnetic monopoles through accretion processes, extreme-mass-ratio inspirals, and ultra-high-energy particle interactions.

Method: 利用激光腔（laser cavity）中引力波对电磁波传播的调制效应（modulating effect），通过高精度光学光谱（optical precision spectroscopy）测量发射光子频率的变化来间接探测高频引力波。

Result: 首次在100 kHz至100 MHz的大部分频率范围内对高频引力波施加了实验约束（experimental limits）。

Abstract: Gravitational waves affect the propagation of electromagnetic waves in laser cavities, modulating the frequency of emitted photons. Our limits constrain much of this frequency range for the first time. We discuss future improvements of the technique, which we expect to enhance the sensitivity by eight orders of magnitude, and to extend the frequency coverage up to at least 1 GHz.

### [126] [Two-fluid $f$-mode oscillations of dark-matter-admixed neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12661)
*Zi-Yue Zheng,Ting-Ting Sun,Huan Chen,Xiao-Ping Zheng,Jin-Biao Wei,G. F. Burgio,H. -J. Schulze*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在全广义相对论（full general relativity, GR）框架下研究暗物质混合中子星（dark-matter-admixed neutron stars, DANSs）的四极 f 模振荡，通过求解双流体极型扰动方程并施加引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）出射边界条件，得到复本征频率。结果显示中等暗物质组分比例下，某一双流体分支可变为弱辐射模式，阻尼时间（damping time）提升数个量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多基于双流体 Cowling 近似，忽略了度规扰动及辐射边界条件，无法准确描述暗物质混合中子星的四极 f 模振荡与引力波辐射特性。本文旨在超越 Cowling 近似，在全 GR 框架下给出更完整的模式频率与阻尼信息。

Method: 采用微观 Brueckner-Hartree-Fock（BHF）物质模型描述普通物质，并匹配 Shen2020 外壳；暗物质（dark matter, DM）组分处理为冷自相互作用费米子流体，仅通过引力与普通物质耦合。在固定 DM 占比序列下，求解极型双流体扰动方程，并施加引力波出射边界条件，得到复本征频率。通过组分动能、位移重叠度及物质四极矩抵消量诊断模式的局域特征。

Result: 频谱包含两条主要的 f 模序列，其局域特征分为普通物质主导、DM 主导或混合型。核心结果是：在中等 DM 占比下，某一双流体分支阻尼时间增强数个量级，呈现弱辐射行为。同时计算了出射 Zerilli 振幅与 GW 阻尼时间，并以此估算达到探测器阈值所需的 GW 能量。

Conclusion: 本研究通过保留度规扰动与辐射边界条件，将前期基于双流体 Cowling 近似的工作推广至更完整的全 GR 处理。所得弱辐射模式对暗物质混合中子星的引力波可探测性具有重要影响。

Abstract: We study quadrupolar $f$-mode oscillations of dark-matter-admixed neutron stars (DANSs) in full general relativity (GR). The ordinary component is described by microscopic Brueckner-Hartree-Fock matter matched to the Shen2020 crust, while the dark matter (DM) component is treated as a cold self-interacting fermion fluid coupled to ordinary matter only by gravity. For fixed-DM-fraction sequences we solve the polar two-fluid perturbation equations with an outgoing gravitational-wave (GW) boundary condition, obtaining complex eigenfrequencies rather than only real mode frequencies. The spectrum contains two principal $f$-like sequences. Their local character can be ordinary-matter-led, DM-led, or mixed, and is diagnosed using the component kinetic energies, the displacement overlap, and the cancellation of the matter quadrupole. A main result is that, for intermediate DM fractions, one of the two-fluid branches can become weakly radiating, with damping times enhanced by several orders of magnitude. The same calculation gives the outgoing Zerilli amplitude and the GW damping time, which we use to estimate the GW energy required to reach a prescribed detector threshold. Thus the analysis extends previous two-fluid Cowling studies by retaining metric perturbations and the radiative boundary condition.

### [127] [Evaluating KAGRA upgrade scenarios for multimessenger observations of binary neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12769)

Motivation: 双中子星并合（binary neutron star mergers）是多信使天文学的关键目标，推动引力波探测器（gravitational-wave detectors）的升级。KAGRA面临宽带灵敏度提升与高频优化两种升级方向，需要一种量化框架来评估其在多信使观测中的综合表现。

Method: 提出一个计算高效的分析框架，将Fisher矩阵（Fisher matrix）估计的定位面积（localization area）与定位体积（localization volume）同探测器占空因子（duty factor）及双中子星并合率相结合，用以评估探测器升级方案的多信使性能，并应用于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA网络中的KAGRA升级场景。

Result: 对相同源而言，高频升级比宽带升级的天球定位（sky localization）改善约20%。但考虑探测率后，宽带升级产生更多精确定位事件。尽管KAGRA的双中子星探测距离短于其他探测器，加入KAGRA仍使定位体积在10^3 Mpc^3以内的事件数增加约60%。

Conclusion: 本研究为从多信使观测角度评估未来探测器升级提供了定量框架。不同KAGRA升级方案各有优势：高频升级侧重定位精度提升，宽带升级侧重事件数量增长；KAGRA在网络中的加入对多信使观测有显著贡献。

Abstract: Binary neutron star mergers are key targets for multimessenger astronomy, motivating future upgrades of gravitational-wave detectors. For KAGRA, both broadband sensitivity improvements that increase the binary neutron star detection range, and high-frequency optimizations targeting neutron-star physics are under consideration. We present a computationally efficient framework to evaluate the multimessenger performance of detector upgrades by combining Fisher-matrix estimates of localization area and localization volume with detector duty factors and binary neutron star merger rates. We apply this framework to proposed KAGRA upgrade scenarios within the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA network. For identical sources, the high-frequency upgrade improves sky localization by about 20% compared with the broadband option. However, when detection rates are taken into account, the broadband upgrade yields a larger number of well-localized events. Despite its shorter binary neutron star range than the other detectors, the inclusion of KAGRA increases the number of events localized within $10^3$ Mpc$^3$ volume by about 60%. These results provide a quantitative framework for evaluating future detector upgrades from the perspective of multimessenger observations.

</details>


### [128] [Qualitative Analysis of Cosmological Models Using Dynamical System Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12791)
*Sayantan Ghosh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文系统研究了宇宙加速膨胀的理论与观测方面，重点分析了f(Q)引力框架下的暗能量模型与修正引力理论。通过多种数据集约束、动力学系统分析和扰动稳定性检验，对耗散Chaplygin气体、Dirac-Born-Infeld (DBI)暗能量及规范标量场等模型进行了全面评估，并给出了其演化行为与理论可行性结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解宇宙加速膨胀的物理机制是当代宇宙学的核心问题之一。论文旨在系统分析暗能量模型与修正引力框架（如f(R)、f(T)、f(Q)引力）的理论可行性与观测约束，以识别能够有效描述宇宙加速膨胀的候选模型。

Method: 论文采用多章节递进式结构，综合运用多种方法：利用宇宙钟（CC）和Pantheon+SH0ES超新星数据集对模型进行观测约束；通过高斯过程（Gaussian Processes）重建DBI暗能量的动力学；采用卡方检验（chi-square）和马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法拟合理论模型；运用动力学系统（dynamical systems）分析标量场宇宙学的相空间行为；推导并分析规范不变扰动变量（gauge invariant variables）的扰动方程，构建扩展相空间以联合分析背景与扰动动力学。

Result: 论文得到了多个关键结果：耗散Chaplygin气体在f(Q)引力中的宇宙学模型通过信息准则和Om及statefinder诊断工具得到评估；DBI暗能量的势函数通过高斯过程从哈勃参数和DESI数据重建并得到MCMC约束；在f(Q)引力中，规范标量场和DBI标量场的动力学系统分析揭示了其相空间结构；背景和扰动层面的标量场演化方程及规范不变扰动方程被推导并整合进扩展相空间框架。

Conclusion: 论文系统总结了各模型在f(Q)引力框架下的动力学行为、观测约束与扰动稳定性结论，并指出了未来研究方向。附录部分补充了场方程、宇宙学方程以及f(Q)引力的基础性数学细节。

Abstract: This thesis investigates theoretical and observational aspects of cosmic acceleration, focusing on dark energy models and modified gravity frameworks. The goal is to analyse their viability, dynamical behaviour, and perturbative stability to identify models capable of describing the accelerated expansion of the Universe. Chapter 1 reviews the essential background General Relativity, and mathematics of teleparallel and symmetric teleparallel geometries, basic cosmological models, matter components, and the key observational probes. The chapter concludes with a summary of modified gravity theories, including f(R), f(T) and f(Q). Chapter 2 studies a dissipative Chaplygin gas cosmology in f(Q) gravity. The model is constrained using the CC and Pantheon+SH0ES dataset, and its performance is assessed through information criteria and diagnostic tools such as Om and statefinder analysis. Chapter 3 reconstructs the dynamics of Dirac-Born-Infeld (DBI) dark energy using Hubble and DESI observations via Gaussian Processes. The reconstructed potential is fitted to theoretical models using chi-square and MCMC techniques, giving constrains on DBI scalar field. Chapter 4 analyses canonical scalar-field cosmology in coincident f(Q) gravity using dynamical systems. Chapter 5 extends the dynamical analysis to the DBI scalar field in f(Q) gravity. Chapter 6 examines scalar-field evolution at both background and perturbation levels. Perturbation equations for key gauge invariant variables are derived, and an extended phase space combining background and perturbation dynamics is constructed. Finally, chapter 7 summarizes the main results along with scope for future research. Further mathematical details including derivation of field equation and cosmology equations and foundational issues related to f(Q) gravity are compiled in the following four sections: Appendix A, Appendix B, Appendix C and Appendix D.

### [129] [The entropy of dynamical black holes deviating from electrovacuum in second order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12794)
*Wen-Tao Fu,Ming-Fei Ji,Yu-Sen Zhou,Li-Ming Cao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论（Einstein-Maxwell theory）中研究动态黑洞的熵。利用高斯零坐标（Gaussian null coordinates）对表观视界（apparent horizon）进行微扰构造，并推导其二阶面积修正。在协变相空间形式（covariant phase space formalism）下引入修正的规范能量（modified canonical energy），通过平衡律（balance law）建立其与熵的二阶变分之间的联系。在零能量条件（null energy condition）和渐近稳态条件下，熵正比于表观视界面积至二阶，并满足第二定律（second law）。若放弃零能量条件，建立该面积定律则需要额外假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态黑洞的热力学性质（尤其是熵的定义与面积定律）是引力量子效应与黑洞热力学（black hole thermodynamics）中的关键问题。现有方法多局限于稳态情形，对于动态黑洞的熵变关系尚缺乏系统的微扰框架。

Method: 采用高斯零坐标对表观视界进行微扰构造，推导其二阶面积修正；利用协变相空间形式引入修正的规范能量，通过平衡律建立熵的二阶变分与该能量的关系。

Result: 在零能量条件和渐近稳态条件下，熵与表观视界面积在二阶微扰下成正比，且满足第二定律。若零能量条件不成立，则需要额外假设才能建立该面积定律。

Conclusion: 在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中，动态黑洞的熵在二阶微扰下可由表观视界面积刻画，其面积定律依赖于零能量条件的成立。

Abstract: We study the entropy of dynamical black holes in Einstein--Maxwell theory. Starting from a stationary electrovacuum background with a bifurcate Killing horizon, the apparent horizon is constructed perturbatively in Gaussian null coordinates, and the area of its cross section is derived to second order. Within the covariant phase space formalism, we introduce a modified canonical energy that incorporates contributions from external matter and is naturally related to the second-order variation of the entropy through the balance law. Under the null energy condition and the asymptotic stationary condition, the entropy is proportional to the area of the apparent horizon up to second-order and satisfies the second law. Without the null energy condition, establishing this area law requires additional assumptions.

### [130] [Prism Effect in Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13012)
*Aliasghar Parvizi,Tomasz Pawłowski*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过扩展Born-Oppenheimer近似（extended Born-Oppenheimer approximation）构建了电磁场（EM field）与量子背景几何（quantum background geometry）相互作用的一般框架，导出了一种准唯象模型来解释电磁波在弯曲时空中的传播。该模型自然重现了非线性光学中类似光-物质相互作用的色散效应（chromatic dispersion effects），并且在所有能量区间均有效，可获取超越半经典极限（semi-classical limit）的量子引力修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电磁波色散关系（dispersion relation）的修正是探测量子引力效应（quantum gravitational effects）的关键途径，但现有半经典方法（semi-classical approaches）在描述模式依赖的色散关系方面存在局限。

Method: 采用扩展的Born-Oppenheimer近似，构建电磁场与量子背景几何相互作用的通用框架，导出准唯象模型，并在平坦量子FLRW背景上结合解析技术与数值模拟分析电磁波传播。

Result: 该框架自然产生了类似于非线性光学中光-物质相互作用的色散效应，并且在平坦量子FLRW背景上观测到了由量子光-几何相互作用（quantum light-geometry interactions）诱导的棱镜效应（prism-like behavior）。

Conclusion: 该模型在所有能量区间均有效，能够获取超越半经典极限的量子引力修正，为探测量子引力效应提供了更一般的理论工具。

Abstract: Modifications to the dispersion relation of electromagnetic (EM) waves are a central probe in the search for quantum gravitational effects. In this work, we construct a general framework for the interaction between the EM field and a quantum background geometry, employing an extended Born-Oppenheimer approximation. This leads to a quasi-phenomenological model for EM wave propagation in curved spacetime. Unlike previous semi-classical approaches for mode-dependent dispersion relations, our framework naturally reproduces chromatic dispersion effects analogous to those observed in light-matter interactions in nonlinear optics. As a concrete application, we analyze EM wave propagation on a flat quantum Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) background, combining analytical techniques with numerical simulations to extract observable signatures of the prism-like behavior induced by quantum light-geometry interactions. Crucially, it remains valid across all energy regimes, enabling access to quantum gravitational corrections beyond the semi-classical limit.

### [131] [Antikick Relation in High-Energy Head-On Collisions of Spinning Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13018)
*Carlos O. Lousto,James Healy,Alessandro Ciarfella,Hiroyuki Nakano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过全数值模拟和理论分析，研究了等质量自旋黑洞在相对论速度下对头碰撞（head-on collision）产生的反冲（recoil）结构，发现了峰值反冲与最终反冲之间的近似线性比例关系（V_p ≈ 7.4 V_f），并给出了反冲幅度对初始动量和自旋大小的依赖特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞以相对论速度碰撞是引力的最极端动力学过程。此前研究已确定了掠射碰撞（grazing collision）的最大引力反冲（~0.1c）和最大辐射能量等关键量，但对头碰撞高能碰撞中反冲的详细结构，特别是自旋对反冲的影响，尚缺乏深入理解。

Method: 采用全数值模拟（full numerical simulation）对自旋大小 s=0.5、0.65、0.8 的黑洞在不同初始动量 γv 下进行序列计算；同时结合零频率极限（zero-frequency-limit, ZFL）分析辐射能量和动量、准正则模（quasinormal-mode）模型描述反冲（antikick），以及叠加助推双克尔（superposed boosted double-Kerr）近闭极限（close-limit）估计。

Result: 在相对论区域（γv > 1），峰值反冲 V_p 与最终反冲 V_f 成正比（V_p ≈ 7.4 V_f，等价于 ΔV ≈ -6.4 V_f），且该比例关系几乎与初始动量和自旋大小无关，表明存在共同的并合后弛豫过程。ZFL 预测反冲幅度主要呈线性自旋依赖，而近闭极限预测主要呈 s³ 依赖；基于三个自旋值的经验指数为 s^{1.27±0.08}。

Conclusion: 对头高能碰撞的反冲行为具有普适的比例关系，提示存在统一的弛豫机制；不同理论预测与数值结果之间的偏差表明，需要更高能量的碰撞自旋序列研究来进一步确定反冲幅度的自旋依赖指数。

Abstract: The collision of black holes at relativistic speeds probes gravity in its most extreme dynamical regime. While the maximum gravitational recoil from \emph{grazing} high-energy collisions ($\approx28\,562$~km/s, i.e., $\sim0.1c$) and the maximum radiated energy $E_{\rm rad}$ and remnant spin $α_f^{\max}$ from such encounters ($E_{\rm rad}/M_{\rm ADM}\approx32\%$ where $M_{\rm ADM}$ is the ADM mass, and $α_f^{\max}\approx0.987$) have been established previously~\cite{Healy:2022jbh,Healy:2024lhl}, here we focus on the \emph{head-on} high-energy collision of equal-mass spinning black holes and on the detailed structure of the resulting recoil. Performing a sequence of full numerical simulations for spin magnitudes $s=0.5,0.65$, and $0.8$ over a range of initial momenta $γv$, we characterize the peak recoil $V_p$, the final recoil $V_f$, and the antikick $ΔV\equiv V_f-V_p$, and we provide phenomenological fits of their dependence on $γv$ and $s$. We complement these results with a zero-frequency-limit (ZFL) analysis of the radiated energy and momentum, a quasinormal-mode model of the antikick, and a superposed boosted double-Kerr close-limit estimate. We find that in the relativistic regime ($γv>1$) the peak and final recoil are directly proportional, $V_p\approx7.4\,V_f$ (equivalently $ΔV \approx-6.4\,V_f$), largely independent of both the initial momentum and the spin magnitude, pointing to a common post-merger relaxation. While the ZFL predicts a leading linear-in-spin dependence, the close-limit analysis predicts a leading $s^3$ dependence of the recoil amplitude; with the three spin magnitudes studied here the empirical exponent is $s^{1.27\pm0.08}$, motivating an even higher energy collision spin sequence study.

</details>

### [132] [Bound states for the magnetic Neumann Laplacian in planar sectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12600)
*Ayman Kachmar,Mikael Sundqvist*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究了无限平面扇形区域中带恒定磁场的磁 Neumann Laplacian，证明了对于任意凸扇形（开角 α∈(0,π)），谱的底部严格低于半平面阈值，从而 H_α 在每个 0<α<π 下都存在离散基态特征值，解决了凸扇形的束缚态问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该问题源于磁定位（magnetic localization）在角点附近的分析以及第二类超导体中第三临界场（third critical field）的建模，此前关于凸扇形中是否始终存在束缚态尚未得到严格证明。

Method: 基于 Bonnaillie-Noël 及其合作者以及 Exner、Lotoreichik 和 Pérez-Obiol 的先前工作，通过分析磁 Neumann Laplacian 的谱下界与半平面阈值的严格不等式关系来完成证明。

Result: 对于每个凸扇形（开角 0<α<π），谱底部严格低于半平面阈值，因此算子 H_α 存在离散基态特征值（ground-state eigenvalue）。

Conclusion: 该结果完整解决了凸扇形中的束缚态问题（bound-state problem），为磁定位和超导临界场理论提供了严格的数学依据。

Abstract: We study the magnetic Neumann Laplacian in an infinite planar sector of opening $α\in(0,π)$ under a constant magnetic field. Building on earlier work by Bonnaillie-Noël and collaborators and by Exner, Lotoreichik, and Pérez-Obiol, we prove that the bottom of the spectrum lies strictly below the half-plane threshold for every convex sector. Consequently, $H_α$ has a discrete ground-state eigenvalue for every $0<α<π$. This resolves the bound-state problem for convex sectors, a model problem arising in the analysis of magnetic localization near corners and of the third critical field in type-II superconductivity.

### [133] [Coordination-Resolved Surrogate Models for Thermodynamic Stability, Band Gaps, and Magnetic Moments of Spinel Oxides, Sulfides, and Selenides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11996)
*Keltoum Khallouq,Ayoub El Maazouzi,Rachid Masrour*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于320种尖晶石（spinel）材料数据，训练了基于树集成（tree-ensemble）的代理模型预测五项性质，采用分组感知（group-aware）评估流程，并与未调优的MEGNet进行比较，同时通过SHAP分析、共形区间（conformal intervals）等方法界定了模型的适用域（domain of applicability）。报告了带隙回归的负结果，并将其归因于样本稀缺和半局域DFT标签（semi-local DFT labels）的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为尖晶石（spinel）材料体系的五项关键性质（形成能、凸包距离、带隙、总磁化强度、金属性）构建高精度且可解释的机器学习代理模型，并系统评估其适用域，同时以分组交叉验证（grouped cross-validation）的方式处理材料数据中固有的组内相关性。

Method: 从Materials Project中筛选出320种立方尖晶石（cubic spinel, $Fd\bar{3}m$）数据（包括氮化物、氧化物、硫化物和硒化物）；利用CrystalNN配位数（coordination number）将阳离子分配至四面体（tetrahedral-like）和八面体（octahedral-like）组，而非依据元素身份（element identity）；采用分组感知（group-aware）的树集成（tree-ensemble）代理模型，在简化式（reduced formula）层面进行分组分裂、仅在训练折（training folds）上拟合变换，并通过交叉验证分数选择冠军模型（champion models）。与未调优的MEGNet进行对比，并使用SHAP、共形区间（conformal intervals）、排列零模型（permutation nulls）和留一化学类型（leave-one-chemistry-out）测试进行可解释性和适用域分析。

Result: 冠军模型在20次重复分组留出测试（grouped holdouts）中：形成能MAE为0.121±0.030 eV/atom，凸包距离MAE为0.048±0.013 eV/atom，磁化强度MAE为1.27±0.19 μB/fu，金属性准确率为0.85±0.06。带隙回归在19个非金属留出样本上未优于平凡基线（trivial baseline）。在相同分组分裂下，表格冠军模型（tabular champion）的形成能MAE（0.087 eV/atom）优于未调优的MEGNet（0.209 eV/atom）。

Conclusion: 树集成（tree-ensemble）方法在尖晶石（spinel）性质预测上具有竞争力，但带隙回归受限于样本规模和半局域DFT标签（semi-local DFT labels）质量。SHAP归因将磁化强度模型与八面体d轨道占据数（octahedral d-occupancy）关联，形成能和带隙模型与电负性描述符（electronegativity descriptors）关联。适用域（domain of applicability）在不同阴离子和阳离子间分布不均匀。该对比为描述符方法（descriptor approach）与图神经网络（graph neural network）方法在有限数据规模下的性能关系提供了边界而非定论。

Abstract: We curated 320 cubic ($Fd\bar{3}m$) spinel entries from the Materials Project-nitrides, oxides, sulfides, and selenides, including single-cation mixed-valence $A_3X_4$ compounds-and trained tree-ensemble surrogates for the formation energy, energy above the convex hull, band gap, total magnetization, and metallicity. Cations were assigned to tetrahedral-like and octahedral-like groups from CrystalNN coordination numbers rather than from element identity, and the evaluation was group-aware throughout: splits were grouped by reduced formula, every transform was fit on training folds only, and champion models were selected on cross-validated scores before the holdout was examined. Over twenty repeated grouped holdouts (single-seed refits that reuse the tuned hyperparameters, and are therefore mildly optimistic) the champions reach mean absolute errors of $0.121\pm0.030$ eV/atom for the formation energy, $0.048\pm0.013$ eV/atom for the hull distance, and $1.27\pm0.19$~\muBfu{} for the magnetization, with a metallicity accuracy of $0.85\pm0.06$. Band-gap regression does not beat a trivial baseline on the 19-member non-metal holdout under paired bootstrap testing, we report this negative result and trace it to sample scarcity and to the semi-local DFT labels. On the identical grouped split, the tabular champion is more accurate than an untuned MEGNet trained from scratch (0.087 versus 0.209 eV/atom formation-energy MAE on the primary holdout), a comparison that bounds, rather than settles, the descriptor-versus-graph question at this data scale. SHAP attribution ties the magnetization model to octahedral $d$-occupancy and the formation-energy and band-gap models to electronegativity descriptors, and grouped conformal intervals, permutation nulls, and leave-one-chemistry-out tests bound a domain of applicability that is uneven across anions and cations.

</details>


### [134] [Hyperfine Structure and Exchange Coupling of Vacancy-Induced Ce$^{3+}$ Spin Centers in Nuclear-Spin-Dilute CeO$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12080)
*T. M. Chithresh,Rudra Banerjee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算（PBE+U、超精细张量及KKR交换计算）系统研究了氧空位二氧化铈（CeO₂）中由本征缺陷化学产生的Ce³⁺小极化子自旋中心的磁性环境，揭示了其独特的核自旋稀释特性——所有天然铈同位素核自旋I=0，唯一的磁性核¹⁷O丰度仅0.038%，并给出了¹⁷O超精细耦合张量与弱氧介导交换作用，为评估该类稀土自旋中心的相干性质提供了第一性原理参数基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过本征缺陷化学（native defect chemistry）而非注入或掺杂方式在二氧化铈中产生稀土自旋中心（rare-earth spin centers）的可行性，并系统表征此类自旋中心的磁性环境与相干性质相关的微观参数。

Method: 采用第一性原理PBE+U计算（线性响应Hubbard参数U=5.8382 eV），结合投影缀加波方法（projector-augmented-wave method）的全电子重构获得超精细张量（hyperfine tensors），并在相干势近似（coherent-potential approximation）下进行Korringa-Kohn-Rostoker交换计算。考虑了四种氧空位构型，浓度范围为3.125%至12.5%。

Result: ¹⁷O超精细景观由少数强耦合、近轴向的第一壳层核（接触耦合达6 MHz）和大量弱耦合、强各向异性的外壳层核组成。相邻极化子间的交换相互作用（exchange interactions）为弱氧介导型，在研究的浓度范围内自旋中心基本独立。所有天然铈同位素核自旋I=0，¹⁷O自然丰度仅0.038%。

Conclusion: 氧缺陷二氧化铈是一种通过本征化学过程产生的、内在核自旋稀释的稀土自旋中心宿主材料，文中提供的第一性原理磁性参数可用于后续评估其自旋相干性质（coherence properties），并为¹⁷O ESEEM和HYSCORE等实验测量提供了可访问的谱学特征。

Abstract: Oxygen vacancies in ceria CeO$_2$ donate electrons that localize as Ce$^{3+}$ ($4f^1$, $S=1/2$) small polarons, creating rare-earth spin centers through native defect chemistry rather than implantation or extrinsic doping. We investigate the magnetic environment of these centers using first-principles PBE$+U$ calculations with a linear-response Hubbard parameter ($U=5.8382$ eV), hyperfine tensors from the all-electron reconstruction of the projector-augmented-wave method, and Korringa-Kohn-Rostoker exchange calculations within the coherent-potential approximation. Four vacancy configurations spanning concentrations from $3.125\%$ to $12.5\%$ are considered. A distinctive feature of the host follows from cerium isotopics: all naturally occurring cerium isotopes possess nuclear spin $I=0$, eliminating on-site hyperfine interactions at the Ce$^{3+}$ center and leaving the nuclear-spin bath entirely on the oxygen sublattice, whose sole magnetic isotope, $^{17}O$ ($I=5/2$), occurs at $0.038\%$ natural abundance. The resulting $^{17}O$ hyperfine landscape consists of a small number of strongly coupled, nearly axial first-shell nuclei with contact couplings reaching $6$~MHz, surrounded by a weakly coupled and strongly anisotropic outer shell. These tensors define experimentally accessible signatures for $^{17}O$ ESEEM and HYSCORE measurements and provide the microscopic hyperfine parameters required for cluster-correlation-expansion calculations of spin coherence. Exchange interactions between neighboring polarons are weak and oxygen-mediated, leaving the vacancy-generated spins largely independent over the concentration range considered. Together, these results establish oxygen-deficient CeO$_2$ as a chemically generated and intrinsically nuclear-spin-dilute host for rare-earth spin centers, and provide the first-principles magnetic parameters needed to assess their coherence properties.

### [136] [Emergent toroidal induction in a polar Weyl ferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12322)
*Yuuri Suzuki,Yukako Fujishiro,Masataka Mogi,Juba Bouaziz,Takahiro Anan,Akiko Kikkawa,Daiki Yamaguchi,Max T. Birch,Yuto Kiyonaga,Minoru Kawamura,Yasujiro Taguchi,Takahiro Morimoto,Naoto Nagaosa,Ryotaro Arita,Yoshinori Tokura*

TL;DR: 本文在非中心对称导体PrAlGe中实验发现了一种新的自旋-电荷转换机制——涌现环形感应（emergent toroidal induction）。空间均匀的铁磁体可通过过去未被认识的贝里相位（Berry phase）机制产生涌现电磁感应（EEMI）：交流电流驱动自旋轨道力矩（spin-orbit torques）引发集体磁化动力学，其产生的涌现环形矩（toroidal moment）作为规范势（gauge potential）随时间变化诱导出霍尔电压（Hall voltage），从而在均匀磁体中实现自旋-电荷相互转换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）是现代自旋电子学（spintronics）的核心，其互逆效应——磁化动力学通过自旋依赖的贝里相位产生电动势，即涌现电磁感应（emergent electromagnetic induction, EEMI）——此前仅被观察到存在于具有空间梯度的磁织构（magnetic textures）中（如畴壁、螺旋磁结构和斯格明子）。本研究旨在探索空间均匀的铁磁体是否也能通过新的贝里相位机制产生EEMI，从而扩展自旋-电荷转换的物理基础与应用可能性。

Method: 以极性Weyl铁磁体PrAlGe为研究对象，施加交流电流（alternating current）以产生自旋轨道力矩（spin-orbit torques），驱动集体磁化动力学（collective magnetization dynamics）。通过测量交流霍尔响应（AC Hall response）中异相分量（out-of-phase component）的频率依赖行为，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）进行理论分析。

Result: 实验发现，交流电流驱动的自旋轨道力矩使均匀磁体产生磁化动力学，进而产生涌现环形矩（emergent toroidal moment）T = P × M（其中P为晶体的极性轴，M为净磁化强度）。该环形矩作为规范势（gauge potential），其时间导数dT/dt诱导出霍尔电压。该贡献出现在交流霍尔响应的异相分量中，且与频率呈线性关系，为EEMI提供了直接证据。第一性原理计算揭示，该环形矢量编码了动量空间中Weyl节点（Weyl nodes）的集体运动。

Conclusion: 这些发现确立了"涌现环形感应"（emergent toroidal induction）作为自旋-轨道纠缠（spin-orbit entanglement）的一种新表现形式，统一了贝里相位、拓扑（topology）和自旋动力学（spin dynamics），为内在且高能效的自旋-电荷相互转换（spin-charge interconversion）开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Spin-orbit coupling (SOC) underpins modern spintronics by enabling the electrical generation of spin torques. Its reciprocal counterpart, in which magnetization dynamics produce electromotive forces through a spin-dependent Berry phase, is known as emergent electromagnetic induction (EEMI). However, this effect has previously been observed only in magnetic textures with spatial gradients, such as domain walls, helices, and skyrmions. Here, we demonstrate that even a spatially uniform ferromagnet can host EEMI through a previously unrecognized Berry-phase mechanism inherent to noncentrosymmetric conductors. In the polar Weyl ferromagnet PrAlGe, an applied alternating current generates spin-orbit torques that drive collective magnetization dynamics. The resulting emergent toroidal moment (T = P \times M), where (P) is the crystal's polar axis and (M) is the net magnetization, acts as a gauge potential whose time derivative (dT/dt) induces a Hall voltage. This contribution appears specifically in the out-of-phase component of the AC Hall response and scales linearly with frequency, providing direct evidence for EEMI. First-principles calculations further reveal that this toroidal vector encodes the collective motion of Weyl nodes in momentum space. These findings establish "emergent toroidal induction" as a new manifestation of spin-orbit entanglement, unifying Berry phase, topology, and spin dynamics while opening a pathway toward intrinsic and energy-efficient spin-charge interconversion.

Abstract: The quantum Hall effect in gapped systems represents a defining signature of nontrivial topology. Realizing this principle in gapless matter has remained a central challenge in quantum materials. Chiral topological semimetals provide a unique platform to achieve this aim via symmetry-protected multifold crossings that act as Berry-curvature monopoles. When optical transitions are confined to a single multifold node, the resulting circular photogalvanic effect is predicted to be quantized in terms of the topological charge of the node. In real materials, however, this phenomenon remains experimentally elusive, obscured by trivial band transitions, the energy separation between the node pairs, and their relative positions with respect to the Fermi level. Here we observe a quantized circular photogalvanic effect in the chiral topological semimetal Rh0.95Ni0.05Si. Ni substitution opens a photon-energy window dominated by interband optical transitions at the Γ-point multifold node. This allows circularly polarized near- to mid-infrared pulses to drive a helicity-odd terahertz response that manifests three hallmarks of quantization: a sharp onset, a wavelength-independent plateau governed by the magnitude of monopole charge, and an abrupt cutoff imposed by Pauli blocking. Our work establishes an all-optical analogue for the quantum Hall effect and a new paradigm for topological quantization in gapless matter.

### [139] [Many-body interactions in the dielectric theory of stopping power of solids for classical and quantum projectiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12498)
*Vladimir U. Nazarov,Vyacheslav M. Silkin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文在电介质理论框架下，通过引入波矢与频率依赖的交换关联核（exchange-correlation kernel）$f_{xc}(\qv,ω)$，研究晶体中运动电荷的阻止本领（stopping power）。结果表明：交换关联效应在晶体中的影响比在凝胶模型（jellium model）中更显著；在低于阻止最大值的速度区间，引入交换关联改进了理论与实验的符合；而在高速度区间，动态交换关联效应可忽略。理论输入为基于随机相位近似（random phase approximation, RPA）的微观介电矩阵（dielectric matrix）$ε_{\Gv \Gv'}(\qv,ω)$，该矩阵可通过现有固体能带计算程序获取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用电介质理论（dielectric theory）框架，将波矢与频率依赖的交换关联核 $f_{xc}(\qv,ω)$ 引入晶体的阻止本领描述中。理论输入为基于随机相位近似（RPA，忽略$f_{xc}$）计算的微观介电矩阵 $ε_{\Gv \Gv'}(\qv,ω)$，该矩阵可利用现有固体能带计算程序实现。研究涵盖经典与量子两种抛射体（projectile）情形。

Result: （I）交换关联效应在晶体中的角色比在凝胶模型中更显著；（II）在低于阻止最大值的速度区间，引入交换关联改善了理论与实验的对比；在高速区间，动态交换关联效应可忽略，该结论与实验不矛盾，并在凝胶模型下通过解析分析得到确认。

Conclusion: 晶体中运动电荷的阻止本领受交换关联效应的影响程度取决于速度区间：中低速时需纳入$f_{xc}$以改进理论与实验的一致性，高速时则可忽略该效应。该结论适用于经典与量子抛射体，且理论框架可利用现有固体能带代码中的RPA介电矩阵作为输入。

Abstract: We take account of the many-body dynamic interactions by including the wave-vector and frequency-dependent exchange and correlations (xc) kernel $f_{xc}(\qv,ω)$ in the framework of the dielectric theory of the stopping power of crystals for moving charges. The cases of classical and quantum projectiles are considered. We find that (I) the role of the xc effects in slowing of charges in crystalline solids is more pronounced than it is within the jellium model and (II) For velocities below the stopping maximum, inclusion of xc leads to the improvement of the comparison of the theory with experiment over a range of solid targets. On the other hand, in the high-velocity regime, the role of the dynamic xc proves negligible, which does not contradict experiment, and which we substantiate analytically within the jellium model of the target. The input to our theory is the microscopic dielectric matrix $ε_{\Gv \Gv'}(\qv,ω)$ within the random phase approximation (i.e., with neglect of $f_{xc}$), the calculation of which matrix is implemented in the existing solid-state codes.

### [140] [Compatibility of Martensitic Microstructures in Polycrystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12572)
*John M. Ball,Myrto Galanopoulou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究多晶中马氏体微结构在晶界上的相容性问题，分析了立方到四方和立方到正交相变中零能微结构（如简单层状组织）在晶界两侧的可实现条件，并证明其仅能在测度为零的闭合参数集中发生；同时定义并研究了泰勒集（Taylor set），给出了其新上界，推广了Bhattacharya和Kohn在线性化几何理论中的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将问题简化为平面晶界情形，分别考虑晶界两侧为零能常数梯度和零能简单层状组织（simple laminates）的情况；利用计算机辅助符号计算（computer-assisted symbolic calculation）分析相容性条件；定义泰勒集并推导其上界。

Result: 立方到四方相变中，晶界两侧为简单层状组织时，相容性仅能在晶界法向量和相对晶粒旋转（relative grain rotations）构成的流形中一个测度为零的闭合集上实现；立方到正交相变得到稍弱的类似结果。泰勒集的新上界推广了Bhattacharya和Kohn的结果，并蕴含了Peigney关于三个四方势阱（tetragonal wells）拟凸包（quasiconvex hull）中正对角矩阵的刻画。

Conclusion: 相容性条件的严格限制解释了为何高阶层状组织经常出现；泰勒集的界提供了多晶零能微结构存在的几何约束，为理解多晶相变微结构提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The paper studies martensitic microstructures in polycrystals, focussing on their compatibility across grain boundaries. After a reduction to the case of a planar grain boundary, the case when the grain boundary separates two constant gradients of zero energy is considered. It is shown that for cubic-to tetragonal transformations such a configuration can occur when the relative grain rotation is not in the cubic group. Then the case when the grain boundary separates two simple laminates of zero energy is considered, it being shown using a computer-assisted symbolic calculation that in the cubic-to-tetragonal case compatibility is only possible for a closed set of measure zero in the manifold of grain boundary normals and relative grain rotations, and that a similar slightly weaker result holds for cubic-to-orthorhombic transformations. The results suggest why higher-order laminates are often observed for such transformations.
  The Taylor set of deformation gradients is defined and studied, this set having the property that any deformation whose gradient belongs to it corresponds to a zero-energy microstructure for the polycrystal independent of grain geometry and grain rotations. New upper bounds for the Taylor set are proved for cubic-to-tetragonal and cubic-to-orthorhombic transformations, generalizing those of Bhattacharya and Kohn using the geometrically linearized theory. The bounds imply in particular a result of Peigney characterizing the positive diagonal matrices in the quasiconvex hull of three tetragonal wells, and we give a simple independent proof of this result.

*Inés García-Manuz,Gabriel Caballero,Jose Luis F. Cunado,Miguel Romera,Mariela Menghini,Carlos León,Jacobo Santamaría,Julio Camarero,Paolo Perna,Fernando Ajejas*

TL;DR: 超薄La0.67Sr0.33MnO3（LSMO）薄膜在3至17纳米厚度范围内表现出厚度无关的交换偏置（exchange bias, EB），其根源在于氧缺失导致的内部铁磁-反铁磁界面，而非人为设计的异质界面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超薄LSMO薄膜通常被视为单相铁磁体，但其维度降低会增强氧化学计量和局域结构畸变的影响。该研究旨在探究这类名义上单相的薄膜是否会在无刻意设计的铁磁-反铁磁界面下自发产生交换偏置（exchange bias, EB）效应。

Method: 制备厚度为3至17纳米的LSMO薄膜；采用角度分辨磁光克尔效应（magneto-optical Kerr effect, MOKE）测量磁滞回线偏移；利用X射线光电子能谱（X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy, XPS）表征Mn价态分布；构建简单的界面交换模型（interfacial-exchange model）进行理论分析。

Result: 所有厚度下均观测到可复现且厚度无关的磁滞回线偏移，该偏移在样品旋转180度后符号反转，证实其内禀来源。XPS显示薄膜中存在厚度无关的约20%的Mn2+组分，表明氧缺失的还原区嵌入在Mn3+/Mn4+铁磁基体中。界面交换模型指出仅需亚百分比的反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）或阻挫自旋冰（frustrated spin-ice-like）区域即可产生观测到的EB。

Conclusion: 超薄LSMO能自发地通过氧缺失驱动形成内禀铁磁-反铁磁界面，从而在名义上的单相锰氧化物薄膜中产生交换偏置效应。这一发现揭示了一条实现EB的新兴路径。

Abstract: Ultra-thin La0.67Sr0.33MnO3 (LSMO) films are generally regarded as single-phase ferromagnets, yet their reduced dimensionality enhances the impact of oxygen stoichiometry and local structural distortions. Here we demonstrate that LSMO layers with thicknesses between 3 and 17 nm develop a robust and thickness-independent exchange bias (EB) despite the absence of an engineered ferromagnetic-antiferromagnetic (FM-AFM) interface. Angular magneto-optical Kerr effect measurements reveal a reproducible hysteresis-loop shift that reverses sign upon 180-degree rotation, confirming its intrinsic origin. X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy shows a thickness-independent Mn2+ fraction (about 20 percent), indicating the presence of oxygen-deficient reduced regions embedded within the Mn3+/Mn4+ ferromagnetic matrix. A simple interfacial-exchange model suggests that only a sub-percent fraction of antiferromagnetic (or frustrated spin-ice-like) regions is required to generate the observed EB. These results demonstrate that ultra-thin LSMO can spontaneously host internal FM-AFM interfaces driven by oxygen deficiency, revealing an emergent route to exchange bias in nominally single-phase manganite films.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 镍基尖晶石氧化物因其优异的磁输运性质在自旋电子学（spintronics）应用中具有潜力，亟需深入理解其磁电耦合机制。

Method: 通过在外磁场下冷却单相纳米晶NiCo₂O₄，测量磁滞回线（hysteresis loop）的水平和垂直偏移来表征交换偏置效应，并测量纵向电阻率的温度依赖性和低场/高场下的磁电阻（magnetoresistance）行为；使用高分辨率透射电子显微镜（HRTEM）确认微观结构。

Result: 在5 K下观测到约375 Oe的交换偏置场，该效应在约300 K消失；NiCo₂O₄呈现半导体型纵向电阻率行为，在10 K下具有约31.5%的显著负磁电阻，低磁场下呈蝴蝶形（butterfly-shaped）行为，高磁场下趋于线性。

Conclusion: 负磁电阻和交换偏置均归因于样品中反相边界的形成，HRTEM图像证实了这一微观起源。

Abstract: Nickel-based spinel oxide has recently attracted significant attention due to its remarkable magneto-transport properties, promising various spintronic applications. In this study, we observe an exchange bias effect, where the magnetic hysteresis loop shifts both horizontally and vertically when single-phase nanocrystalline NiCo2O4 is cooled in the presence of an external magnetic field. The magnitude of the exchange bias field is approximately 375 Oe at 5 K, and this effect disappears around 300 K. Furthermore, NiCo2O4 shows semiconducting behaviour in longitudinal resistivity and demonstrates a substantial negative magnetoresistance of ~31.5% at 10 K. The magnetoresistance exhibits a butterfly-shaped behaviour at low magnetic fields and becomes almost linear at high magnetic fields. A detailed analysis of the negative magnetoresistance and exchange bias reveals that both phenomena originate from the formation of antiphase boundaries in the as-synthesized NiCo2O4 sample, as confirmed by the high-resolution transmission electron micrograph.

Abstract: In this work, we report the discovery of a new crystal structure on the Ge-rich side of the Pr-Ge binary phase diagram. Hall resistivity data indicate that electron-like carriers dominate, with a carrier concentration on the order of $10^{27}~\mathrm{m}^{-3}$. The magnetic order is readily suppressed by a magnetic field of approximately 0.4 T applied along the easy $b$ axis.

Abstract: Coherent lattice dynamics can be observed in pump-probe time-resolved and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (TR-ARPES) as a periodic modulation of intensity and energy of photoelectrons over probe time. We present an ab initio time-dependent GW approach including electron-phonon (e-ph) couplings to simulate the photogeneration of coherent phonons and their effects on the TR-ARPES of monolayer MoS2. We demonstrate that state-resolved e-ph coupling strength can be obtained from analyzing coherent phonon modulations on TR-ARPES. Features of both the impulsive stimulated Raman scattering mechanism and the displacive excitation mechanism of coherent phonon generation are identified in our simulations. This method provides supports to analyze coherent phonon dynamics and e-ph couplings in TR-ARPES and enables quantitative engineering of band structure through coherent phonons.

### [145] [Strain-Tunable Shift Current and Magneto-Optical Kerr Effect in Multiferroic Altermagnet Fe2Mo3O8](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12799)

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，系统研究了极性多铁材料Fe2Mo3O8中铁电极化、交错磁序（altermagnetic order）与自旋相关响应之间的耦合机制，发现极化翻转可反转移位电流符号并重塑动量空间自旋劈裂织构，且应变可显著调控光电响应并激活本征态中禁阻的磁光克尔效应。

Result: 铁电极化翻转不仅反转了移位电流的符号，还全面重塑了动量空间的自旋劈裂织构（spin-splitting texture）。移位电流与磁光谱在机械应变下表现出强可调性。值得注意的是，施加a轴单轴应变（a-axis uniaxial strain）打破了晶体对称性，从而激活了本征相中禁阻的有限磁光克尔效应（magneto-optical Kerr effect）。

Conclusion: Fe2Mo3O8中铁电-交错磁耦合可通过极化翻转和应变工程实现多通道电光与磁光响应的协同调控，为发展基于交错磁（altermagnet）的多场耦合自旋电子器件提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Altermagnetism has recently emerged as a compelling frontier in spintronics, seamlessly merging the agile tunability of ferromagnets with the hallmark merits of antiferromagnets. As a prototypical polar multiferroic featuring distinctive altermagnetism, Fe2Mo3O8 hosts an ideal playground for exploring the intricate interplay among ferroelectric polarization, altermagnetic order, and spin-dependent responses. Here, employing first-principles calculations, we systematically investigate the coupling among polarization, spin splitting, shift current, and magneto-optical responses in Fe2Mo3O8. Our findings reveal that switching the ferroelectric polarization not only inverts the sign of the shift current but also comprehensively reshapes the momentum-space spin-splitting texture. Furthermore, the shift current and magneto-optical spectrum exhibits strong tunability under mechanical strain. Remarkably, the application of a-axis uniaxial strain breaks the crystalline symmetry, thereby activating a finite magneto-optical Kerr effect that is otherwise forbidden in the pristine phase.

### [146] [Single-orbital tight-binding model for chiral one-dimensional hybrid organic-inorganic lead halide perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12806)
*Yuya Ominato,Tetsuya Furukawa,Ayumi Ishii,Tetsuaki Itou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文为手性一维有机-无机杂化铅卤钙钛矿(R/S-PEA)PbI₃构建了一个单轨道紧束缚模型，该模型基于四个对称等效位点，包含层、面内子晶格和自旋自由度，能够复现DFT能带结构并定量捕捉能带边自旋分裂与极化模式。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性铅卤钙钛矿（chiral lead halide perovskites）的低能电子态结构尚未被充分理解，缺乏一个兼具对称性透明性和定量准确性的紧束缚模型，以支撑对光学、自旋和输运响应的深入分析。

Method: 从原胞中四个对称相关位点上的单个有效轨道出发，构建包含层（layer）、面内子晶格（in-plane sublattice）和自旋（spin）自由度的紧束缚模型；对导带和价带分别采用不同的参数集，并通过对称性适应的自旋相关跃迁项（symmetry-adapted spin-dependent hopping terms）编码能带边的自旋分裂与自旋极化。

Result: 有效哈密顿量成功复现了密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算的总体能带色散关系，并定量捕获了能带边附近的自旋分裂；同时再现了布洛赫态的主要自旋极化模式。进一步利用螺旋本征值（screw eigenvalues）和反幺正算符（antiunitary operators）分析了偶然简并（accidental degeneracies），将其区分为有效哈密顿量限制项内容所致与由非对称性螺旋对称性（nonsymmorphic screw symmetries）和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）强制导致的简并。

Conclusion: 该模型为理解手性铅卤钙钛矿的能带边电子结构提供了一个对称性透明的起点，并为分析此类材料中的光学、自旋及输运响应奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We present a single-orbital tight-binding model for the low-energy electronic states of the chiral one-dimensional hybrid organic-inorganic lead halide perovskite $\mathrm{(}R/S\mathrm{-PEA)PbI}_3$. The model is constructed from a single effective orbital on each of the four symmetry-related sites in the primitive unit cell and incorporates layer, in-plane sublattice, and spin degrees of freedom. Using separate parameter sets for the conduction and valence bands, the effective Hamiltonian reproduces the overall band dispersions obtained from density-functional-theory calculations and quantitatively captures the spin splittings near the band edges. It also captures the leading spin-polarization patterns of the Bloch states, showing that the band-edge spin splitting and spin polarization are encoded in a small number of symmetry-adapted spin-dependent hopping terms. We further analyze the accidental degeneracies of the effective Hamiltonian using screw eigenvalues and antiunitary operators. This analysis separates accidental degeneracies originating from the restricted term content of the effective Hamiltonian from degeneracies enforced by nonsymmorphic screw symmetries and time-reversal symmetry. The present model provides a symmetry-transparent starting point for understanding the band-edge electronic structure of chiral lead halide perovskites and for analyzing optical, spin, and transport responses in this class of materials.

### [147] [Decoupling Strain-Rate Sensitivity and Deformation Length Scale Effects in Neutron-Irradiated Tungsten: A Coupled Nano-Indentation, HR-EBSD and Crystal Plasticity Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12960)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用球形纳米压痕（应变率范围3.2e-5至3.2e-3 s⁻¹）、原子力显微镜（AFM）、高分辨率电子背散射衍射（HR-EBSD）和晶体塑性有限元（CPFE）建模，研究了未辐照和中子辐照单晶钨。建立了包含热激活滑移、几何必要位错（GND）硬化、辐照诱导障碍物硬化和应变依赖软化的应变梯度CPFE框架，使用单一实验条件标定后在所有应变率下验证。

Result: 仿真结果表明，应变率主要控制热激活塑性流动所需应力，而压痕深度主导塑性区演化、堆积和GND累积。辐照提高了障碍物强度并促进变形局域化，但仍基于共同的热激活机制。模型成功预测了多晶立方体的压缩响应，验证了跨加载条件和长度尺度的可迁移性。

Conclusion: 建立的应变梯度CPFE框架能够有效解耦应变率与长度尺度的耦合效应，为辐照硬化材料在瞬态加载下的本构建模提供了稳健基础。

Abstract: Plastic deformation during strain-rate-controlled spherical nanoindentation is governed by the coupled evolution of constitutive strain-rate sensitivity and deformation length scale, making the intrinsic influence of strain rate difficult to isolate experimentally. This coupling is investigated in unirradiated and neutron-irradiated single-crystal tungsten using spherical nanoindentation, atomic force microscopy, high-resolution electron backscatter diffraction (HR-EBSD), and crystal plasticity finite element (CPFE) modeling. Nanoindentation experiments were performed at strain rates from 3.2e-5 to 3.2e-3 per second. AFM and HR-EBSD quantified surface pile-up, residual lattice strain, and geometrically necessary dislocation (GND) distributions. A strain-gradient CPFE framework incorporating thermally activated slip, GND hardening, irradiation-induced obstacle hardening, and strain-dependent softening was calibrated using a single experimental condition and validated across all remaining strain rates without further parameter adjustment. The validated model was then used to independently vary strain rate and indentation depth. Simulations show that strain rate primarily controls the stress required for thermally activated plastic flow, whereas indentation depth governs plastic-zone evolution, pile-up, and GND accumulation. Irradiation increases obstacle strength and promotes deformation localization while remaining consistent with a common thermally activated mechanism. The framework also predicts the compression response of a polycrystalline cube, demonstrating transferability across loading conditions and length scales, providing a robust basis for constitutive modeling of irradiation-hardened materials under transient loading.

### [148] [Surface Phase-Field-Crystal-Helfrich model for out-of-plane deformations in thin crystalline sheets with lattice mismatch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12997)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 薄柔性晶体片因其能够发生面外（out-of-plane）变形而表现出独特的弹性性质，理解这一行为需要同时考虑面内弹性、面外变形及其耦合作用，并纳入晶体结构及其缺陷的影响。

Method: 通过扩展表面相场晶体-赫尔弗里希模型，允许空间变化的平衡晶格间距，从而能够模拟异质结构中的局部晶格本征应变（lattice eigenstrain）以表征晶格失配。

Result: 该扩展模型在单轴压缩和埃舍尔比夹杂问题（Eshelby's inclusion problem）两种情形下，均与经典Föppl-von Kármán方程和Eshelby理论的解析预测结果吻合，验证了模型有效性。

Conclusion: 基于验证后的框架，论文展示了局部压缩应力如何驱动薄晶体片发生面外变形。

Abstract: Thin, flexible crystalline sheets exhibit unique elastic properties due to their ability to undergo out-of-plane deformations. Understanding this behavior requires a description that couples in-plane elasticity, out-of-plane deformation, and their coupling, taking the crystalline structure and its defects into account. We develop a multiscale description for these systems by extending the surface Phase-Field-Crystal-Helfrich model. The extension permits a spatially varying equilibrium lattice spacing, enabling the representation of localized lattice eigenstrain to mimic lattice mismatch in heterostructures. We validate the extended model against analytical predictions from classical Föppl-von Kármán equations for uniaxial compression and from Eshelby's inclusion problem. Using this validated framework, we then show how locally induced compressive stresses drive out-of-plane deformation in the sheets.

</details>

### [149] [Peak-Decomposition-Free Inverse Metrology of Hyperspectral Moiré Photoluminescence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12325)
*Katsunori Wakabayashi*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需峰分解（peak-decomposition-free）的逆推断框架，通过构建物理驱动的描述子（descriptor）统计量，从莫尔过渡金属硫族化合物异质双层（moiré TMD heterobilayer）的超高光谱光致发光（hyperspectral photoluminescence, PL）数据中定量推断有效无序坐标（effective disorder coordinates），并明确量化了参数的可辨识性极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔过渡金属硫族化合物异质双层的超高光谱PL数据中编码了空间变化的激子（exciton）景观信息，但多峰光谱分解（multi-peak spectral decomposition）的歧义性严重阻碍了这些信息的提取。现有方法无法有效处理该歧义性，亟需一种不依赖于峰分解的定量光学计量方法。

Method: 从原始数据立方体 \(I(x,y,E)\) 出发，构建六类物理驱动的描述子映射（descriptor maps），包括质心能量（centroid energy）、主导发射能量（dominant emission energy）、光谱宽度（spectral width）、低/高谱权重比（low/high spectral-weight ratio）以及主导-质心偏移（dominant–centroid offset）。利用这些描述子的空间自相关层次（spatial autocorrelation hierarchy）与协方差结构（covariance structure）形成稳健的描述子指纹（descriptor fingerprint），并与基于最小化光滑加陷阱模型（smooth-plus-trap generative model）通过网格贝叶斯逆推断（grid-Bayesian inverse）进行匹配，从而推断有效无序坐标 \(\Theta_{\text{eff}} = \{W_s, \xi_s, W_t, n_t\}\) 并给出显式不确定度。

Result: 使用受控多尺度景观（controlled multi-scale landscapes）生成的合成PL立方体，成功恢复了光滑无序坐标并约束了陷阱区域（trap sector），但存在强度-密度简并性（strength–density degeneracy），该简并被明确报告为内在可辨识性极限（intrinsic identifiability limit）。将四种典型无序区间映射到无序坐标图（disorder-coordinate diagram）。描述子统计量对散粒噪声（shot noise）和像素间距（pixel pitch）稳健，且在光学分辨率和能量窗口变化下行为可预测。同一流程可直接应用于实验立方体。

Conclusion: 基于描述子的超高光谱PL方法为光学无序诊断（optical disorder diagnostics）提供了一条实用、最小假设的路径，并构建了一个可复用的分析工作流核心（命名为HyperPL-Diag），适用于二维材料和莫尔激子系统。

Abstract: Hyperspectral photoluminescence (PL) of moiré transition-metal dichalcogenide heterobilayers encodes spatially varying exciton landscapes, but extracting that information is hampered by the ambiguity of multi-peak spectral decomposition. Here we develop a peak-decomposition-free inverse framework for quantitative optical metrology of effective disorder coordinates. From the raw cube $I(x,y,E)$ we construct physically motivated descriptor maps -- centroid energy, dominant emission energy, spectral width, low/high spectral-weight ratio, and dominant--centroid offset. Their spatial autocorrelation hierarchy and covariance structure form a robust descriptor fingerprint of multi-scale disorder-sensitive spectral statistics. By matching these descriptor summary statistics to a minimal smooth-plus-trap generative model through a grid-Bayesian inverse, we infer effective disorder coordinates $\Thetaeff=\{\Ws,\xis,\Wt,\nt\}$ with explicit uncertainties. Using synthetic PL cubes generated from controlled multi-scale landscapes, we recover the well-identified smooth-disorder coordinates and constrain the trap sector up to a strength--density degeneracy. We report this degeneracy explicitly as an intrinsic identifiability limit rather than a deficiency of the method, and map four canonical disorder regimes onto a disorder-coordinate diagram. The descriptor statistics are stable against shot noise and pixel pitch, and behave predictably under optical-resolution and energy-window changes. The same pipeline ingests experimental cubes without modification, making it directly applicable to two-dimensional and moiré materials. Our results establish descriptor-based hyperspectral PL as a practical, minimal-assumption route to optical disorder diagnostics and provide the validated core of a reusable analysis workflow (\texttt{HyperPL-Diag}) for moiré exciton systems.

</details>

### [150] [Oscillatory Active Brownian Motion: A Minimal Model for Sperm Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12158)
*Adrian Pacheco-Pozo,Arturo Matamoros Volante,Pilar Ameijeiras,Mariano G. Buffone,Diego Krapf*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出振荡主动布朗运动（OABM）模型，扩展了标准主动布朗运动（ABM），通过引入周期性角驱动来描述微观游泳者（如精子）的固有振荡运动，并定量再现了从单细胞轨迹到群体动力学的实验观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准主动布朗运动（active Brownian motion, ABM）无法显式描述主动微观游泳者（如精子）中由鞭毛或纤毛拍击产生的周期性振荡运动，限制了其对依赖于周期性头部运动的多细胞输运行为的解释能力。

Method: 提出振荡主动布朗运动（oscillatory active Brownian motion, OABM）模型，在ABM框架中让游泳者方向经历定向扩散（directional diffusion）的同时，叠加一个周期性角驱动（periodic angular drive）。该模型可解析推导出时间平均均方位移、速度自相关函数和横向摆动幅度等实验可观测量的表达式。

Result: 模型预测了两种弹道（ballistic） regime 之间的交叉：短时间尺度由游泳速度主导的运动，以及中间时间尺度由角拍幅决定的有效速度降低的振荡平均输运。利用人类精子轨迹，从标准运动学指标推断模型参数，该模型定量再现了对照条件和超活化（hyperactivation）诱导后的单细胞轨迹及群体动力学。

Conclusion: OABM提供了一个紧凑的活性物质（active matter）理论框架，将可测量的鞭毛运动学与粗粒化输运行为联系起来，能够描述不同生理状态下精子的运动特征。

Abstract: Active biological microswimmers typically combine persistent self-propulsion with cyclic motion generated by flagellar or ciliary beating. However, standard active Brownian motion (ABM) does not explicitly account for these intrinsic oscillations. This limitation is particularly relevant for sperm cells, whose transport depends not only on directional persistence and stochastic reorientation but also on periodic head motion. Here we introduce oscillatory active Brownian motion (OABM), a minimal extension of ABM in which the swimmer orientation undergoes directional diffusion while being modulated by a periodic angular drive. The model yields analytical expressions for experimentally relevant observables, including the time-averaged mean-squared displacement, velocity autocorrelation function, and transverse excursion amplitude. A central prediction is a crossover between two ballistic regimes: short-time motion governed by the swimming velocity and an intermediate regime with a reduced, oscillation-averaged effective velocity determined by the angular beat amplitude. Using trajectories of human sperm, we infer model parameters from standard motility measures. The model quantitatively reproduces both single-cell trajectories and population-level dynamics under control conditions and following induction of hyperactivation. Overall, OABM provides a compact active-matter framework that links measurable flagellar kinematics to coarse-grained transport, enabling a description of sperm motility across different physiological states.

### [151] [Solvent Mixing Effect on Free-Energy Barrier and Stability for Molecular Recognition Driven by the Translational Motion of Solvent Molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12307)
*Mika Matsuo,Ryo Akiyama*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究利用三维 Ornstein-Zernike 方程结合改进超网链闭包（3D-MHNC-OZ theory），计算了环状主体与球形客体在溶剂混合物中的平均力势（PMFs）。研究确认了识别位点处的熵稳定化效应，并发现其周围存在自由能垒壁；混合溶剂中的自由能垒远低于单组分溶剂。与球形溶质二聚化不同，混合效应并未显著降低主-客体识别的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用硬体相互作用（hard-body interactions）描述粒子间作用，利用三维 Ornstein-Zernike 方程耦合改进超网链闭包（3D-MHNC-OZ theory）计算平均力势（potentials of mean force, PMFs）。

Result: 识别位点处观察到熵稳定化（entropic stabilization）效应，其周围存在自由能垒壁（free-energy barrier wall）。混合溶剂的自由能垒远低于单组分溶剂；混合效应虽然降低了球形溶质的二聚化稳定性，但并未显著降低主-客体识别的稳定性。

Conclusion: 主-客体缔合（host-guest association）行为与两个球形溶质分子缔合的行为存在本质差异：在混合溶剂中，主-客体识别稳定性受混合效应影响较小，而球形溶质二聚化稳定性则显著降低。

Abstract: We calculated the potentials of mean force (PMFs) between a ring-like host and a spherical guest in a solvent mixture. We adopted hard-body interactions between particles to discuss the effects of solvent-particle translational motion. The PMFs were obtained using the three-dimensional Ornstein-Zernike equation coupled with the modified hypernetted-chain closure (3D-MHNC-OZ theory). The entropic stabilization at the recognition site is confirmed, and a free-energy barrier wall is observed surrounding it. The free-energy barrier for the solvent mixture is much lower than that for the one-component solvent. Similar barrier reduction for the association of two spherical solute molecules has also been reported, and the mixing effect also reduced the dimerization stability. By contrast, the mixing effect does not significantly reduce recognition stability in the present study. In this respect, the behavior of the host-guest association is different from that of the association of two spherical solute molecules.
