### [152] [Tunable Signal Penetration and Response Plateaus in Bistable Mechanical Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12405)
*Sven Pattloch,Joachim Dzubiella*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过理论模型与模拟，证明内部双稳性（bistability）能够主动控制力学超材料的响应与信号衰减，揭示了类似静电“趋肤效应”的通用屏蔽机制以及频率不敏感响应平台，并为可调谐软物质信号处理提供了显式设计规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统粘弹性材料缺乏内在可调谐性（intrinsic tunability），难以满足软体机器人（soft robotics）和机械感知（mechanosensing）领域对动态机械信号处理的需求。因此，需要探索一种能主动控制力学响应与信号衰减的新机制。

Method: 模型中的每个双稳单元（bistable element）在由势能差ε、平衡长度变化Δl和弹簧常数差Δk区分的状态之间，以预设时间尺度进行离散切换。系统通过耦合泊松切换（Poisson switching）的微观布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics）模拟，并在宏观层面由非线性连续场论（nonlinear continuum field theory）描述。

Result: 模型给出了线性响应（linear response）和空间穿透深度（spatial penetration depth）的闭式解析解，揭示了两种现象：驱动频率超过内部弛豫率时，信号空间穿透减弱的通用屏蔽机制（类似静电“趋肤效应”）；以及由时间尺度分离（timescale separation）导致的频率不敏感响应平台。屏蔽长度主要由Δl控制，而衰减区间和平台可通过切换速率ν调谐。系统存在基本设计权衡：增大Δl增强耗散但提高能垒，导致状态锁定（state-locking）并使阻尼消失。

Conclusion: 该框架由于解析可处理性（analytical tractability），为精细调控双稳介质的自适应响应提供了显式设计规则。其适用范围涵盖从生物聚合物到合成捕捉键（catch bonds）和超材料（metamaterials）等多种实验系统，为面向频率选择性信号处理的智能软物质预测性工程设计奠定了基础。

Abstract: Dynamically processing mechanical signals is crucial for soft robotics and mechanosensing, where classical viscoelastic materials lack intrinsic tunability. We show that internal bistability actively controls the response and signal attenuation in mechanical (meta)materials. In our model, bistable elements switch discretely with a predefined timescale between states distinguished by potential energy $ε$, equilibrium length $Δl$, and spring constant $Δk$. The system is simulated via microscopic Brownian dynamics coupled to Poisson switching with rate $ν$, and described macroscopically by a nonlinear continuum field theory. Crucially, the model yields closed-form analytical solutions for the linear response and spatial penetration depth, revealing two phenomena: a universal screening mechanism (akin to the electrostatic 'skin effect') reducing spatial signal penetration when the driving frequency exceeds the internal relaxation rate, and a frequency-insensitive response plateau from timescale separation. The screening length is controlled primarily by the conformational length change $Δl$, while the attenuation regime and plateau are tuneable via the switching rate $ν$. A systematic parameter study exposes a fundamental design trade-off: larger $Δl$ strengthens dissipation but raises the energy barrier for state transitions, eventually causing state-locking where damping vanishes. Optimal attenuation thus requires a compromise between pronounced bistability and a surmountable barrier. Due to its analytical tractability, our framework provides explicit design rules for fine-tuning the adaptive response of bistable media. It applies to diverse experimental systems-from biopolymers to synthetic catch bonds and metamaterials-enabling the predictive engineering of intelligent soft matter for frequency-selective signal processing.

</details>


### [153] [IceCAPA: patterning particles and microorganisms at a freezing front](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12574)
*Isabelle M. Feller,Jakob Paulsen,Muriel Scherer,Robert W. Style,Lucio Isa*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于定向冷冻（directional freezing）的稳健图案化技术，可在不同基底上对合成颗粒和微生物细胞进行高保真图案化，并揭示了温度梯度和冷冻前沿与颗粒相互作用的关键机制，以及与空气-水界面的类比例关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图案化技术缺乏通用性，难以在多种基底上对广泛的合成与生物对象（如胶体颗粒和微生物细胞）进行精确图案化，因此需要开发一种兼具普适性和温和性的可靠方法。

Method: 该方法利用在图案化基底上对颗粒或细菌悬浮液进行定向冷冻：生长的冰将目标对象推入基底陷阱，同时将未被捕获的对象移走，从而留下高保真图案。研究中通过调节温度梯度控制颗粒与冷冻前沿（freezing front）的相互作用。

Result: 该方法适用于多种材料（合成颗粒和微生物细胞），且不受基底润湿性影响。图案化后的细菌细胞保持良好的活性，表明该组装技术具有温和性。此外，研究发现温度梯度是决定颗粒与冷冻前沿相互作用的关键控制参数。

Conclusion: 该定向冷冻图案化技术提供了一种通用且温和的微纳图案化方案，可拓展至多种应用场景。同时，研究揭示了颗粒与冷冻前沿及空气-水界面（air-water interface）之间的紧密类比例系，提示毛细现象（capillarity）的研究成果可能有助于理解冷冻过程。

Abstract: The ability to precisely pattern micro- and nano-scale objects on surfaces is important for a range of different applications. For example, colloidal patterning has been used to create plasmonic surfaces, light-emitting diodes or authentication marks, while microbial cell patterning can be applied to screening antibiotic response and cellular interactions over larger populations at the single-cell level. However, we still lack versatile techniques that can pattern a wide range of synthetic and biological objects on a spectrum of different substrate types. Here, we present a robust patterning technique based on the directional freezing of a particle or bacterial suspension over a patterned substrate. Growing ice pushes the desired objects into traps in the substrate, while sweeping away non-trapped ones, leaving behind high-fidelity patterns. We show that this method works for a range of different materials (both synthetic particles and microbial cells), and is unaffected by substrate wettability. Furthermore, patterned bacterial cells retain excellent post-assembly viability, highlighting the gentle nature of the assembly technique. Beyond patterning applications, our results also give insights into processes involving the freezing of particulate suspensions. In particular, we demonstrate the importance of the temperature gradient as a key control which determines how particles interact with freezing fronts. Finally, we highlight a tight analogy between particles interacting with a freezing front and with air-water interfaces, suggesting that results from capillarity may shed light on freezing phenomena.

</details>


### [154] [How Quasicrystals Remember: Hierarchical Memory Under Cyclic Shear](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12674)
*Edwin A. Bedolla-Montiel,Marjolein Dijkstra*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过非热准静态剪切模拟，展示了二维十二重准晶（quasicrystal）在循环加载下能够编码和恢复力学记忆（mechanical memory），并识别出引起记忆效应的基本微观切换单元——类相位子（phason-like）的瓦片重排，这类重排在周期性近似物中缺失，揭示了结构无序与双稳态滞后元（hysteron）之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准晶（quasicrystal）介于周期性晶体与无序玻璃之间，是研究无序与力学记忆涌现（emergence of mechanical memory）相互作用的理想平台，但其微观记忆机制尚不明确。

Method: 采用非热准静态剪切模拟（athermal quasistatic shear simulations），对二维十二重准晶（two-dimensional dodecagonal quasicrystal）施加循环剪切（cyclic driving），并分析应力-应变响应及可逆塑性事件。

Result: 在屈服（yielding）以下，循环剪切产生嵌套滞后回线（nested hysteresis loops），呈现回环-返回点记忆（loop-return point memory）；微观上，类相位子的瓦片重排（tile-switch rearrangements）是基本切换单元，具有紧凑核心、尖锐双稳态（sharp bistability）和埃舍尔比兼容弹性远场（Eshelby-compatible elastic far field）。周期性近似物（periodic approximant）缺乏这些双稳态瓦片重排。

Conclusion: 准晶中的结构无序（结构无序）与类相位子自由度（phason degrees of freedom）是产生双稳态滞后元（bistable hysteron）和循环剪切记忆的必要条件；准晶为研究无序系统中的记忆效应提供了比非晶固体更易微观分辨的模型体系。

Abstract: Quasicrystals occupy a unique middle ground between periodically ordered crystals and disordered glasses, making them an ideal platform for examining the interplay between disorder and the emergence of mechanical memory. Using athermal quasistatic shear simulations, we show that two-dimensional dodecagonal quasicrystals encode and recover memory under cyclic driving. Above the yielding transition, the response becomes irreversible, characterized by persistent shear bands and locally transformed regions. Below yielding, cyclic shear with varying amplitudes produces a hierarchy of nested hysteresis loops in the stress-strain response characteristic of loop-return point memory. By resolving the underlying reversible plastic events, we reveal localized phason-like tile rearrangements as the elementary switching units and identify tile-switch hysterons responsible for memory in the quasicrystal. Such a microscopic identification of the fundamental switching units is considerably more challenging, and often impossible, in amorphous solids. Despite their structural diversity, these rearrangements share a compact core, sharp bistability, and an Eshelby-compatible elastic far field. In contrast, a periodic approximant of the quasicrystal lacks both the structural disorder and the bistable tile-switch rearrangements required for cyclic-shear memory, linking phason degrees of freedom to bistable hysterons.

</details>


### [155] [Entropy-Driven Initiation and Cellular Uptake Mediated by Viscoelastic Cytoskeleton: A Kinetic Phase Diagram from Onsager Variational Principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12766)
*Jinjie Liu,Zhong-Can Ou-Yang,Hao Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于昂萨格变分原理（Onsager variational principle）构建了一个统一的连续介质模型，提出拥挤细胞环境中纳米尺度生物分子产生的熵力（entropic forces）是受体介导内吞作用（receptor-mediated endocytosis）中配体与受体初始靠近的驱动力，模型预测了关键浓度阈值、可包裹粒子尺寸窗口以及最优病毒半径，并与HIV-1尺寸吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受体介导内吞作用中一个基本问题尚未解答：是什么初始驱动力使配体与受体相互靠近？以往模型假设已存在接触，回避了这一起始问题。本文旨在提出并验证拥挤细胞环境中纳米生物分子的熵力作为关键启动机制。

Method: 基于昂萨格变分原理构建统一的连续介质模型，以包裹深度（engulfment depth）为广义坐标，驱动力来自熵、结合、细胞膜及细胞骨架贡献的自由能景观（free energy landscape）。模型自然纳入：熵驱动粘附作为起始、配体-受体结合作为维持力、基于Helfrich-Canham哈密顿量的膜变形、以及通过弹性-粘弹性对应原理（elastic-viscoelastic correspondence principle）的细胞骨架粘弹性。

Result: 动力学相图（kinetic phase diagram）预测了启动所需的关键生物分子浓度、完全包裹所需配体密度的下界、可包裹粒子的有限尺寸窗口，以及随结合能增加而减小的最优病毒半径30–60 nm。昂萨格溶解条件（Onsager solubility condition）自然给出相边界。模型在大粒子平面极限下与经典Asakura-Oosawa结果渐近一致。更硬的细胞导致更长的包裹时间和更窄的尺寸窗口。在生理学合理参数下，最优尺寸与HIV-1尺寸匹配。

Conclusion: 该工作为细胞摄取（cellular uptake）提供了变分基础，对病毒学（virology）、纳米技术（nanotechnology）和药物递送（drug delivery）具有启示意义。

Abstract: A fundamental question in receptor-mediated endocytosis remains unanswered: what initial driving force brings ligands and receptors into close proximity? While previous models assume pre-existing contact and overlook this initiation problem, we propose that entropic forces from nanoscale biomolecules in crowded cellular environments provide the essential driving mechanism. We develop a unified continuum model rooted in the Onsager variational principle, where engulfment depth serves as the generalized coordinate and the driving force derives from a free energy landscape of entropic, binding, membrane, and cytoskeleton contributions. The framework naturally incorporates: (i) entropy-driven adhesion as initiation; (ii) ligand-receptor binding as the sustaining force; (iii) membrane deformation via the Helfrich-Canham Hamiltonian; and (iv) cytoskeleton viscoelasticity through the elastic-viscoelastic correspondence principle. The kinetic phase diagram predicts a critical biomolecule concentration for initiation, a lower bound of ligand density for complete engulfment, a finite size window for engulfable particles, and an optimal virus radius of 30--60 nm that decreases with increasing binding energy. The Onsager solubility condition naturally yields the phase boundaries. The model exhibits asymptotic consistency with the classic Asakura-Oosawa result in the large-particle flat-surface limit. Stiffer cells lead to longer engulfment times and narrower size windows. Strikingly, the optimal size matches HIV-1 dimensions under physiologically realistic parameters. This work provides a variational foundation for cellular uptake with implications for virology, nanotechnology, and drug delivery.

</details>


### [156] [Active Quantum Nematics: The First Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12961)
*Ghansham Chandel,Siddhartha Das*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文将活性向列相（Active Nematics）和液晶理论形式化为量子力学框架，通过引入复值向列波函数（Nematic Wavefunction）到Beris-Edwards方程，将时空变化的向列系统分解为量子化状态，并得到了活性微泳者的普朗克能量-频率关系、趋化系统中的捕食者-猎物动力学以及心脏搏动的量子化描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 向列对称性（nematic symmetry）蕴含了拓扑缺陷数和涡胞数等守恒的量子化量，活性向列相中已发现大量量子类比现象，因此有必要建立严格的形式化框架来统一描述这些现象。

Method: 通过引入复值向列波函数到Beris-Edwards方程，将活性向列相和液晶理论纳入量子力学框架，从而将时空变化的向列系统分解为量子化状态（quantized states）。

Result: 得到了活性微泳者（如蠕动蠕虫和细菌）的普朗克能量-频率关系（Planck's energy-frequency relationship）；对于依赖扩散趋化性（diffusive chemotaxis）的生物，得到了捕食者-猎物动力学（predator-prey dynamics），该动力学演化以最大化/最小化信息素场梯度重叠；心脏搏动的量子化类比氢原子轨道，状态函数可表征心脏的节律（rhythm）以及不同谐波（harmonics）收缩活动的时空分布。

Conclusion: 该形式化框架表明，活性向列系统与量子力学之间存在深层结构类比，可用于从量子化视角理解活性物质、生物趋化以及心脏生理状态。

Abstract: Nematic symmetry entails conserved quantized quantities such as number of topological defects and vorticity cells. Correspondingly, countless quantum analogies have been found in Active Nematics. We formalize Active Nematics and Liquid Crystal theory into the framework of Quantum Mechanics by introducing a complex valued Nematic Wavefunction to the Beris Edward equations, thus splitting spatiotemporally varying nematic systems into quantized states. We obtain the Planck's energy-frequency relationship for active micro-swimmers such as peristaltic worms and bacterium as a consequence of local complex phase-symmetry of the governing equations, similar to the gauge formulation of Electromagnetism. For organisms operating on diffusive chemotaxis, we obtain predator-prey dynamics that evolve to maximize/minimize pheromones field gradient overlap. Furthermore, when quantizing beating hearts, similar to the orbitals of hydrogen atoms, the state-function allows us to characterize hearts not only through the rhythm, but also the spaciotemporal distribution of contractile activity of various harmonics among healthy and unhealthy hearts.

</details>

### [157] [A cryogenic neutral-atom platform with full optical access and 2-hour trap lifetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12988)
*Akhil Kumar,Lorenzo Festa,Avishay Grinberg,Eran Reches,Dimitrios Tsevas,Kevin P. Mours,Zhao Zhang,Robin Eberhard,Sebastian Blatt,Andrea Alberti,Johannes Zeiher,Immanuel Bloch,Max Melchner*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种新型低温增强的中性原子量子计算装置，能够在保持完全光学可访问性的同时，实现光学镊子阵列中单个$^{88}\mathrm{Sr}$原子长达两小时的真空限制俘获寿命，为扩展到数万个原子的可排序阵列提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中性原子量子处理器（neutral-atom quantum processors）正迅速向超过一万个量子比特（qubit）的系统规模扩展，但现有平台通常需要在光学可访问性（optical accessibility）与原子在光学势阱中的存储时间（storage time）之间做出折衷，从而限制了可用的量子比特数量。

Method: 设计并运行了一种新型低温增强的中性原子装置（cryogenically enhanced neutral-atom apparatus），该装置采用相对简单的低温恒温器（cryostat）设计，无需复杂低温密封结构，即可在光学镊子阵列（optical tweezer array）中捕获单个$^{88}\mathrm{Sr}$原子。

Result: 实验实现了真空限制下长达两小时的单个原子俘获寿命（trapping lifetime），同时保持了完整的光学可访问性。该架构可被直接移植到其他原子种类。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，利用相对简单的低温设计即可实现极长的单原子寿命，为扩展到数万个原子的可排序阵列（sorted arrays）展示了一条可行的规模化路径。

Abstract: Neutral-atom quantum processors are rapidly scaling toward system sizes of more than ten thousand qubits, allowing for the realization of a new class of quantum computing algorithms and quantum simulation experiments. However, current neutral-atom platforms generally have to find a compromise between the optical accessibility and the storage time of atoms in optical potentials, limiting the available qubit numbers. Here we report on the operation of a novel, cryogenically enhanced, neutral-atom apparatus that overcomes these apparently conflicting requirements. We demonstrate vacuum-limited trapping lifetimes of up to two hours of single $^{88}\mathrm{Sr}$ atoms in an optical tweezer array while preserving full optical access and without the need for complex cryogenic enclosures. Our measurements show that exceptionally long single-atom lifetimes can be achieved with a relatively simple cryostat design. Our architecture can be straightforwardly ported to other atomic species and shows a viable path for scaling up to sorted arrays of tens of thousands of atoms.

</details>


### [158] [High-fidelity entanglement of polar molecules by dynamic geometric control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13008)
*Scarlett S. Yu,Avikar Periwal,Jiaqi You,Zirui Liu,Qinshu Lyu,Youngju Cho,Loïc Anderegg,Eunmi Chae,John M. Doyle*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出通过控制偶极相互作用几何结构并利用可编程相干保持分子运动，在超冷分子光镊阵列中抑制热运动退相干，实现了Bell态保真度达0.976的高保真纠缠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超冷分子的光镊阵列量子信息系统中，分子的热运动会降低相互作用相干性，从而限制纠缠保真度及系统的科学应用潜力。

Method: 通过控制偶极相互作用（dipolar interaction）的几何结构，即使分子占据光镊中多个运动态（motional states），也能保持相干性；同时利用可编程的相干保持分子运动，在纠缠过程中对光镊相对位置抖动（relative positional jitter）引起的退相位（dephasing）进行重聚焦（refocusing）。

Result: 多种几何结构可抑制热涨落敏感性；所提方法显著提升了偶极相干性，并在直接激光冷却的分子中实现了双分子纠缠，Bell态保真度达$\mathcal{F}= 0.976^{+0.008}_{-0.011}$。

Conclusion: 通过几何控制和运动重聚焦可有效克服分子热运动对量子相干性的限制，为超冷分子光镊阵列实现高保真纠缠提供了可行路径。

Abstract: In quantum information systems made of optical tweezer arrays of ultracold molecules, thermal motion of molecules degrades the coherence of their interactions, which limits entanglement fidelity and the concomitant scientific applicability of these systems. We show that by controlling the geometry of the dipolar interaction, even when a molecule occupies many motional states in the tweezer, coherence can be preserved. We characterize several geometries that suppress sensitivity to thermal fluctuations. We further use programmable, coherence-preserving motion of the molecules during entanglement to refocus dephasing from relative positional jitter of the tweezers, which is relevant even on the 10 nm scale. These methods yield substantially improved dipolar coherence and enable generation of two-molecule entanglement with a Bell state fidelity of $\mathcal{F}= 0.976^{+0.008}_{-0.011}$ in directly laser-cooled molecules.

</details>
